---
name: Intangamarara ya Bitcoin n'Igiceri
goal: Ivyiyumviro vyimbitse ku Bitcoin, Stablecoins, & Ubusegaba Buzana Navyo
objectives: 

  - Gutahura ukuntu amahera yateye imbere mu mateka be n’ibintu nyamukuru bibabaza biva ku bijanye n’ubutunzi bwacu bwo muri iki gihe.
  - Gutegura ugutahura gutomoye kwa Bitcoin, kuyitandukanya n’amahera ya fiat ya kera.
  - Gusuzuma uruhara rw’ama stablecoins, cane cane Tether, mu gushikama kw’ivy’ubutunzi no nk’ikiraro hagati ya Bitcoin n’amafaranga y’agaciro.
  - Kumenya no gukuraho ivyiyumviro bitari vyo abantu benshi bafise ku bijanye na Bitcoin n’amahera y’amahera.

---

Woba warigeze kwibaza ngo:


Ni kuki ubuzima bwanje bubandanya kuduga?

Mbega vy’ukuri inflation ni nziza kuri jewe?

Ni ubuhe buryo bwo kumfasha kwikingira inflation?

None Bitcoin canke stablecoins zija gute muri ivyo vyose?


Nimba wishuye ngo ego kuri kimwe muri ivyo bibazo, uri mu kibanza ciza.


Ikaze muri "Opting In To Change," aho twihweza munsi y'uburebure bw'amahera yacu mu gihe turaba ibikoresho bimwe bimwe biriho vyo gutuma habaho ihinduka ryiza. Uko isi yacu iriko irahangana n’ibintu bitera ubwoba umwidegemvyo be n’uguhohotera uburenganzira bwa muntu, iyo nyigisho iragerageza gutanga umuco wo kuyobora, ni ukuvuga uburyo bundi busubiza ubutegetsi mu minwe y’umuntu ku giti ciwe.


Nimba ivyo uhejeje gusoma vyaguteye umunezero, twizigiye ko uzokwifatanya natwe muri uru rugendo rw’inyigisho.


Ivyo wokwitega:


Umugenzi w'intango

Nk'amasaha 3 y'ibirimwo vy'ukwigenza

Ibibazo bikorana kugira ngo ugerageze ubumenyi bwawe

Yanditswe n'abahinga mu vy'inganda

Ingero zivuye hirya no hino kw'isi no mu mice yose y'ubuzima


Ibisabwa: Ugukunda cane kwiga


Iyi nyigisho yatewe inkunga na TETHER .

# Imenyekanisha


<partId>d44d9f32-c72e-58a4-9855-12e29f3e763c</partId>


## Incamake y'amashure


<chapterId>2eaf5947-8180-540e-9418-c40bf04e07ce</chapterId>

Murakaze mu nyigisho ya ECO104!


**Tuba mw'isi aho:**


● Abantu 20% gusa baba mu mibano ibonwa ko "ifise umwidegemvyo mu buryo bwa demokarasi." Yamara, no muri ako gace k’agateka, ukurenga kw’uburenganzira bwa muntu kuragenda kurarushiriza kuba ikintu gisanzwe—kuva ku gufunga amakonte ya banki gushika ku gucengera. Abasigaye 80% basanga bariko barahangana n’ugutera kw’ubutegetsi bw’agahomerabunwa. Haciye imyaka mirongo ibiri gusa, hafi ica kabiri c’abantu bo kw’isi bari bafise umwidegemvyo w’ishimikiro kuruta iyindi yose.


● [1.4]" ancial-services#:~:text=Ku isi yose%2C%20bamwe%201.4%20miliyaridi%20 z'abantu bakuze,genda%2C%20vyinshi%20ibindi%20bikenewe.) abantu bakuze amamiliyaridi kw’isi yose baguma batagira amabanki, mu gihe abandi batagira uko bangana bashobora gukoresha ibikorwa bikeyi vyo mu mabanki.


● Mu mpera z’umwaka wa [2022](https://Elements.visualcapitalist.com/mapped-ibihugu-bifise-igipimo-c’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro/), hafi igice c’isi cari gifise igipimo c’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro c’imirongo ibiri, ivyo bikaba vyatuma agaciro k’amahera umuntu aronka mu Hard kagabanuka. Kugira ngo ivyo ubishire mu buryo bubereye, n’igipimo c’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro c’ibice 10 kw’ijana mu myaka cumi, woba watakaje ibice 65 kw’ijana vy’ubushobozi bwawe bwo kugura.


● Kandi naho ata bihe vy’ugutera imbere nk’ukwo, USD, ishobora kuvugwa ko ari yo mafaranga akomeye kuruta ayandi yose kw’isi, yarabonye [96%](https://www.visualcapitalist.com/ubushobozi-bw’ugugura-bw’idolari-ry’Amerika-mu-gihe/) gutakaza ububasha bwo kugura kw’idolari rya nyuma.


Ivyo ni bimwe mu kuri gukomeye kw’ibidukikije vy’ubutunzi bwacu kw’isi yose. Uburyo bwacu bw’ivy’ubutunzi burabura cane mu guha ivyo abantu benshi bakeneye. Izo nzira zituma ubusumbasumbane bugumaho, zigatuma abantu benshi batagira aho bahuriye, kandi zigatuma abantu amamiliyaridi kw’isi yose babura ububasha.


Niwaba uremerewe n’imikazo idahera y’uguduga kw’ibiciro canke ukubura ivy’amahera mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwacu bwo muri iki gihe, nimba ari ihumure, menye ko utari wenyene. Ivyo ni vyo biva mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwacu bw’amahera bwo muri iki gihe.


Naho dusa n’ababona ibintu mu buryo buteye akaga, ico twibandako muri iyo nyigisho si ugushira umutima ku ngorane ziri mu mibereho yacu ubu. Ahubwo dushaka guhindura ivyiyumviro vyacu ku gushika ku kwidegemvya no ku guhabwa ubushobozi bw’amahera.


Ivyo bivuzwe, iri shure si iry’abahanganye n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro canke ubukene bwo kuronka ibikorwa remezo vy’ivy’ubutunzi canke ibikorwa vya banki gusa. Waba usanzwe uzi neza ivyo bibazo canke ushaka gusa kwagura ubumenyi bwawe, iri shure ryagenewe kugirira akamaro umuntu wese arondera kwongerera ugutahura kwiwe no kuronka ibikoresho bikenewe kugira ngo ashobore gutsinda izo nzitizi no gusubira kuronka ubusegaba mu vy’amahera.


Dufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, igikorwa cacu ni ukubazana ku ruhande rw’imbere rw’ihinduka mu bijanye n’ivy’ubutunzi bwacu, guhangana n’amategeko ariho no gutanga ubundi buryo bwo gutorera umuti ibibazo. Mu kwihweza cane amateka y’amahera, gukuraho amabanga ya Bitcoin, no gutohoza Tether n’isi y’amahera adahinduka, dufise intumbero yo gutuma abantu basubira kwiyumvira kazoza kabo k’amahera.


**Ivyo wokwitega:**


**Icigwa ca mbere: Igiciro c'Iterambere - Kwihweza neza Uburyo bwacu bw'Ivy'Imari**

Turatangura ubushakashatsi bwacu mu kwihweza inyuma y’imirongo y’ubutunzi bwacu bwo muri iki gihe, aho ugucengera ivy’ubutunzi, ubusumbane bw’ubutunzi n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro bitera ingorane ubuzima bwacu bwa misi yose. Biciye mu mateka make y’amahera, turaza kuraba ingene twasanze aho turi, dutanga umuco kuri bimwe mu bintu nyamukuru bibabaza twese turiko turashikirwa.


**Icigwa ca 2: Ukwidegemvya mu vy'amahera - Intangamarara ya Bitcoin**

Iyi module izotuma Bitcoin idasobanutse, irenge amajambo y’ikirundi kugira ngo igufashe gutahura ico gitandukanya Bitcoin n’amahera ya kera. Kuva ku kuntu ikora gushika ku kuntu uyikoresha, turakuyobora mu mikorere n'uburyo bwo gukorana na Bitcoin.


**Icigwa ca 3: Gushikama hagati mu kavuyo - Intangamarara y'Ivy'Imirongo n'Isi y'Ibiceri Bikomeye**

Muri iki kiganiro, turaba munsi y’igipfukisho c’ifaranga rihambaye, Tether, turiko turatohoza ingene iyo mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none iguma ifise agaciro kandi ifise ubushobozi bwo guha umwidegemvyo abahanganye n’intwaro y’ubutegetsi, ukubura ibikorwa vy’ivy’ubutunzi canke ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro.


**Icigwa ca 4: Gutsinda amakenga - Gukuraho ivyiyumviro bitari vyo n'ivyo gukoresha mu isi nyakuri**

Kugira ngo dusoze, tuzorwanya ivyiyumviro bitari vyo bikunze kuvugwa ku bijanye na Bitcoin n’amahera y’amahera agumaho maze dutange ingero z’ikoreshwa ry’abantu bamaze kwakira kandi bariko bararonka inyungu muri izo tekinoloji.


Igihe iki cigwa kizoba kirangiye, ntuzoba uronse ubumenyi bukomeye gusa n’ibikoresho vy’agaciro vyo gukoresha mu bijanye n’ivy’ubutunzi, ariko kandi uzotahura neza ingene Bitcoin n’amahera adahinduka, nka Tether, biha ubushobozi abakoresha mu kubashoboza guhitamwo uburyo bundi bwo kugenzura amahera, uburyo bwo gucungera amahera umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ufise ukwo gutahura, uzoba ufise ibikoresho vyiza vyo gukurikirana umwidegemvyo w’amahera, guha ubushobozi umuntu ku giti ciwe no kwidegemvya.


Turanezerewe cane no kuba mwifatanya natwe muri uru rugendo rwo kuja mu bwimbike bw’ubuhinga bwacu bw’amahera.


# Igiciro c'Iterambere - Kwihweza neza Uburyo bwacu bw'Ivy'Imari


<partId>25ed8242-1b5a-5b53-b833-824b0dd80bcc</partId>


## Intangamarara y'amahera


<chapterId>927ad49a-d8d6-5dd3-9250-cdcadcbf425e</chapterId>


Amahera ni ikintu gishimishije kandi gihambaye mu buzima bwacu bwa misi yose. Turayikoresha ku musi ku musi kugira ngo tugure ibifungurwa, twishure amafaranga, kandi dukore amahera menshi cane. Ariko none amahera ni iki, mu vy’ukuri? Mu ntumbero yayo, amahera ni uburyo gusa bwo gukoresha Exchange, igikoresho kidufasha gucuruza ibintu n’ibikorwa hagati yacu. Ni iciyumviro kitaboneka twese dufata nk’ikintu gisanzwe, yamara ni co gihambaye mu bijanye n’ubutunzi bwacu.


Ariko amahera yose ntaremwe angana. Hari ubwoko bw’amahera buraruta ubundi, bivanye n’ubushobozi afise bwo gukora nk’ububiko bw’agaciro, uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange, n’igice c’amahera. Nk’akarorero, inzahabu imaze imyaka ibihumbi ihabwa agaciro kanini kubera ko iramba kandi ikaba idasanzwe. Ku rundi ruhande, amahera y’impapuro afise agaciro gusa nk’uko twizigira inzego ziyatanga.


Muri iki kiganiro, tuzokwihweza ibikorwa n’ibiranga amahera bitandukanye be n’igituma amahera aba meza. Waba uri Joe asanzwe, umucuruzi, umushoramari, canke gusa ushaka kumenya ivy’isi y’ivy’ubutunzi, intumbero yacu ni ukugufasha gutahura neza cane iki ciyumviro kitaboneka ariko gihambaye gikora ku mutima ubuzima bwacu bwose. Rero reka twinjiremwo...


### Amahera ni iki?


Mu buryo bworoshe, amahera ashobora gutahurwa nk’uburyo abantu babiri bemeranya gutanga Exchange y’ikintu, ivyiza canke igikorwa.


Amahera aratuma dushobora guhindura ubutunzi bwacu canke ibikorwa vyacu kugira ngo turonke ububiko bw’agaciro, tutaravye nimba dufise ico dukoresha ubwo nyene kuri ako gaciro kabitswe. Ivyo vyatumye ubutekerezi bwacu bwaguka kandi bugakura neza cane kuruta uko bwari kuba iyo tubandanya kwizigira imigenzo nk’uguhinduranya.


Ku muntu asanzwe, amahera arafise agaciro kuko hari uburyo bubiri gusa bwo kuronka amahera:


1. Tubwirizwa gukoresha umwanya n’inguvu kugira ngo turonke amahera (i.e. akazi, ubukozi, ibikorwa).

2. Tubwirizwa gucuruza ibintu canke ubutunzi kugira ngo turonke amahera.


Ni vyiza kumenya ko mu ngingo ya kabiri iri hejuru, kugira ngo umuntu aronke ivyo bintu n’ivyo bikoresho vyo gucuruza, ku rugero runaka yategerezwa gukoresha umwanya n’inguvu kugira ngo abireme. Turashobora rero gushika ku ciyumviro c’uko dutegerezwa gukoresha umwanya n’inkomezi kugira ngo turonke amahera. Rero:


Amahera = Igihe + Inguvu


Mu kubona amahera nk’ububiko bw’igihe n’inguvu, mu mvugo y’ikigereranyo, turashobora gutahura neza ko amahera ari mu vy’ukuri ibateri– ububiko bw’inguvu bushobora gukoreshwa mu nyuma. Dufise iyo ngereranyo mu muzirikanyi, ugutera imbere kw’amahera, mu vyiyumviro, ni uku kurondera ubudasiba bateri ikora neza kuruta izindi zo kubika umwanya n’inguvu.


### Ni igiki gituma umuntu agira amahera menshi?


Uko usoma intangamarara, ushobora kuba warabonye amajambo atatu ahambaye: ububiko bw’agaciro, ububiko bw’agaciro ka Exchange, n’igice c’ikonti. Ntuhagarike umutima nimba utamenyereye iri lingo. Izo nshingano zitatu ni ngirakamaro kugira ngo amahera agire agaciro uwuyifise kandi zikunda kwitwa inshingano z’amahera.


Reka turabe kimwe cose muri vyo:


1. **Ububiko bw’Agaciro:** Amahera akora nk’uburyo bwo kubika agaciro kugira ngo azoyakoreshe muri kazoza, agatuma uwuyifise ashobora kuzigama ubushobozi bwiwe bwo kugura mu gihe c’igihe. Mu kubigira, bituma uwubifise agira ubushobozi bwo kuzigama no gutegura ivyo azokora muri kazoza. Inzahabu ni akarorero nyamukuru k’ububiko nk’ubwo bw’agaciro, kuko imaze ibinjana n’ibindi ishobora kugura ikoti ryiza ikoresheje ounce imwe gusa.

2. **Igikoresho ca Exchange:** Kugira ngo amahera akore nk’igikoresho gishoboka ca Exchange ku bicuruzwa n’ibikorwa, ategerezwa guhindurwa bitagoranye. Naho umutungo uwo ari wo wose ushobora gukoreshwa nk'amahera, umutungo munini kandi udashobora kwimuka nk'amazu ntushobora gukoreshwa nk'uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange.

3. **Unit of Account:** Ubwa nyuma, amahera akwiye gukora nk’igipimo c’ibiciro vy’ibicuruzwa n’ibikorwa. Ivyo bisigura ko ibintu bishirwako igiciro kandi bikagira agaciro hakurikijwe ayo mahera, bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kugereranya mu buryo bworoshe agaciro k’ibintu n’ibikorwa bitandukanye.


Iyo izo nshingano zitatu z’ingenzi z’amahera ziranguwe zose, ayo mahera arafise ubushobozi bwo gushitsa ivyo ubudandaji busaba bikomeye. Iyo amahera atagira izo nshingano, ntashobora kwizigirwa cane kandi ntashobora kwizigirwa, ivyo bikaba bituma haba ukudatekana n’ukudakeka mu bucuruzi, ivyo bikaba bishobora kugira ingaruka mbi ku muntu ku giti ciwe no ku rwego rw’igihugu.


Dufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, iyo amahera dukoresha aduha uburyo bwo kwizigirwa bwo kubika agaciro, uburyo bwiza bwo kworohereza ibikorwa, n’ingero rusangi y’agaciro, biradushoboza kuzigama no kwubaka ubutunzi, gucuruza twizigiye no gucuruza mu buryo bworoshe. Izo nshingano zose hamwe ntizidufasha gusa mu bushobozi bwacu bwo gucuruza no kuzigama, ariko kandi zirashinga umushinge w’ubutunzi buhamye kandi bukora neza, bugatuma ubutunzi butera imbere cane kandi butera imbere ku bantu ku giti cabo no ku mibano.


Kumbure uriko uricara wibaza uti: "Ok, ndatahura ko kugira ngo amahera atange agaciro, ategerezwa guhura n'ibikorwa vy'amahera vyashizweho haruguru, ariko ivyo abikora gute?"


Ikibazo ciza cane...


Iciyumviro c’amahera menshi coshobora gusa n’ikigoye, ariko mu mutima waco, gisobanurwa n’ibiranga bimwebimwe vy’ingenzi bituma gikora nk’ububiko bw’agaciro bwizigirwa kandi bukora neza, uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange, n’igice c’ikonte. Ivyo Elements vyose hamwe bizwi nk’ibiranga amahera. Dutahuye isano riri hagati y’ibiranga amahera n’ibikorwa vyayo, turashobora gutahura neza igituma amahera amwamwe aryoherwa kuruta ayandi.


### Ibiranga amahera


#### Ububiko bw'agaciro


Kugira ngo amahera akomeze kugira ubushobozi bwo kugura mu gihe kirekire, ategerezwa kuba:


**Durable:** Iyo tuvuga ko amahera ashobora gukomera, tuba turiko turavuga ubushobozi bwayo bwo kwihanganira ukuntu igihe n’ugukoresha bigenda. Ububiko bw’agaciro buramba bisigura ko ayo mahera azoguma afise agaciro uko igihe kigenda kirarenga, ata kuraba ibintu vyose vyo ku mubiri canke vyo mu bidukikije bishobora gutuma yononekara. Nk’akarorero, niwabika amahera yawe mu nzahabu, azoguma afise agaciro kandi akayangane naho ibiceri agereranya vyoba vyacitse ivya kera. Amahera aramvye ni ngirakamaro kuko atuma dushobora kuzigama ubutunzi bwacu mu gihe kirekire ata bwoba bwo gutakaza agaciro kayo.


**Scarce:** Iyo amahera atanga ubukene, tuba dushaka kuvuga Supply iriho. Ivyo birahambaye ku bubiko bw’agaciro kuko iyo hari amafaranga menshi cane, arashobora kugabanya agaciro. Amafaranga make arashobora kuguma afise agaciro uko igihe kigenda kirarenga, ivyo bikaba bituma aba ububiko bw’ubutunzi bwo kwizigirwa. Iyumvire nk'ikintu gifise aho kigarukira - nimba ari bikeyi gusa, birafise agaciro kandi biraronderwa kuruta iyo habayeho Supply itagira aho igarukira. Mu buryo nk’ubwo, amahera makeyi arashobora kuguma afise agaciro kandi akaguma afise ubushobozi bwo kugura, ivyo bikaba bituma ari uburyo bwiza bwo kubika ubutunzi.


**Immutable:** Kugira ngo amahera atange ubudahinduka, akwiye kuba adashobora guhindurwa canke guhindurwa iyo umuntu amaze gucuruza. Ivyo ni ikintu gihambaye cane kiranga ububiko bw’agaciro bwizigirwa kuko bituma agaciro k’amahera katahindurwa canke ngo gahindurwe ataco buvuze. Nk’akarorero, iyo uguze ikintu ukoresheje amahera, ntushobora guhindura ivyiyumviro mu nyuma maze ugasubira inyuma. Navyo nyene, ku mafaranga y’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none nka Bitcoin, iyo amafaranga amaze kwandikwa kuri Blockchain, ntashobora guhindurwa canke gusubirwamwo. Ukwo kudahinduka gutuma abaguzi n’abagurisha bose bagira inyiyumvo yo gutekana no kwizigirwa mu bijanye n’ivy’amahera.


#### Uburinganire bwa Exchange


Kugira ngo amahera abe umuhuza mwiza wo kugura no kugurisha ibintu n’ibikorwa, ategerezwa kuba:


**Portable:** Iyo tuvuze ko amahera ari "portable", tuba dushaka kuvuga ko yoroshe gutwara no gutwara kuva ahantu hamwe uja ahandi. Ivyo ni ikintu gihambaye kiranga umurongo wa Exchange kuko bidushoboza gukoresha amahera mu kugura no kugurisha ibintu n’ibikorwa mu bibanza bitandukanye. Nk’akarorero, nimba ushaka kugura ikawa mu kafe, woshobora gukoresha amahera yawe yo mu minwe (nk’amahera canke ikarata y’inguzanyo) kugira ngo wishyure, naho woba uri hehe. Mu buryo butandukanye n’ubwo, iyo ubwirizwa gutwara ibintu bininibinini kandi biremerera nk’uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange, vyoba bigoye cane kubikoresha mu gucuruza.


**Ibigabanywa:** Ivyo ni ikimenyetso gihambaye c’umurongo mwiza wa Exchange, kikaba kivuga ubushobozi bw’amahera bwo kugabanywa mu bice bitobito kugira ngo bishobore kworohereza ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji vy’ubunini butandukanye. Nk’akarorero, kugura ibintu bitobito vyoba ari urugamba iyo tugira amahera menshi gusa. Ugucapura bituma dushobora kwishura neza, tutaravye ubunini bw’amahera, ivyo bikaba bituma amahera aba ngirakamaro kandi akagira akamaro mu buzima bwa misi yose. Mu vy’ukuri, uko amafaranga ashobora kugabanywa ni ko n’abantu bashobora kuyakoresha no kuyakoresha.


**Yemewe:** Iyo tuvuga ku kwemerwa, tuba turiko turavuga nimba hariho ukwemerwa kwagutse kw’ubwoko bumwe bw’amahera. Ivyo bisigura ko abantu biteguriye kwemera no gukoresha ubwo buryo bw’amahera nk’uburyo bwa Exchange ku bicuruzwa n’ibikorwa. Iyo ifaranga ryemewe cane, biroroshe ko abantu binjira mu bucuruzi, kuko hariho ifaranga rusangi ryo kugura no kugurisha ibintu n'ibikorwa. Uko amafaranga yemerwa cane, ni ko arushiriza kugira agaciro, kuko abantu benshi biteguye kuyakoresha. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo amafaranga atemewe cane, aratakaza agaciro kayo, kuko abantu bazokekeranya kuyemera nk’uburyo bwo gutanga Exchange.


#### Igice ca konti


Kugira ngo amahera akoreshwe nk’ingero rusangi y’agaciro k’ibintu n’ibikorwa, ategerezwa kuba:


**Fungible:** Iyo amahera avuzwe ko ari fungible, igice cose c’amahera gishobora guhindurwa n’ikindi gice cose. Mu majambo yoroshe, bisigura ko amahera ari kimwe kandi asa, ata kuraba aho yava canke uwuyafise. Nk'akarorero, iyo ufise umwenda w'umuntu \$10 ukamuha \$10, ntaco bimaze nimba iyo fagitire yava kuri Wallet yawe canke Wallet y'uwundi muntu. Igihe cose ari amafaranga y'ukuri y'amadolari 10, afatwa ko afise agaciro kangana. Iciyumviro c’uguhindura amahera ni ikintu gihambaye kuko gituma amahera akora neza nk’ingero rusangi, bigatuma ibikorwa vyo gucuruza vyoroha kandi bikaba vyiza.


Iciyumviro


Amahera ni ikintu gihambaye kandi gishimishije mu buzima bwacu bwa misi yose. Ikora nk’umuhuza, igatuma dushobora gucuruza ibintu n’ibikorwa hagati yacu. Ariko rero, amahera yose ntaremwa angana. Hari ubwoko bw’amahera buraruta ayandi nk’ububiko bw’agaciro, nk’ibiceri vy’inzahabu, mu gihe ubundi bushobora kuba bwiza cane nk’uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange, ni ukuvuga idolari ry’Amerika. Ariko iyo izo nshingano ziranguwe zose, biradushoboza gukorana n’abandi twizigiye kandi bitagoranye, ivyo bikaba bitadufasha gusa nk’abantu ku giti cabo, ariko kandi bikaba bituma ubutunzi bwacu butera imbere cane kandi bugatera imbere cane.


Mu biganiro bizoza, tuzokwihweza uburyo bubiri buzwi cane bw’amahera: Bitcoin na stablecoins. Mu kubisuzuma biciye mu birimwo vyavuzwe muri iki gice, turaza kumenya ingene birangura ibikorwa bitandukanye vy’amahera n’ingene bishobora kugirira akamaro kanini abantu.


Kuva ku guhinduranya amafaranga gushika ku guhingura ibiceri n’amahera y’impapuro, amahera yarahindutse cane kugira ngo ashobore guhura n’ivyo abantu bakeneye biguma bihinduka. Uko tuja mu kigabane gikurikira, reka duhindure inzira, tushire umutima ku bijanye n’ugutera imbere kw’amahera.


## Isuzuma ry'ingene twashitse hano


<chapterId>4c8ebb36-a6d5-5637-93ca-9a4a222a1c58</chapterId>


Kuva mu misi y’uguhinduranya ibintu gushika mu gihe ca none c’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none, amahera yarateye imbere bitangaje. Ba sogokuruza bacu bakoresha ibikoko, amabuye, eka mbere n’ibitungwa nk’ivyo gukoresha Exchange. Uyu musi, dufise ama wallets virtuels n’ukwishura ata muntu akora. Ni urugendo rudasanzwe rwabonye ibisubirwamwo bitagira uko bingana, uguhinduranya, n’uguhindura ibintu kugira ngo bishobore gushitsa ivyo abantu bakeneye bihora bihinduka.


Ariko none amahera dukoresha yahindutse gute kugira ngo abe ikintu gihambaye cane mu buzima bwacu nk’uko ari muri iki gihe? Muri iki gice, tuzokwihweza ingene amahera yateye imbere, kuva ku buryo bwayo bwa kera gushika ku mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none dukoresha muri iki gihe. Tuzokwihweza cane isubiramwo ry’amahera ryose, turabe ingene ryafashije mu guhingura ikibano cacu ca none.


_**Iciyumviro gica bugufi:** Ni ngombwa kugaragaza ko iki gice atari inkuru y’urutonde rw’ibihe vy’iterambere ry’amahera. Ahubwo ni urugendo rw’inyigisho cane ku bijanye n’ugutera imbere n’ugugwa kw’ubwoko butandukanye bw’amahera. Benshi muri abo bavuzi ba Exchange barabaho icarimwe, kandi bamwebamwe baracariho n’ubu mu buryo bumwe, mu buryo canke mu buryo._


Uhejeje gusoma iyi ntangamarara, woshobora kwibaza uti: **Kubera iki amahera akeneye gutera imbere no guhinduka uko igihe kigenda kirarenga?**


Inyishu ni yoroshe: ivyo dukeneye n’ivyo twipfuza birahinduka uko ikibano n’ubuhinga bitera imbere. Kandi uko ivyo dukeneye n’ivyo twipfuza bihinduka, ni ko n’ingene dukoresha amahera n’ingene tuyaha agaciro birahinduka. Nk’akarorero, mu bihe vya kera, abantu barizigira guhinduranya ibintu n’ibikorwa vy’amahera y’agaciro ka Exchange, mugabo uko imibano yagenda iratera imbere, vyaragaragaye ko hari hakenewe uburyo bumwe bw’amahera bushingiye ku rugero kandi bushobora gutwara umuntu. Ivyo vyatumye habaho ibiceri, amaherezo vyasubiriwe n’amahera y’impapuro, ubu hakaba n’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none. Igihe cose umuntu asubiramwo amahera, arafise ivyiza n’ibibi, kandi uko ubuhinga n’imibano bigenda biratera imbere, birashoboka cane ko tuzobona mbere n’amahinduka menshi mu bijanye n’ingene dukoresha amahera be n’ingene tuyaha agaciro.


Gutahura ico ciyumviro c’ugutera imbere kw’amahera ni ikintu gihambaye kuko bidufasha kubona ingene amahera yahindutse uko igihe kigenda kirarenga be n’ingene yoshobora kubandanya guhinduka muri kazoza.


Dufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, reka turabe uburyo nyamukuru bwa Exchange bukoreshwa muri iki gihe canke bwakoreshejwe mu gihe kanaka kera.


1. **Guhinduranya:** Exchange y’ibicuruzwa canke ibikorwa ataco ikoresheje amahera.

2. **Amahera y’Ibicuruzwa:** Exchange y’ibicuruzwa vyemejwe ko bibonwa ko bifise agaciro, nk’umunyu canke ibikoko vyo mu kiyaga.

3. **Amahera y'ibiceri:** Gukoresha ivyuma vy'agaciro, nk'inzahabu canke ifeza, mu buryo bw'ibiceri nk'uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange.

4. **Amahera y’Impapuro Ashigikiwe n’Ivyuma:** Amahera y’impapuro ashigikiwe n’ikintu gifatika, nk’inzahabu canke ifeza.

5. **Amahera ya Fiat:** Amafaranga adashigikiwe n’ikintu gifatika ahubwo afise agaciro kubera ko Leta itangaza ko ari amafaranga yemewe n’amategeko.

6. **Cryptocurrencies:** Amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none canke y’ubuhinga bwa none akoresha ubuhinga bwa digitale kugira ngo akingire amafaranga no kugenzura uguhingura ibice bishasha.


Ivyo tubifise mu muzirikanyi, reka dusuzume kimwe cose kugira ngo turonke ugutahura kwose kw’ingene twashitse aho turi uno musi.


### Guhanahana


Guhinduranya! Ni iciyumviro coroshe: ugura ikintu ufise n’ikintu ushaka canke ukeneye.


Ariko none, vyoba ari ngirakamaro?


Ikibazo co guhinduranya ni uko kuronka umuntu ashaka ivyo ufise kandi afise ivyo ushaka bishobora kuba urugamba. Nk’akarorero, wiyumvire ko uri umurimyi w’ingano ukeneye ishati rishasha. Woshobora gushaka kure cane kugira uronke umuhinguzi w’amashati yiteguriye guhindura ishati n’ingano zawe. Ariko none uwo muhinguzi w’amashati yoba adashaka ingano zawe? Ico kibazo kizwi nk’uguhuza kabiri kw’ivyo umuntu yipfuza. Gucuruza neza bisaba ko ivyo umuntu ashaka bihuye kabiri, bisobanura ko abo bompi bategerezwa kuba bafise ikintu uwundi ashaka gucuruza.


Ikindi kibazo kiri mu guhindura ibintu ni uko bishobora kuba bidashoboka ku bintu bimwebimwe. None wogabanya gute inka nzima kugira ngo uyigurishe inkweto? Kandi ata n’urugero rumwe rwo guharura, kugereranya agaciro k’ibintu n’ibikorwa biragoye. Mbega inka yoba ifise agaciro karenze canke gatoyi kuruta amasaka cumi y’ingano canke imizingo ibiri y’impuzu?


Hejuru y’ivyo vyose, ibintu vyinshi n’ibikorwa vyinshi birashobora kwonona kandi bikabura agaciro uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Rero nimba wizigiye uguhinduranya nk’uburyo bwo kuronka Exchange, utegerezwa gukomeza gucuruza no gukoresha ibintu vyawe n’ibikorwa vyawe kugira ngo ntutakaze agaciro.


Naho hari izo ngorane, uguhinduranya ibintu biracakoreshwa mu bihe bimwebimwe. Kenshi uzobona uguhinduranya bikoreshwa mu gihe c’ugucuruza kw’isoko ryo kuri Internet, canke mu bihugu aho amafaranga yananiwe gutanga ububiko bw’agaciro, abantu barondera kubika agaciro mu bicuruzwa. Ivyo bivuzwe, ntivyemerwa cane.


Muri vyose, uguhinduranya bishobora kuba ari uburyo bwiza kandi bwakoreshwa cane mu gucuruza ibintu mu bihe vya kera, ariko bwari bufise akaga kamwe gakomeye: "uguhuza ivyifuzo." Mu yandi majambo, kugira ngo uguhinduranya Exchange kuroranirwe, ababiri bategerezwa kuba bafise ico uwundi ashaka. Ivyo bishobora kuba umutwe nyawo kandi bikajana mu biganiro vyinshi bitagira ico bivamwo. Turakenguruka ko twaciye kure y’uguhinduranya kandi twateguye uburyo bwiza bwo gushika ku bicuruzwa n’ibikorwa vya Exchange.


### Ibicuruzwa


Uko uguhinduranya ibintu vyatangura kwerekana ubugoyagoye bwavyo mu bucuruzi, abantu ku giti cabo be n’ubutunzi vyari bikeneye cane ubundi buryo bwo guhindura ibintu. Igishimishije, n’uguseruka kw’ibicuruzwa nk’uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange, ivyo twari dukeneye vyarahaze... mu gihe gito. Mu gusobanura imbere y’igihe igicuruzwa umuntu wese yemera ko gifise agaciro, twari dufise uburyo bwacu bwa mbere bw’amahera bwakora nk’umuhuza kugira ngo tugabanye ugushihana mu vy’ubudandaji.


Ikintu gikomeye mu guhitamwo uburyo bwa Exchange bwategekanijwe imbere y’igihe ni uko imiryango yoshobora guhitamwo ikintu gitanga ubukene kandi kitazokwonona, kigatuma iba ububiko bw’agaciro buramba. Ibintu nk’amabuye y’ibirahuri, umunyu be n’ibikoko vyo mu kiyaga vyaciye vyihuta kuronderwa uko vyaharurwa, bikaba bikomeye cane kandi bikaba bishobora gutwarwa mu masaho. Umunyu cane cane wari ukunzwe cane kuko wari ufise akamaro - gukiza inyama, n’ibindi.


Ariko rero, uko ingendo zagenda zoroha, isi yaratanguye gufunguka, abantu baratahura yuko ubutunzi buke bwo mu karere kamwe bwari bwinshi mu bindi. Ivyo vyatumye haba ugukoresha nabi, Supply igabanuka, kandi bituma haba ibintu nk’ubudandaji bw’abaja. Nk’akarorero, Abanyaburaya bariko baragendera muri Afirika babonye ko abantu bo ng’aho bariko bakoresha amabuye y’ibirahuri nk’uburyo bwo kuronka amahera. Kubera ko abaje kwimukira mu Buraya vyari vyoroshe gukora ibirahuri, ivyo bikaba vyatuma bazana ayo mabuye menshi muri Afirika, ivyo bikaba bituma agaciro kayo kagabanuka. Bamwe mbere bovuga ko iyo nzira y’ugusenyuka ari kimwe mu vyatumye haba [ubudandaji bw’abaja](https://breedlove22.medium.com/ba shebuja-n’abaja-b’amahera-255ecc93404f), ivyo bikaba vyatumye ubutunzi bwa Afirika busenyuka.


Muri rusangi, amahera y’ibicuruzwa yaragize uruhara runini mu guteza imbere ubudandaji n’ubudandaji, kuko yatanga uburyo bumwe bumwe bwa Exchange bwemewe cane. Ariko rero, uko imibano yagenda iratera imbere, ni ko hatangura kuboneka ubundi buryo bw’amahera bwari bubereye kandi bushobora kugabanywa.


Kugira ngo abantu bashobore gutorera umuti izo ngorane, batanguye kurondera ibicuruzwa vyari vyemewe kw’isi yose ko bikenewe, ivyo bikaba vyatumye hakoreshwa ivyuma vy’agaciro nk’uburyo bwo gukoresha Exchange.


### Amahera yahinguwe


Naho mu vy’ubuhinga bari bakiri amahera y’ibicuruzwa, uko abantu babandanya kurondera amahera aruta ayandi, baratsitaye ku ntwari batari biteze: ivyuma vy’agaciro. Ivyo vyuma ntivyari vyiza gusa kandi vyipfuzwa kubera ko vyakoreshwa mu gukora amabuye y’agaciro, ariko kandi vyarashirako akamenyetso kenshi mu masandugu y’ivyo bituma umuntu aba ubutunzi bwiza cane bw’amahera. Kubera ko ivyo vyuma vyari bike cane kw’isi yose be n’amahera menshi vyasabwa kugira ngo ivyo vyuma bicukurwe, bitunganywe kandi bibikwa, vyatumye baronka amahera menshi kuruta ayandi mafaranga yari afise kera.


Vyongeye, ivyuma nk’inzahabu vyari bimwe mu vyuma bitagira ico bikora cane Elements biri mu rutonde rw’ibihe, ivyo bikaba vyatuma bikomera cane kandi ntibishobora gusenyuka.


Uko ubuhinga bwagenda buratera imbere, inzahabu n’ifeza vyarahindutse, bica bifungwa, bikagira ishusho, bigaca bishirwako ikidodo bikagira ibiceri, ivyo bikaba vyatumye Exchange irushiriza kworoha. Agaciro kagereranywa n’ibimenyetso vyari kuri ivyo biceri vyagabanuye cane amahera yakoreshwa mu kugenzura uburemere n’ubusuku bw’ivyuma vy’agaciro. Ariko, nk’uko bigenda ku bintu vyiza vyinshi, hari umuntu yama aronka uburyo bwo kuvyungukirako. Gucapura ibiceri vya Coin vyarateye imbere cane, abantu ku giti cabo be n’intwaro baracapura ibice vy’ivyo biceri kugira ngo bagabanye uburemere bwavyo bw’ivyuma vy’agaciro mu gihe bagerageza kuguma bafise agaciro kavyo k’intango. Ivyo vyatumye haba uburyo bwa mbere bwo guca agaciro k’amahera, bituma habaho ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro.


Ikintu catumye ibintu bikomera kuruta, ni uko uko isi yagenda irahinduka isi yose, inzahabu n’ifeza vyagenda birushiriza kugora gutwara no gucuruza, na canecane abagendera mu mazi.


### Amafaranga y'impapuro zishigikiwe n'icuma


Injira mu mpapuro zishigikiwe n’ivyuma, umuti w’amahera menshi yo gutwara ibintu be n’ingorane zo gutakaza ivyuma vy’agaciro. Ariko nk’uko tuzobibona, uwo muti wari ufise ingorane zawo wo gutsinda.


Twaravuye kure cane mu misi yo guhinduranya no kugurisha ibintu. Igihe ivyuma vy’amahera vyaza, amaherezo twararonse ububiko buhamye bw’agaciro bwashobora gukoreshwa kw’isi yose. Ariko rero, ni ukuzana amahera y’impapuro ashingiye ku cuma kwahinduye vy’ukuri uburyo dukorana.


Iyumvire: ntuzosubira gutwara imifuko iremereye y’inzahabu canke kwiganyira ku bijanye n’ubusuma. Ahubwo, abantu ku giti cabo barashobora gushiramwo inzahabu yabo mu bubiko maze bakaronka ikimenyetso c’uko bashobora kugurisha nk’inzahabu y’umubiri. Ivyo vyatumye amahera ashobora guhindurwa, kugabanywa no gutwara, bituma ubudandaji bwo kw’isi yose bworoha cane. Ivyo bihembo vyari gushobora rero gutwarwa bitagoranye mu nzira ndende, ivyo bikaba vyatuma umuntu ashobora gukora ubudandaji mpuzamakungu ata n’amahera menshi yo gutwara. Naho vyatwaye igihe gitoyi kugira ngo impapuro zishingiye ku cuma nk’uburyo bw’amahera ziveho, igihe Ubwami bw’Ubwongereza bwagenda buragwira, vyaciye vyihuta kuba ikintu gisanzwe.


Ariko nk’uko bigenda ku buhinga bushasha ubwo ari bwo bwose, ibibazo vyaratanguye kuvyuka.


Ica mbere, ububiko bw’inzahabu, kubera ko bamenye ko abakiriya babo badakunda kugaruka gukura inzahabu izo mpapuro z’inzahabu zari zivuga, batangura gutanga amafaranga y’impapuro ata n’inzahabu zishigikiwe, ivyo bikaba vyatumye habaho ugushinga mu mpisho uburyo bwa mbere bwo gucungera inzahabu (abazitanga bafata gusa igice c’amahera abakiriya bazigamye). Kandi mbere n’igihe ibihugu vyagerageza gushigikira amafaranga yabo n’inzahabu, kenshi vyarakoresha nabi iyo nzira, ivyo bikaba vyatuma ubutunzi buhungabana.


Ubwa kabiri, amahera y’impapuro akoresheje ivyuma ntiyari akingiwe n’ukwihenda. Naho hariho ibintu vy’umutekano, abahimbaza amahera boshobora guhingura amakete y’ibinyoma yoshobora kugora kumenya.


Naho amafaranga y’impapuro akoresheje ivyuma yari afise ingorane zayo, ukuntu yari ashobora guhindurwa, kugabanywa be n’ugutwarwa, vyatumye habaho uburyo bwo gukoresha amafaranga y’impapuro dukoresha muri iki gihe, aho akenshi uburyo bwo gukoresha bushobora gusumba ubukene.


### Ifaranga rya Fiat


Amafaranga ya Fiat ni yo yabaye umushinge w’ubuhinga bwacu bw’amahera mu myaka mirongo. Ijambo "fiat" ni ijambo ry'ikilatini risobanura "reka bikorwe" kandi ryerekeza ku bubasha bwa Leta bwo gutangaza amafaranga nk'amahera yemewe. Udakunze amafaranga yahora ashigikirwa n’inzahabu canke ibindi bintu vy’agaciro, agaciro ka fiat kava ku masezerano ya leta y’uko hari uwuzoyemera muri Exchange ku bicuruzwa n’ibikorwa.


Amafaranga ya Fiat yaje mu gihe ibihugu vyari bihanganye n’ugucika intege kubera amafaranga y’impapuro ashigikiwe n’ivyuma– intwaro zobwirizwa kuronka inzahabu nyinshi kugira zicape amahera menshi y’impapuro. Ivyo vyari intambamyi, rero igihe cose igihugu cari gikeneye umutungo, caraheba iyo nkoko mu gihe gitoyi, kigaca kigwiza amahera yaco Supply. Iryo shirahamwe rishasha nta kindi ryari rishigikiwe atari ukwizera Leta kubera ko ryari amahera yemewe n’amategeko. Si ivyo gusa, iyo mafaranga mashasha yaragabanyije agaciro k’amafaranga yasigaye mu nzira mu gutera imbere Supply y’amahera, kandi amadolari menshi akurikira ibicuruzwa nk’ivyo, ibiciro vyaradutse.


Amafaranga y’impapuro ashingiye ku cuma yatanguye gusenyuka mu mpera z’Intambara ya Kabiri y’Isi Yose. Kubera ukwizera kwinshi muri Amerika, abarongozi b’isi yose barahuriye i Bretton Woods, muri New Hampshire, maze bafata ingingo y’uko Amerika izofatanya idolari ryayo n’inzahabu, isi yose na yo ikafatanya amafaranga yabo n’idolari. Ivyo vyasobanura ko inzahabu nyinshi zo kw’isi zasukwa muri Amerika kugira ngo zibe nziza, ivyo bikaba vyatumye ibihugu vyinshi bitakaza inzahabu zavyo zo mu gihugu.


Mu mpera z’imyaka ya 60 no mu ntango z’imyaka ya 70, Amerika, yumvise ko ifise uburenganzira bwo gushigikira inzahabu, yatanguye kwagura amahera yabo Supply kugira ngo ifashe mu ntambara yo muri Vietnam. Ubufaransa ntibwavyishimiye, buca busaba ko basubizwa inzahabu yabo. Ivyo vyatumye abantu bihutira kurondera inzahabu, kandi kubera ko Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika zari zacapye amadolari menshi cane kuruta inzahabu zari zifise, zaciye zicapura rwose iyo nkoko. Ico kintu citwa Nixon Shock, casobanura ko abantu ku giti cabo n’ibihugu bitagishobora Redeem amadolari yabo kugira ngo baronke inzahabu. Kuva uyu musi, twabonye ukwiyongera kw’amafaranga y’amafiat– amafaranga ata kindi ashigikiwe atari umwenda n’ukwizera kwacu muri Leta.


Ariko rero, ugutera imbere kw’amahera ntikwahagaze aho. Kubera iterambere ry’ubuhinga, amahera ya fiat yarabandanije gutera imbere. Muri iki gihe, gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none vyarateye imbere cane, aho gukoresha banki za internet n’uburyo bwo kwishura kuri internet nka Visa, Mastercard, Paypal, Square, na Venmo ni vyo bimenyerewe.


Kandi mu myaka ya vuba, twabonye ibiganiro vyinshi ku bijanye n’amafaranga y’amabanki nkuru (CBDCs), ihinduka rishasha ry’amafaranga y’amafaranga, ritanga uburyo bwose bw’amafaranga yacu y’amafaranga y’amafaranga.


CBDCs zitandukanye n’amafaranga ya fiat twamenyereye kuko ziha uwuzitanga uburenganzira bwo kubona vyose mu bikorwa vyose n’ubushobozi bwo gufata ingingo y’uwushobora n’uwudashobora gukoresha ayo mafaranga. Leta n’amabanki akomeye vyaravuze cane ku bijanye n’intumbero zavyo zo gushiramwo ama CBDC, zivuga inyungu nk’ubugenzuzi bushingiye ku rwego rwo hejuru, gutuma amafaranga akoreshwa neza, n’ubushobozi bwo gushiramwo amasheki y’inyongera vyihuse.


Naho CBDC zitanga inyungu nyinshi, zizana kandi n’ingorane zikomeye zishobora gushika. Nk’akarorero, intwaro zishobora guhagarika amakonti ya banki ataco zitwaye, zigashiraho igihe co gukoresha amahera yacu kugira ngo ziteze imbere ugukoresha no kubuza abo dushobora gukorana n’abo tudashobora gukorana na bo.


Ikindi kandi, ubushobozi bwo guhindukira buja ku bijanye n’akaranga k’ubuhinga bwa none buriko buragwira cane, nk’uko bigaragara mu Bushinwa n’ivy’ubuhinga bwabo bwa CBDC be n’ugushiraho amanota y’inguzanyo z’imibano, ivyo bikaba vyaragize ingaruka ku mwidegemvyo mu gihugu cose mu kubuza abantu kuronka inzu, ibigo vy’imari, n’uburenganzira bw’ishimikiro bwo kwimuka.


Kubera ko CBDCs ahanini zitageragejwe, ntidushobora kuvuga neza ivyiza n’ibibi bizoba. Ariko rero, turashobora kwemera tudakeka ko CBDC ziha intwaro n’amabanki ububasha bukomeye cane ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bwacu bw’amahera.


Amafaranga ya Fiat nta gukeka ko yahindutse cane mu bihe vya vuba, ahanini bivuye ku gutera imbere kw’ubutunzi bw’ubuhinga bwa none. Kugira ngo amafaranga y’amafiat ashobore gushitsa ivyo abaguzi bakeneye bigenda birahinduka, yarahindutse bivanye n’ivyo. Ariko rero, n’uguseruka kw’ama CBDC, dutegerezwa kuguma twirinda ingorane zishobora guterwa n’aho yoba afise inyungu mu bijanye n’ukwihuta n’ubushobozi.


Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, abantu babonye ukuntu ububasha bwo kugura bugenda buragabanuka be n’ukuntu Leta igenda igenzura neza hamwe n’ukwiyongera kw’amahera y’amahera, batanguye kurondera uburyo bundi bwo kuyakoresha.


### Amafaranga y'ibanga


Ibaze isi aho amahera yawe yoshobora kubikwa no guhindurwa mu buryo bwa digitale ata n’umwe akeneye abahuza canke abandi bantu bo kwizigira. Isi aho Supply y’amahera yari idashobora guhindurwa, idasanzwe kandi iri mu minwe y’abanyagihugu aho kuba intwaro canke amabanki. Iyi ni isi amafaranga y’imbere mu gihugu, Bitcoin, yaremye kuva yatanguye mu 2009.


Bitcoin yavutse mu kurondera kw’umuhinga mu vy’ubuhinga bw’amabanga (cryptographer) kugira ngo akore ubuhinga bushasha kandi buteye imbere bw’ivyuma vy’amahera dukunda cane. Bariko barondera inzahabu y’ubuhinga bwa none, ni ukuvuga ubutunzi bw’amahera bushobora kubika agaciro, bugatanga ubuzima buramba, kandi bugakoreshwa mu gukora ibikorwa vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Kandi rero, Bitcoin yasohotse nk’umutungo wa mbere w’agaciro, w’ubuhinga bwa none, kandi w’amahera make.


Igituma Bitcoin idasanzwe vy’ukuri ni uko ari igikoresho co gutwara ibintu mu buryo bwa digitale, bisobanura ko ata bahuza canke abandi bantu bizigira bakenewe. Itegeko ry’amahera rigenzurwa n’abagira uruhara mu bijanye n’ibidukikije, bikaba bituma bidashoboka guhindura canke guhindura mu buryo bumwe n’ubwo bwari busanzwe mu buryo bw’amahera bwa kera. Kandi nk’uko Bitcoin iriho hanze y’ububasha bwa Leta n’amabanki nkuru, iriko iragenda yihuta kwemerwa cane nk’ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha amahera kuko idashobora gukoreshwa nabi.


Kuva yatangwa, Bitcoin yarabandanije gukura mu kwemerwa no kwemerwa nk’ikintu c’amahera. Nkako, ubu iriko irakura ku rugero rwa [137%](https://www.benzinga.com/markets/cryptocurrency/22/03/26114752). 76% kubera iterambere rya internet mu myaka imwe. Kandi naho izindi cryptocurrencies zashizweho mu myaka iheze, nta n’imwe yarwanya ikibanza ca Bitcoin nk’ikintu c’amahera gisumba ibindi.


Bamwe mu ba naysayers bavuga ko Bitcoin igenda buhoro, izimvye gukoresha, kandi itakaza inguvu, ariko reka ntitwihutire gucira urubanza. None iyo tubabwira ko Bitcoin iserukira uguhinduka kw’akarorero mu buryo twiyumvira ku bijanye n’amahera n’agaciro?


Mu biganiro bizoza, tuzokwihweza Bitcoin biciye mu yindi nzira, iyo gukoresha intumbero n’ugutera ubwoba. Nuko rero mutwihanganire.


Hagati aho, naho amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none yo muri banki nkuru yoshobora gufatwa nk’aho ari yo ahanganye na Bitcoin, benshi bavuga ko ataco atandukaniyeko n’ayandi mafaranga yose y’ubuhinga bwa none kiretse ko afise ingaruka ziteye ubwoba ku vya politike no ku mibano.


Uko tubandanya tuja mw’isi y’amahera ashobora gutegurwa, Bitcoin iguma mu rwego rwayo bwite. Supply yayo ntishobora gusenyuka canke kwaguka, irafise ingaruka nyinshi ku rubuga n’abakoresha, kandi agaciro kayo n’umutekano wayo bizobandanya gukomera uko urubuga rugenda rurakura. Kandi naho yoba atari yo mafaranga mashasha y’ubuhinga bwa none, aratanga ikintu c’agaciro kuruta cane: ubusegaba nyakuri ku mahera y’umuntu bwite.


Ivyo bivuzwe, naho amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none aserukira urubibi rushasha mu gutera imbere kw’amahera, atanga urugero rwo hejuru rw’umutekano, ubuzima bwite, n’uburyohe, na yo nyene azana n’ingorane zayo bwite n’ingorane zayo, zitegerezwa kwihwezwa neza imbere y’uko zifatwa nk’uburyo bw’amahera.


Tumaze gusuzuma ubwoko butandukanye bw’amahera mu mateka yose, ivyo biratuma haba ikibazo gihambaye:


### Twoba turiko tuja mu nzira nziza?


Muri uru rugendo rwose, twasuzumye ingene amahera atera imbere biteye umunezero, dukurikirana ingene atera imbere kuva ku guhinduranya amahera gushika mu gihe cacu c’ubuhinga bwa none. Twarabonye amafaranga atandukanye aduga akagwa, kuva ku bikoko n’amabuye y’agaciro gushika ku vyuma vy’agaciro n’amahera y’agaciro.


Ariko rero, nk’uko twabibonye, ​​inzira y’ugutera imbere kw’amahera ntiyabaye ata ngorane. Ukwiyongera kw’ugucapura Coin n’ugukoresha nabi amafaranga, ugutera imbere mu gushiramwo ubutegetsi hagati no kuva ku buryo bwemewe muri rusangi bwa Exchange ni ingero nkeyi gusa z’intambamyi twahuye na zo mu nzira.


Uko tuja imbere muri kazoza, dutegerezwa kwibaza, **ugukoresha nabi amafaranga bizobandanya gute kugira ingaruka ku mibereho yacu y’ivy’ubutunzi?**


Kandi, naho bigaragara ko twashize imbere ukworohereza gukoresha uko twava ku guhinduranya amafaranga tuja ku bicuruzwa tuja ku mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none, **twoba dukwiye gusubira kwiyumvira ibiranga duha agaciro cane mu buryo butunganye bw’amahera?**


Ivyo ni ibibazo bikomeye bisaba ko umuntu abizirikana neza kandi akabizirikana. Ariko rero, ikintu kimwe kiratomoye - kazoza k’amahera kari mu maboko yacu. Turafise ububasha bwo guhingura amahera yacu, tukamenya neza ko akora ivyo abantu bakeneye aho gukora gusa uwuyatanga canke intwaro zacu.


Uko tubandanya gutohoza isi y’amahera, birahambaye kwemera amahinduka akomeye yabaye kuva amafaranga y’amahera y’amahera (fiat) atera imbere. Naho ayo mafaranga yatumye habaho uburyo bwiza n’ugushikama, yarazanye kandi ingorane nshasha, nk’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro, ugutera imbere kw’imyenda, n’ubusumbane mu butunzi. Mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza cane ivyo bibazo, kandi mu bice bikurikira, tuzorondera inyishu zishobora gutorera umuti izo ngorane ziteye ubwoba.


## Raba aho turi n'ico dushobora kwitega mu gutera imbere


<chapterId>0c38e8fd-c973-57a5-a673-abec706f6054</chapterId>


Nk’uko twabibonye mu kigabane ca mbere, mu mateka, amahera kenshi yarashigikiwe n’ikintu nk’inzahabu. Ivyiza biva muri ivyo ntibishobora kuvugwa birenze urugero. Iryo sano ntiryari risobanura gusa ko agaciro k’ayo mahera kari gafitaniye isano n’agaciro k’ico kintu, ariko kandi ryasobanura ko uwutanga amahera, cane cane Leta, yari afise aho agarukira mu bijanye n’amahera yashobora gucapura kuko yari gutegerezwa kuronka inzahabu nyinshi.


Ariko uko twagenda tuva ku rugero rw’inzahabu, mu myaka 100 iheze, amahera yararushirije gushirwa ahantu hamwe, amabanki akomeye nka Federal Reserve na banki nkuru ya Amerika akagira ububasha bwinshi ku bijanye n’aho amahera aja.


Muri iki gihe, amabanki akomeye, iruhande y’itunga, mu bisanzwe arafise uburenganzira bwo kuganza ataco akora ku bijanye n’ingene amahera aja be n’ingene amahera agenda. Bafise ubushobozi bwo kwongera Supply y’amahera igihe cose babona ko bikenewe, hamwe no guhindura inyungu kugira ngo ubutunzi butere imbere, mbere no gutanga imfashanyo ku mabanki n’ubudandaji bigenda bibura.


...ariko nk’uko bigenda ku buryo bwose bwo gufasha, nta n’ifunguro ry’umutaga ry’ubuntu.


Iyo amabanki akomeye afashe ingingo yo kwinjiramwo, naho yoshobora gucapura amahera ataco akora, ntashobora gutuma haba agaciro. Kugira ngo ayo mahera aherutse gucapwa abe afise agaciro, agaciro kayo kategerezwa kuva ku bari bafise amahera mbere.


**Tushaka kuvuga iki?** Wiyumvire amahera Supply nk’i pizza, wiyumvire ko yaciwemwo ibice bine. Gukubita kabiri amahera Supply ntivyoba bingana no gukubita kabiri igitigiri ca pizza. Ahubwo vyoba bingana n’uguca ivyo bipande bine mu bice bibiri kugira ngo ukore ibipande umunani. Nta pizza y’inyongera twaronse. Turafise gusa ibice vyinshi, kimwe cose kikaba ari gitoyi mu bunini.


Iyo ducapye amahera menshi, turagabanya agaciro k’amahera asanzwe ariho.


Kugira ngo amabanki akomeye ashobore gukiza igice kimwe c’ubutunzi, ategerezwa gukura mu kindi. Ni co gituma ata mfungurwa zo ku mutaga zitangwa ku buntu.


Kandi kubera ko amahera atagiboshe ku kintu nk’inzahabu, hariho uburyo buke bwo gucungera no gupima Leta itegerezwa gukurikiza, bikaba bituma bagira ububasha bwinshi bwo kwinjiramwo igihe cose babona ko bikenewe. Nk’akarorero, mu bihe vy’ugusubira inyuma kw’ubutunzi nk’ubwo twahuye na bwo mu 2000, 2008 na 2020, amabanki akomeye yarashoboye gufasha ku rugero rutari bwigere ruboneka. Gushiramwo amamiliyaridi y’amadolari mashasha mu bukungu kugira ngo amasoko y’ivy’ubutunzi ahagaze neza.


Iryo koraniro ryaje rifise igiciro kinini ku bucuruzi buto buto, uwuronka umushahara n’ugushikama kw’ubutunzi mu kiringo kirekire, kuko iyo nzira yongerekanye yatumye umwenda w’igihugu utera imbere cane, n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro. Ivyo, nk’uko ndazi neza ko mushobora kubikeka, vyatumye ibiciro vy’ubuzima vyiyongera, bituma abantu ku giti cabo n’imiryango bigorana kuronka ivyo bakeneye.


Muri rusangi, ukuntu amahera ari ahantu hamwe muri iki gihe vyatumye amabanki akomeye agira ububasha butagira uko bungana bwo kwivanga mu bukungu. Naho ivyo bishobora gusa n’ibifise akamaro mu bihe vy’ingorane z’ubutunzi, birashobora kandi gutuma habaho ingorane zikomeye nk’ukwiyongera kw’imyenda n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro. Ivyo tubizirikanye, reka turabe munsi y’ivyo bivugwa bisa n’ibitagira akamaro, umwenda n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro maze dusuzume bimwe mu biva muri vyo.


Imbere yo kwisukamwo, ushobora kubona ko tuvuga muri Amerika uko usoma iki canditswe gikurikira. Turavye ko idolari ry’Amerika ari ryo ry’ububiko bw’isi yose, ivyo bizoshikira idolari bizobagirako ingaruka zija hasi ku bukungu n’amafaranga yose yo kw’isi. Turashira ahabona rero ingorane zimwe zimwe ziri mu rwego rwa Amerika kugira ngo tugaragaze ingorane dufise kw’isi yose. Akenshi, niwasuzuma ububasha bwo mu karere kawe bwite, woshobora gusanga ivy’igihugu cawe bishobora kuba bibi kuruta.


### Ibiciro


Inflation ni ukwiyongera kw’ibiciro vy’ibintu canke ukugabanuka kw’ubushobozi bwo kugura bw’amahera bitewe n’ukwaguka kw’amahera. Kandi bishobora gutahurwa neza nk’amadolari menshi cane akurikira ibicuruzwa bidahagije, bigatuma ibiciro biduga.


Nk’uko twabibonye, ​​ikigereranyo c’ingirakamaro c’amahera Supply ni pizza. Iyo amabanki akomeye ashize amahera mashasha acapwe mu bukungu, ntaba ariko ararema pizza nyinshi. Ahubwo bariko barakata iyo pizza mu bipande bitobito. Ivyo bituma amahera yacu agabanuka, bisobanura ko agaciro k’igice kimwekimwe cose—canke idolari—kagabanuka uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Uko amahera menshi agenda arapompa mu bukungu, ni ko n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro, kandi ubushobozi bwo kugura bw’idolari buragabanuka, ivyo bikaba bituma ibiciro vy’ibintu n’ibikorwa vyiyongera.


Kugira ngo mubone iciyumviro c’urugero rw’icapa ry’amahera turiko turavuga, mu myaka cumi iheze gusa, amadolari y’Amerika yacapuwe ararengeye amadolari yose y’Amerika yacapuwe mu mateka yose y’ayo mafaranga. Nivyo - amahera menshi yaracapwe mu myaka cumi iheze kuruta ayo mu binjana bibiri vyaheze vyose hamwe! Ntibitangaje rero kubona agaciro k’amahera yacu gasa n’akariko karagenda karazimangana ningoga kuruta itosi ry’amazi ryo mu bugaragwa.


Ivyo bishobora kuba Hard kugira ngo ubibone, rero reka turabe akarorero k’ivyiyumviro.


Reka tuvuge ko turonka umushahara w'amadolari 30.000 ku mwaka, kandi turiko turategura kugura imodoka nshasha igura amadolari 15.000. Tumaze gukora ibiharuro, turabona ko ushobora kuzigama \$5,000 ku mwaka. Ivyo bisigura ko, kubera zero inflation, vyodutwara imyaka itatu kugira ngo tuzigamire amahera y’imodoka. Bimeze nk'ibibereye...


Ariko rero, muri iyo nzira, turiko turananirwa gutanga inyishu ku bijanye n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro. Iyo dushizemwo inflation mu vyo twavuze haruguru, duhura n’inkuru itandukanye cane.


Dufashe ko amafaranga twinjiza n'ubushobozi bwo kuzigama biguma ari uko biri, inyuma y'imyaka itatu y'ugutera imbere kw'ibiciro kw'ibice 10%, iyo modoka ubu yoba igura \$19,965. Ubu turi \$4,965, kandi igihe tuzozigama uwundi mwaka maze tukagira \$19,965, ubu bigura \$21,961. Imodoka iriko iragenda yihuta gushika kure cane.


Muri vyose, kubera ko ata inflation iriho, vyofata imyaka itatu kugira ngo tuzigame imodoka y’amadolari 15.000 iyo dushobora kuzigama amadolari 5.000 ku mwaka. Ariko rero, kubera inflation iri ku 10%, ubu dutegerezwa kuzigama imyaka 4,5. Ivyo ni 50% vy’igihe kirenze! Imyaka 1.5 y’ubuzima bwacu ntituzosubira kuronka.


Iyo umushahara wacu udatera imbere n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro, tuba turiko turaronka amahera make uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Ivyo ni kubera ko ubuzima buriko buraduga, ariko umushahara wacu uguma ari uko uri. Ivyo bituma ubushobozi bwacu bwo kugura bugabanuka, bigatuma bigorana cane kuronka ubuzima nk’ubwo twari dufise kera.


### Amadeni


Mu mateka, intwaro zari zigowe mu bushobozi bwazo bwo gutuma ubutunzi butera imbere kuko zategerezwa kuronka inzahabu nyinshi kugira ngo zironke umutungo wo gutera imbere. Ibi vyagabanya ubushobozi bwabo bwo gukura no kwaguka ibihe bidahera, kuko bategerezwa kwubahiriza amategeko ya fizike.


Ariko rero, inyuma y’Igitero ca Nixon, igihe Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika zaheba urugero rw’inzahabu, intwaro n’amabanki akomeye kw’isi yose vyaronse ubushobozi bwo kwagura amahera Supply uko bishaka, nk’umutungo w’umubiri utagishigikiye amahera. Iryo hinduka ryatumye mu ntango banki nkuru ya Amerika ishobora gutera imbere mu buryo bworoshe mu bihe vy’imibabaro y’ubutunzi. Ariko rero, ivyo vyatanguye nk’ingero yo gutuma ubutunzi butera imbere, vyaciye bihinduka vuba cane, ahubwo vyakoreshwa mu gutuma ubutunzi butera imbere mu buryo bw’ubuhinga.


Haciye igihe, Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika n’izindi leta zaciye zigira icipfuzo kitari ciza co gufata amadeni, ivyo bikaba vyatumye tugira uko tumeze ubu. Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika zakoresheje amahera menshi kuruta ayo zaronse biciye mu misoro no mu bindi bikoresho vy’amahera mu myaka 20 mu myaka 21 iheze. Iyo dushira mu ngiro iyo nzira yo gukoresha amahera mu vy’amahera yacu bwite, turazi ingene vyotuma tugira ingorane z’amahera ningoga.


Amabanki akomeye ubu ari mu bibazo bigoye. Kubera umuzigo w’imyenda, bafise ubundi buryo buke uretse guhagarika inyungu mu buryo bw’ubuhinga mu kugerageza kugabanya umuzigo w’imyenda– Nimba inyungu ziri hasi, rero n’ukwishurwa kw’ibikorwa vy’imyenda ni ko biri. Iyo ibiciro vy’ubutunzi biduga, birashoboka ko imice myinshi y’ubutunzi itazoshobora gutanga inyungu zayo, ivyo bikaba bizotuma yihuta gutakaza amahera.


Ariko rero, ukwo guhagarika inyungu birazana igiciro: Bituma umutungo ushobora kuronka bitagoranye. Ivyo bituma abantu ku giti cabo, ubudandaji be n’intwaro bikunda gufata imyenda y’inyongera, ivyo bikaba bituma umuzigo w’imyenda muri rusangi urushiriza gukomera. Ivyo bituma haba igikorwa co gushiramwo uburinganire kigoye ku mabanki akomeye, ategerezwa kuguma afise inyungu ntoyi bihagije kugira ngo ashobore gucungera imyenda iriho mu gihe kandi abuza kwirundanira imyenda mishasha yoshobora gutuma ubutunzi buhungabana mu gihe kirekire.


Ico gikorwa co gufatanya ntikigenda neza nk’uko vyategekanijwe...


![image](assets/1.webp)


Igishushanyo [Ideni n'Igihugu](https://www.imigenderanire y'igihe kirekire.net/us-imyenda-ku-Gdp/)


Iyo dushize hamwe umwenda wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika, w’amashirahamwe, n’uw’ingo, igiharuro kivamwo ni \$63.14 trillions, bitandukanye n’umusaruro wose w’igihugu ca Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika (GDP) w’amadolari \26.13 trillions. Ivyo bisigura ko USA ifise umwenda wose hamwe w’ibice 241%. Mu yandi majambo, ku \$1 yose y’umusaruro w’igihugu, hariho umwenda munini cane \$2.41.


\$63,14t / \$26,13t = 241%


Reka twiyumvire ko inyungu y’uwo mwenda ari 3%.


3% \* 241% = 7,23%


Urugero rw’umuzigo w’imyenda ya Amerika ni nk’uko mbere no gutanga inyungu ku myenda vyosaba ko haba iterambere ry’umwaka ry’ibice 7,23% - igipimo kiri hejuru cane y’iterambere ry’umusaruro w’igihugu ry’ibice 3,13 kw’ijana.


7,23% - 3,13% = 4,1%


No mu gihe ciza cane aho Amerika yohagarika gukoresha amadeni, igashobora gucungera ibitabu vyayo, umwenda woguma wiyongera n’ibice 4,1% ku mwaka. Ivyo ni kubera ko iterambere ry’umusaruro w’igihugu ridashobora gupfuka neza inyungu z’umwenda.


Kumbure urashobora kubona aho ivyo biriko biraja. Ku Address umuzigo w’imyenda, abari mu bibanza vy’ubutegetsi baragoberwa no kwinjiramwo mu kwinjiza amahera menshi mu bukungu, bigatuma amafaranga agira agaciro gatoyi, bigatuma ubutunzi butera imbere cane. Turi mu nzira y’imyenda ata nzira itomoye yo gusohokamwo.


Naho ubu buryo butanga imfashanyo y’igihe gito, amaherezo, turiko turarushirizaho gusa ingorane y’imyenda myinshi. Kuronka umuti w’igihe kirekire wo kugabanya umwenda bizosaba amahitamwo agoye n’umutima ukunze wo gufata ingingo zikomeye mu gihe gito. Ariko ivyo ni ivy’iyindi nzira yose. Hagati aho, reka turabe igituma umwenda n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro bitagira ingaruka ku bantu bose kimwe. Bigira ingaruka zidahuye n’ivyo umuntu aronka umushahara.


### Ubusumbasumbane bw'ubutunzi


Amahera iyo yinjiye mu bukungu, akunda guteranira hamwe mu bintu bimwebimwe: Itunga!


Kubera iki? Woshobora kubaza. Iyo amabanki akomeye yongeye amahera Supply mu gucapura amahera mashasha, agaciro k’amahera yose karagabanuka. Ivyo bisigura ko ibiciro vy’ibicuruzwa n’ibikorwa bikunda kwiyongera uko igihe kigenda kirarenga, bikaba bituma habaho ibiciro vyinshi vy’ibintu vy’ishimikiro nk’ibifungurwa, inzu, n’ubuvuzi. Uwo muvuduko w’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro urasenyura ubushobozi bwo kugura bw’abantu bizigira umushahara n’imishahara kugira ngo baronke amahera.


Ufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, woba uvyurirwa umutima wo kubika amahera yawe uzigamye mu mafaranga Hard? Birumvikana ko atarivyo. Iyo ufise ubushobozi, urasohoka ukagura ivy’ubutunzi. Kubera ko abantu basaba ivy’ubutunzi mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, agaciro kavyo karaduga. Abafise rero ivy’ubutunzi nk’ivy’ubutunzi, ivy’ubutunzi, n’ivy’ubutunzi, bararonka inyungu, ku rugero runaka, ku bijanye n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro kuko agaciro k’ivyo bintu gakunda kwiyongera uko ibiciro vy’ubutunzi vyiyongera. Ivyo bituma ugutera imbere kw’ubutunzi gutuma ubusumbasumbane bw’ubutunzi bukomera mu gutuma haba amacakubiri hagati y’abafise itunga n’abashingiye ku mishahara n’imishahara, ivyo bikaba bituma ubutunzi bwinjira mu maboko y’abantu bo hejuru.


Reka dukoreshe ugutahura kwacu gushasha kugira ngo dusuzume ivy’amazu n’ibindi.


Kubera ko amakuru aguma atangazwa ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi, kumbure warabonye ikibazo c’ugutera imbere kw’imivurungano n’ubusumbasumbane bw’ubutunzi kw’isi yose. Kimwe mu bituma iyo migumuko iguma itera imbere ni uko umuntu asanzwe arushiriza kugorwa no kuronka inzu, nk’uko bigaragazwa n’uko igitigiri c’ibiciro vy’inzu n’imishahara cavuye hejuru gato y’ine mu myaka ya 1980 kija hejuru y’indwi muri iki gihe. Mu yandi majambo, umuntu asanzwe ubu ategerezwa gukoresha incuro indwi umushahara wiwe w’umwaka kugira ngo ashobore kuronka inzu y’igiciro gisanzwe.


**Kubera iki bigorana cane kugura inzu?** Biriko biragora cane kugura inzu kubera imvo zibiri.


1. Inflation iriko iragabanya agaciro k’ubushobozi bwo kugura bw’amahera yacu. Kubera ko amafaranga ariko arasenyuka, abantu ntibaciye bavyurirwa umutima wo kuzigama. Ivyo bihatira Abantu bafise ubutunzi kwerekeza ubutunzi bwabo mu mitungo y’amahera mu gihe abantu batagira ubutunzi bayobora mu gukoresha. Uko ugukoresha birungika amahera mu mashirahamwe afiswe n’abatunzi, amahera y’ubwenge na yo akayobora amahera yabo mu mitungo, turabona ingaruka z’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro vy’imitungo bitewe n’ukwiyongera kw’abasaba. Ivyo vyose mu gihe inflation iriko iratera ingorane ubushobozi bwo kugura bw’amahera.


2. Kubera umuzigo w’imyenda yacu urenze urugero, intwaro ziraterwa intege zo guhagarika inyungu. Mu kubigira, ugukoresha amadeni birarushiriza gukwegera, canecane abafise ubutunzi. Iyo igiciro c’itunga kiri hasi cane, abantu bagurana ibirenze ubushobozi bwabo, bagatuma itunga ryinshi rigira itunga kandi bigatuma ibiciro biduga. Ivyo ni vyiza ku bafise itunga; ariko rero, ibiciro biriko birarushiriza kuba ibidashobora kuronka ku bagerageza kwinjira mu ngazi y’amazu canke gutera amano mu masoko y’ivy’ubutunzi. Itegeko ryoroshe ni uko uko inyungu zigabanuka, ibiciro vy’itunga biraduga uko umutungo ushobora kuboneka mu mwidegemvyo.


**Iyo inflation ikomeza gute ubusumbasumbane bw’ubutunzi?** Turavye ko abantu bo hejuru bafise itunga kandi abo hasi bagakunda gufata amafaranga, ikivako ni ubusumbasumbane bw’ubutunzi bugenda buragabanuka uko ubushobozi bwo kugura bw’amahera bugenda buragabanuka kandi igiciro c’itunga kigenda kiduga, kikaba kigenda kirushiriza kuba unobta. Ivyo biraboneka mu “Gishushanyo X” kiri aha hepfo. Uzobona itandukaniro rikomeye mu gushimira ivy’ubutunzi ugereranyije n’imishahara.


**Ibikorwa hakurikijwe umugwi w'umutungo**


| Asset Class         | Total Growth (Jan 2010 - Jan 2021) | Annualized Growth (Jan 2010 - Jan 2021) |
| ------------------- | ---------------------------------- | --------------------------------------- |
| Stock Market        | 236.84%                            | 11.67%                                  |
| Real Estate         | 66.38%                             | 4.74%                                   |
| Gold                | 73.10%                             | 5.11%                                   |
| Average Hourly Wage | 33.37%                             | 2.65%                                   |

Igishushanyo: Ibikorwa hakurikijwe umugwi w’itunga ([Itunga](Itunga](%5EGSPC/amateka/), [Itunga](ibiciro-vy’inzu-z’amateka/), [Inzahabu](Igiciro c’inzahabu/), [Imishahara](https://ubudandaji.com/leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika/imishahara.))


Kubera iyo nzira y’ugusubira inyuma kw’imishahara ku bici- ro vy’itunga, twabonye kimwe mu bihe bikomeye cane vy’uguhindura ubutunzi buva mu rwego rwo hasi buja mu rwego rwo hejuru mu mateka ya vuba .


![image](assets/2.webp)


Igishushanyo: Umugabane w'Igitigiri cose [Agaciro] (uruhererekane/WFRBSN40188#0.)


### Boom & Bust


Mu nzira y’ubudandaji isanzwe, y’isoko ry’uburenganzira, ukwaguka n’ugucika intege vyerekeye uburyo busubira inyuma bw’iterambere n’ugusubira inyuma mu bukungu burongowe n’inguvu z’isoko. Mu gihe c’ukwaguka, ubudandaji buratera imbere, amahera abaguzi bakoresha aragwira, kandi igikorwa c’ubutunzi muri rusangi kiragwira. Ico gice kirangwa cane cane n’ukwiyongera kw’ishoramari, ukwiyongera kw’akazi, n’inyungu nyinshi.


Ariko rero, ukwaguka kw’ubutunzi na kwo nyene kurimwo imbuto z’ugucika intege kwavyo bwite. Ibintu nk’ugushiramwo amahera birenze urugero, ugutera imbere kw’imyenda canke uguhinduka kw’inyiyumvo z’isoko birashobora gutuma ibikorwa vy’ubutunzi bigenda buhoro. Ico gihe c’ugucika intege, akenshi citwa ugusubira inyuma kw’ubutunzi canke ugusubira inyuma kw’ubutunzi, kirangwa no kugabanya amahera abaguzi bakoresha, inyungu z’ubudandaji zigabanuka, be n’ugutakaza akazi.


Amasezerano y’ubutunzi, naho ari urugamba, akora nk’inzira ikenewe yo gusukura, agatuma inyifato idafise inshingano n’abaremerewe n’imyenda babazwa ivyo bakora. Bituma haba ingorane z’amahera zituma abantu n’ubudandaji bashobora gukosora inyifato yabo canke bagahura n’ingaruka. Ukwo guhinduka kw’isoko n’ugusenyuka kw’isoko bitera imbere mu guhingura ibintu bishasha no gukura mu gihe c’ukwaguka no gukuraho ukutagira inshingano mu vy’ubutunzi mu gihe c’ugusenyuka.


Ariko rero, iyo nzira ishobora gushika neza gusa iyo inyungu zemerewe guhinduka mu mwidegemvyo bishingiye kuri Supply n’ivyo umuntu asaba. Woshobora kwibaza kubera iki? Inyungu zikora nk’ingero y’ingorane z’ubutunzi, zigaduga iyo ubusabe bw’imyenda burengeye umutungo uriho, zigaca zigabanuka iyo umutungo uri mwinshi ariko ubusabe ari buke.


Ikibabaje ni uko urutonde rwacu rw’ubu ruva kuri ico ciyumviro. Ingamba za banki nkuru zigamije gutuma ubutunzi buhungabana akenshi zigira ingaruka zitari izo umuntu yiteze. Gukoresha nabi inyungu birahungabanya ibimenyetso vy’isoko bimeze neza, bikaba bihungabanya ukuntu izo nzira zikora. Inyungu zihagaritswe mu buryo bw’ubuhinga ziremesha inguzanyo zirenze urugero n’ibibumbano vy’ibiharuro, mu gihe ugutera imbere bukwi na bukwi kw’inyungu kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kugenzura ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro bituma ubutunzi buhungabana kandi ubutunzi bukagenda buhoro.


Kubera ugukoresha nabi inyungu, ukwaguka kw’ubutunzi gukunda kumara igihe kirekire, bikaba bituma habaho ukwiyongera kw’imyenda n’ukutagira inshingano mu vy’ubutunzi. Ku rundi ruhande, uguhungabana kw’ubutunzi kurarushiriza gukomera, bigatuma abari hasi cane mu mibano barushiriza kugira ukudatekana n’ingorane.


### **Iciyumviro**


Inzira dufise ubu yo gufasha mu vy’amahera ntabwo iramba. Umuzigo w’imyenda uguma wiyongera, hamwe n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro kudasanzwe be n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro vy’ubuzima, biriko biratuma haba ubusumbasumbane bwinshi mu vy’ubutunzi be n’imivurungano mu kibano. Turashobora kwitega gusa ko izo ngorane zizorushiriza kuba mbi nitwabandanya muri iyo nzira.


Igishimishije ni uko hariho uburyo dushobora guhitamwo. Kubera ko Bitcoin yasohotse, ubu turafise ubushobozi bwo kuva mu buryo bwa kera bw’amahera y’amahera y’amahera, tukaja mu buryo bundi busubiza uburongozi mu minwe y’abanyagihugu. Uburyo bwa Bitcoin bushingiye ku rwego rwo hejuru kandi buboneka, buratanga uburyo bw’ivy’ubutunzi buringaniye kandi butekanye, butagira ubugenzuzi bw’amabanki nkuru na Leta. Ivyo bituma abantu ku giti cabo n’imiryango bashobora gukorana n’abandi mu mwidegemvyo mwinshi no mu kwizigira ata ngorane z’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro n’ubusumbasumbane bw’ubutunzi buterwa n’ingingo ngenderwako y’amahera ya kera. Kandi n’ama stablecoins, ababa mu ngorane nyinshi cane z’amahera barashobora kuva mu mafaranga yabo yo mu karere bitagoranye bakimukira mu kintu gikomeye cane, ni ukuvuga USD.


Uko tugenda turatera imbere, turaguhimiriza kwegera ubu buhinga bushasha ufise ubwenge bufunguye n’ijisho ry’uguca irya n’ino, ugatohoza ingene bushobora gutanga ubundi buryo bwo gusubirira uburyo bwacu bwo gukoresha amahera muri iki gihe. Mu kubigira, turafise ubushobozi bwo gutorera umuti ingorane z’ubusumbasumbane n’imivurungano biriko biraduga mu gihe twubaka kazoza k’ubutunzi karamba kandi buringaniye.


## Ivyigwa


<chapterId>f25c229f-2af0-5324-bc40-e90f7668985a</chapterId>


None ko mwaciye mu Module "Igiciro c'Iterambere" muzobwirizwa kugerageza ubumenyi mushasha muronka kugira ngo mumenye neza ko mwatahuye ibice vya nyuma. Tuzotangura n’Ibibazo vyinshi vyuguruye hanyuma dukore ikibazo gitoyi.


1. Rimbura ukuntu Bitcoin na stablecoins vyaje nk’uburyo bundi bwo gukoresha amafaranga y’agaciro. Ni ibiki wibaza ko ari bimwe mu vyiza n’ibibi bishobora gushika, kandi vyoshobora gute gutuma ubutunzi bugira uburinganire muri kazoza?

2. Ni amakuru ayahe woshobora gukusanya mu kigereranyo c’imyenda n’umusaruro w’igihugu ca Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika? Ni umwenda uwuhe ku GDP y’igihugu cawe bwite?

3. Guhagarika inyungu bigira ico bikoze gute ku muzigo w’imyenda yose?

4. Ni gute uburyo bw’amahera buriho ubu butuma ubusumbasumbane bw’ubutunzi bukomera kuruta?

5. Hakurikijwe amakuru yatanzwe ku bijanye n’imyenda n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro, wewe ubona iki ku bijanye n’ugukomera kw’uburyo bw’amahera buriho ubu? Woba wibaza ko urutonde rwacu rw’ubu ari ngirakamaro canke rugira nabi mu gihe kirekire?


# Ukwidegemvya mu vy'amahera - Intangamarara ya Bitcoin


<partId>c00843b2-bde3-57bb-ae2e-8ecad6631d71</partId>


## Abatsimvyi, Abahinguzi b’ibintu bishasha, n’Ishingiro rya Bitcoin


<chapterId>37d779ce-46b5-56d1-91d8-d04442236e35</chapterId>


Ikaze mu kiganiro ca kabiri, aho tuzokwihweza isi iryoshe cane ya Bitcoin. Dushingiye ku gutahura kwacu amateka y’amahera, iki kiganiro kizovuga ku ngingo zikurikira:



- Inkuru y'inyuma ya Bitcoin n'umuremyi
- Inyungu za Bitcoin nk'ifaranga ry'ubuhinga bwa none
- Itandukaniro hagati ya Bitcoin umutungo na Bitcoin urubuga
- Uko wokorana na Bitcoin n'ibice vyayo bitandukanye


Mu mpera z’iki kiganiro, uzoba ufise ugutahura gukomeye kw’inkomoko ya Bitcoin, ibiranga be n’ingene ishobora gukoreshwa. Ariko imbere y’uko twisuka mu bigoranye vya Bitcoin, reka tubanze twihweze amateka y’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none yateguye inzira y’ubu buhinga buriko burahindura ingene twiyumvira amahera.


### Ico kintu citwa Bitcoin ni ikihe


Bitcoin ni Trustless kandi ni amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none yegerejwe ata ruhusha. Ivyo vyoshobora kumvikana nk’ibiteye urujijo, reka rero tubisigure. Kubera ko ata leta canke ikigo kigenzura Bitcoin, ntubwirizwa kwizigira uwundi muntu canke ngo usabe uruhusha rwo kuyikoresha. Ahubwo, ibungabungwa n'urubuga rw'abakoresha kw'isi yose bemeza kandi bagakora ibikorwa vy'ubudandaji ku kintu citwa Blockchain.


Iyumvire Blockchain nk’igikoresho kinini cane citwa Ledger canke urupapuro rwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none rufise amakuru y’ibintu vyose umuntu akora biciye kuri Bitcoin. Nk’uko umuntu wese kw’isi yose afise internet ashobora gukurikirana, kwemeza canke gukora amafaranga, ivyo bituma amafaranga agira umutekano kandi adashobora kwigana.


Bitcoin nayo ni iyo kwihariza kuko ifise Supply igabanutse. Bitcoin imiliyoni 21 gusa ni zo zizokwigera ziremwa, ivyo bikaba bituma zigira ubukene, nk’inzahabu n’ibindi vyuma vy’agaciro. Ukwo kubura ni kimwe mu bituma Bitcoin igira agaciro.


Ica nyuma, kandi gihambaye kuruta ibindi vyose, kubera ko ikora yigenga kuri Leta canke amabanki. Bitcoin ishoboza abantu guha agaciro Exchange n’abandi ataco baciye, nk’uko nyene bigenda ku mafaranga. Ariko rero, bitandukanye n’amahera, Bitcoin irashobora gukoreshwa mu kugura ibintu n’ibikorwa ku rubuga, ata kwizigira uburyo bwa kera bwo kwishura. Ivyo bisigura ko kubera ubuhinga bwayo bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none, Bitcoin ikuraho ivy’ugukenera abahuza, amafaranga y’amahera n’ibiceri, bigatuma ugucuruza vyoroha, vyihuta kandi bikaba bitekanye.


Ku ncuro ya mbere mu kiringo kirekire, Bitcoin igereranya uburyo bushasha bwo kwiyumvira ibijanye n’amahera n’agaciro. Ni co gituma dufise umunezero wo kubajana mu mwobo w’inkwavu turi kumwe.


### Abatsimvyi b'amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none


Imbere y’uko Bitcoin iremwa, abantu bakeyi bafise iyerekwa barashizeho umushinge wa Bitcoin uko biyumvira isi aho amahera yoshobora guhererezwa biciye ku buhinga bwa none ata n’umwe ayihuza. Abo bantu batazi baragize uruhara runini mu gutegura Bitcoin, kuko iyo batagira intererano zabo mu bijanye n’ugukora amakuru y’ibanga, ntiyari kubaho uno musi. Mu bamenyekana cane muri abo batsimvyi harimwo:


#### Aba Cypherpunks


Aba Cypherpunks ni umugwi w’abagarariji bazi ivy’ubuhinga bwa none baje hamwe mu myaka ya 80 kugira ngo barwanire umwidegemvyo w’umuntu ku giti ciwe n’uw’abanyagihugu bakoresheje igikoresho kimwe gikomeye: ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru. Bemera yuko ubushobozi bwo gupfuka amakuru bwoha abantu ububasha bwo gusubira kugenzura ubutegetsi bushingiye ku butegetsi. Ibaze ko woshobora kuguma uvugana n’abandi kuri internet mu mwiherero kandi ukaba ukingiye amaso y’abantu - ivyo ni vyo bariko barwanira!


Kimwe mu bintu bihambaye cane vyavuye mu bikorwa vya Cypherpunks ni urutonde rw’abantu barungika ubutumwa, rwashinzwe mu 1992. Biciye kuri urwo rutonde, abantu bashobora gusangira ivyiyumviro no kuganira ku buhinga bwo gukora amakuru y’ibanga, ivyiyumviro vy’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none, n’imigambi yibanda ku buzima bwite. Ivyo vyatumye habaho umuryango w’abantu bafise ivyiyumviro nk’ivyabo, harimwo abategura ibintu, abaharanira uburenganzira bw’abantu n’abashakashatsi.


Muri iki gihe, ivyiyumviro vy’iyerekwa vy’aba cypherpunks birabandanya guhingura iterambere ry’ubuhinga bwa none, bikaba biha abantu ububasha bwo kugenzura cane amakuru yabo n’ivy’itumanaho. Imwe mu nzira zabo zihambaye cane ni Bitcoin, kuko ikomoka cane kuri Hashcash— ubuhinga bwateguwe na Cypherpunk Adam Mu 1997 kugira ngo barwanye ubutumwa butari bwo bwo kuri email.


Abandi ba Cypherpunks bazwi cane ni:



- Timothy May:** Yashinze urutonde rw’abarungika ubutumwa rwa Cypherpunks kandi yanditse cane ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru n’ubuzima bwite mu myaka yose ya 90 no mu ntango z’imyaka ya 2000. Ivyo yanditse vyashizeho umushinge w’ibiganiro ku bijanye n’ubuzima bwite bw’abantu ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bwa none be n’uburyo bwo gutanga amahera mu buhinga bwa none.
- Eric Huges:** Uwundi muntu yashinze umurwi Cypherpunks akaba n'umwanditsi w'igitabu "A Cypherpunk's Manifesto," cashimikiye cane ku kamaro k'ubuzima bwite n'ukutamenyekana mu gihe c'ubuhinga bwa none.
- Whitfield Diffie na Martin Hellman:** Bateye imbere iciyumviro co gukoresha ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru y’urufunguzo rwa bose, bihindura cane uburyo bwo guhanahana amakuru kuri internet butekanye.
- Julian Assange:** Yashinze ishirahamwe WikiLeaks, ritanga amakuru y’ibanga kandi y’agaciro kugira ngo habeho uguseruka no gutanga amakuru.
- Bram Cohen:** Yaremye BitTorrent, ubuhinga bwo gusangira amadosiye n’abandi bwatumye ibirimwo bikwiragizwa ahantu hamwe kandi bikaba vyatuma umuntu ashobora kubikuramwo vyihuta.
- John Gilmore:** Umudandaza akaba n’umunyagihugu w’umunyagihugu yashinze ishirahamwe ry’ubuhinga bwa none (EFF) kandi akaburanira uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none n’ubuzima bwite bwo kuri internet.


...kandi urutonde rurabandanya.


#### David Chaum (Se w'amahera y'ubuhinga bwa none)


Mu ntango z'imyaka ya 1980, David Chaum yarahinduye isi y'amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none n'igikorwa ciwe c'ubuhinga bwa none ku "mikono ya blinded." Ivyo vyatuma umuntu ashobora gusinya ubutumwa mu buryo bw’ibanga atazi ibirimwo, ivyo bikaba vyatuma haba ubuzima bwite n’umutekano mu bikorwa vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Mu mwaka w’1982, David Chaum yarashizeho iciyumviro ca Ecash, ubuhinga bwo gukoresha amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none butazwi, bukoresha ubuhinga bwa cryptography, bwaje gushirwa mu ngiro biciye mu kigo ciwe Digicash.


Naho Digicash yakoreshwa nk’uburyo bwo kwishura amahera make muri banki imwe yo muri Amerika kuva mu 1995 gushika mu 1998, Chaum yaje gusaba gusenyuka. Ivyo bivuzwe, ivyiyumviro vyiwe bishasha vyatumye abandi bashakashaka amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none, bica bituma habaho iterambere ry’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none, nka Bitcoin.


#### E-inzahabu


Bakurikije inzira ya Chaum, mu mwaka w’1996, abahinga babiri, Douglas Jackson na Barry Downey, barashizeho E-gold, ifaranga rya mbere ryakoreshejwe cane ry’ubuhinga bwa none, rituma abakoresha bashobora gutanga inzahabu Ownership biciye ku buhinga bwa none. Ico ciyumviro carakunzwe cane kandi carakwegereye abantu amamiliyoni babonye ubushobozi bw’ubwo buryo budasanzwe bw’amahera. Hakoreshejwe E-gold, abantu barashobora gutanga amahera mu buryo bworoshe kandi bwihuse bajabuka imipaka ataco bakoze ku buryo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki bugenda buhoro kandi bugoye.


Ariko nk’uko bigenda ku buhinga bushasha bwose, E-gold yarahuye n’ingorane z’amategeko be n’ibibazo bijanye n’ibikorwa bitemewe n’amategeko nk’ugukoresha nabi amahera n’ubuhendanyi. Ivyo vyatumye iyo sosiyete itegekwa guhagarika ibikorwa vyayo, ivyo bikaba vyatumye habaho ugutera imbere kw’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none.


Naho nyene yananiwe, E-gold yari intambwe ihambaye mu gutera imbere kw’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none. Ivyigwa vyakuwe mu vyo E-gold yaciyemwo vyatanze ikarita y’inzira ku bazokora ibintu bishasha mu gihe kizoza ku ngorane z’amategeko n’ivy’umutekano vya Address.


Kubera ko Bitcoin yateye imbere cane, abantu benshi bihenda ko ari yo mafaranga ya mbere y’ubuhinga bwa none yabayeho. Ariko rero, nk’uko ubu bigaragara, ivyo vyiyumviro biri kure y’ukuri. Bitcoin yaje kubera ubushakashatsi n’igerageza ry’imyaka mirongo ryakozwe n’abatsimvyi mu vy’ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru. Iyo hataba intererano z’abantu bari hejuru n’abandi benshi, Bitcoin yoshobora kuba itarigeze iremwa. Naho ayo mafaranga ya kera y’ubuhinga bwa none yaje gutsindwa, Bitcoin yarize ku makosa yayo, amaherezo iba amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none tuzi uno musi.


Ivyo bivuzwe, iyo hataba umuntu umwe... canke umugwi (ntituzi neza), Bitcoin ntiyari kubaho. Kandi uwo ni Satoshi Nakamoto. Umuremyi w’amayobera.


#### Satoshi Nakamoto


Naho Bitcoin yafashe ubwenge bw’abantu amamiliyoni n’ubushobozi bwayo bwo guhungabanya abantu be n’ubuhinga bwayo budasanzwe, naho izwi cane, inkomoko yayo y’akabanga irabandanya gushimisha abantu no kubabaza. Satoshi Nakamoto, uwaremye Bitcoin, n’ubu ntamenyekana, naho nyene hari abantu benshi bagerageje kumenya uwo ari we vy’ukuri. Naho haciye imyaka irenga cumi Bitcoin ivutse, n’ubu ntituri hafi yo gutorera umuti ikibazo kigira kiti: Satoshi Nakamoto ni nde? Ariko none, kubera ukuntu Bitcoin ikoreshwa n’abantu benshi, vyoba vy’ukuri bifise akamaro?


Uko biri kwose, reka turabe inkuru z’imigani n’imigani.


Satoshi Nakamoto yasohotse kuri internet mu 2008 afise iciyumviro gishasha: amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none y’urunganwe. Yasangije iyerekwa ryiwe mu [mpapuro z'impapuro icenda](https://Bitcoin.org/Bitcoin.pdf) zitwa "Bitcoin: Uburyo bwo gukoresha amahera y'ubuhinga bwa none" n'urutonde rw'abarungika ubutumwa rwa Cypherpunk. Naho mu ntango benshi mu bagize urutonde rw'abarungika ubutumwa batavyishimiye, ico ciyumviro caratumye umunyamuryango umwe, Hal Finney, agira amatsiko ahagije, amaherezo ashikira Satoshi. Ukwifatanya kwa Hal mu gutegura Bitcoin kwagaragaye ko ari ihinduka rikomeye, bituma abantu benshi batanga infashanyo yabo.


Ariko rero, inyuma y'imyaka ibiri akora kuri uwo mugambi, Satoshi yarazimiye ata n'akarongo, n'[itangazo ryiwe rya nyuma ry'ukuri] (https://plan99.net/~mike/Satoshi-emails/thread5.html) ku wa 23 Ndamukiza 2011, aho yavuze ko "yimukiye mu bindi bintu."


Ukuzimira kw’akabanga kwa Satoshi Nakamoto kwatumye habaho ivyiyumviro bitandukanye ku bijanye n’aho yagiye. Bamwebamwe biyumvira ko yumvise ko yarashitse ku co yari yiyemeje gukora, abandi na bo bemera ko yacitse intege kubera abantu bariko baramwitaho Bitcoin. Mu kwezi kwa kigarama [2010](2010), igihe WikiLeaks yabujijwe gukoresha uburyo bwa kera bwo kwishura, G11. Ivyiyumviro vya Satoshi ku bijanye n’uko abantu barushiriza kwitwararika Bitcoin be n’ingaruka zishobora guterwa n’amategeko yo kurema amafaranga akoreshwa mu guhungabanya inyungu za Amerika mu vy’ubuhinga bw’isi, bishobora kuba vyatumye asubira inyuma. Canke rero, yoba yarahinduye ivyiyumviro vyiwe akabishira ku yindi migambi, yoba agitanga intererano kuri Bitcoin mu yandi mazina, canke mbere akaba yarapfuye.


Naho twoba tutazi uwo Satoshi ari we, turafise ishusho itomoye y’imigambi yiwe inyuma ya Bitcoin. Yaremye Bitcoin nk’inyishu y’ingorane z’ivy’ubutunzi kw’isi yose mu 2008 n’ukutagira icizigiro kwavuyemwo ku bijanye n’uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki n’amahera agenzurwa na Leta.


Mu biganiro vyiwe vyo kuri internet, yaseruye ukuntu afise ivyiyumviro bitari vyo ku bijanye n’uko amahera n’amabanki bihuriye hamwe, agaragaza akaga ko kwizigira amabanki akomeye ko atazogabanya agaciro k’amahera yabo. Iciyumviro, canditswe mu gice ca mbere ca Bitcoin, ni:


"Ikinyamakuru Times 03/Jan/2009 Umukuru w'igihugu ari ku ruhande rwo gufasha amabanki ubwa kabiri."


Ivyo ni ibivugwa mu kinyamakuru Times [ingingo](https://www.thetimes.co.uk/ingingo/cancellor-alistair-darling-ari-ku ruhande-rw’ugufasha-amabanki-n91382mn62h), yerekana ivyiyumviro vyiwe vy’uko amabanki yoba ariko aragira ingaruka zitari nke, zishobora kuba zifise ingorane. gusangira n’abafise amafaranga.

Ikindi kandi, turazi mu butumwa bwiwe bwa vuba cane ko Satoshi atemeranya n’ingene ubuhinga bwacu bw’amahera bukora ubu:


"Ikibazo nyamukuru c'amafaranga asanzwe ni ukwizigira kwose gukenewe kugira ngo akore. Banki nkuru itegerezwa kwizigirwa kugira ngo ntiyigere igabanya amafaranga, ariko amateka y'amafaranga y'ubuhinga yuzuyemwo ukurenga kuri ukwo kwizigira."


Naho uruyeri rwa Satoshi rwongera uruyeri ku mateka ya Bitcoin, hari ikintu kimwe tudashobora guharirako. Ingingo ya Satoshi yo kuguma atamenyekana irashimika ku ngingo ngenderwako nyamukuru zo kwegereza ubutegetsi abaturage n’umwidegemvyo w’umuntu ku giti ciwe zishigikira umugambi wa Bitcoin. Kuba Satoshi itamenyekana bituma umuntu aguma yibanda ku buhinga n’ingaruka bushobora kugira aho kwibanda ku gusenga umuntu.


**Iciyumviro**


Mu ncamake, Bitcoin yarahinduye cane uburyo twiyumvira ku bijanye n’amahera n’agaciro. Ku ncuro ya mbere muri kahise, dufise amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none ari yo:



- Peer-to-Peer:** Bitcoin iremesha abantu ku giti cabo kohereza no kwakira amahera ataco bakeneye abahuza, nk’amabanki canke abajejwe amahera.
- Decentralized:** Bitcoin ikorera ku rubuga rwegerejwe, bisobanura ko ata butegetsi buhambaye canke ubugenzuzi ku mafaranga.
- Secure:** Amafaranga y’ama Bitcoin arakingirwa hakoreshejwe ubuhinga bwo gukingira, ivyo bikaba bituma kwigana canke ibiceri vya Double-spending bigorana.
- Limited in Supply & Divisible:** Supply ya Bitcoin irafise aho igarukira—ifise ibiceri vy’amamiliyoni 21 gusa biriho—mu gihe muri ico gihe nyene, ishobora kugabanywa mu bice umunani vy’icumi, bikaba bishoboka ko umuntu ashobora gukoresha agace k’isenti. Ukwo kubura ni ugutanga agaciro k’amahera no gukingira inflation.
- Psuedoanonymous:** Naho amafaranga Bitcoin atamenyekana rwose, atanga urugero rw’ubuzima bwite n’izina ry’ikinyoma uburyo bwo kwishura bwa kera butatanga.


Ivyo vyose hamwe bisigura ko Bitcoin iha umuntu wese ubuzima bwite bw’amahera, umutekano n’ubushobozi bwo gukorana kw’isi yose ata mahera menshi n’ugushikirana. Mu mpera, Bitcoin ni igikoresho gikomeye ku barondera umwidegemvyo mwinshi mu vy’ubutunzi no kwigenga. Ivyo birahindura urukino ku barondera uburyo bwo kuzigama butekanye, reka tuvuge ababaho mu ntwaro z’agahomerabunwa, abashikirwa n’ugutera imbere kw’ubutunzi, abahunga ibihugu vyasambuwe n’intambara, canke abasubiza amahera ababo bari mu mahanga. Kubera ko Bitcoin itanga uburyo bushoboka bwo guhindura amahera mu buryo bwa kera, ivyo bisiga amahera menshi mu maboko y’abayakeneye cane. Umuntu wese afise Bitcoin, arashobora kuba banki yiwe bwite, akagenzura kazoza kiwe k’ivy’ubutunzi.


Kugira ngo dusoze, ata kuraba uwo Satoshi Nakamoto ari we, nta gukeka ko uguhingura Bitcoin kwatumye haba uburyo bushasha bwo kwiyumvira ku bijanye no kwimurira agaciro.


## Bitcoin ikora gute? Ibikorwa vyo mu mutima vy'aya mahera y'amageza yo kuri Internet


<chapterId>b0f736fc-ed4d-5887-b22e-d958db9144d1</chapterId>


Bitcoin akenshi yitwa amahera y’amageza ya internet... kandi kubera imvo nziza. Iyumvire – ukoresheje Bitcoin, urashobora kohereza agaciro umuntu wese, aho ari ho hose kw’isi, ata muntu wo hagati ukeneye nka banki canke leta. Ni nk’aho woba ufise ububasha ku banki yawe bwite, ububasha bwo kohereza amahera hanze y’imipaka ukoresheje gukanda buto bukeyi gusa.


Kubera inyungu nyinshi Bitcoin ifise, kuva ku gutanga uburyo bwihuta, butekanye kandi buzimvye bwo gukorana n’abandi gushika ku kwemerera abantu kwigenzura mu vy’ubutunzi bwabo bwite ata nkenerwa y’ubutegetsi bumwe, ushizwmwo n’intambamyi zikomeye z’ubuhinga bwa none zategerezwa gutorera umuti kugira ngo zibe nk’iz’ubuhinga bwa none. imikorere yayo ni ikintu abantu bakeyi gusa bategerezwa gutahura. Ushobora mbere kwumva uteye ubwoba gatoyi n’iciyumviro c’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none yegerejwe abantu bose. Ariko ukuri ni uko Bitcoin mu vy’ukuri yoroshe cane iyo umaze gutahura ingene ikora mu mutima.


Muri iki gice, turaza kwihweza neza abakinyi b’ingenzi mu bidukikije vya Bitcoin n’ingene bakorana kugira ngo ayo mahera y’amageza ya internet akore.


Reka dutangure!


Nk’uko vyavuzwe mu ntangamarara y’iki kiganiro, Bitcoin ni ikintu kidasanzwe kuko dufise amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none akora neza, akoreshwa cane, akoreshwa n’abantu benshi, ari bwo bwa mbere muri kahise. Ivyo bisigura ko aho kwizigira ubuyobozi bukuru nka banki canke Leta kugira ngo burongore amafaranga, burongorwa n’uruja n’uruza rw’abafatanyabikorwa bakorana. Ubwo buryo bushasha buratuma dushobora gukorana n’abandi ata n’umwe akeneye abahuza.


Iyo ugereranyije n’uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki, naho Bitcoin ikora mu buryo butandukanye, uruhara itegerezwa gukora nta ho rutandukanye. Nk’akarorero, amabanki yose na Bitcoin ategerezwa:


1. kwemeza no gukora amafaranga,

2. gukurikirana ibikorwa kugira ngo ntihagire ubuhendanyi canke inyifato mbi,

3. kumenya ko vyose biri ku gihe, bikora neza kandi bifise umutekano.


Naho amabanki akora izo nshingano mu nzu, akayiha ububasha bwose ku bijanye n’ingene ivyo bikorwa bigenda, Bitcoin isaba ubufatanye bw’abanyagihugu kugira ngo bashobore gukora izo nshingano.
