Mu yandi majambo, kugira ngo Bitcoin ishobore gusubiramwo izo nzira mu buryo bwegerejwe, Bitcoin itegerezwa gutanga igikorwa cose muri ivyo kugira ngo ntihagire umuntu canke ikigo kimwe gifise ububasha burengeye ubw’abandi ku bijanye n’urwo rutonde.


Kugira ngo ivyo bikorwa bishoboke, Bitcoin yaciyemwo izo nshingano zitatu z’ingenzi: ama node, abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro n’abategura amabuye y’agaciro. Aho ama node agenzura ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji kandi agashiraho amategeko kandi agashira mu ngiro, abacukuzi barategeka kandi bakemeza ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji, abahinguzi na bo bagatuma urubuga ruguma rujanye n’igihe kandi bagatanga ivyiyumviro vyo guhindura. Mu gutanga izo nshingano muri abo bafatanyabikorwa b’ingenzi, Bitcoin yararemye uburyo butekanye, buboneye, kandi bushobora kubazwa abakoresha bose.


Reka rero, turabe umwe wese muri izo nshingano...


### Uruhara rwa Bitcoin


#### Uturongo


Nodes ni ngirakamaro ku butungane n’umutekano w’urubuga rwa Bitcoin. Bakora nk’abacungera amarembo y’urwo rutonde, bagakora vyose kugira ngo amafaranga akoreshwa neza kandi akurikije amategeko. Buri node irakura kandi ikagenzura mu karere kopi yuzuye ya Blockchain, iyo na yo ikaba ari Ledger y’ubuhinga bwa none yandika amafaranga yose yigeze gukorwa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin. Biciye mu kwumvikana, ama node yemeranya ku vyerekeye ukuri kw’isoko ryose kandi akabona ko amategeko ariko arakurikizwa. Ivyo bisigura ko izo node zizokwanka iyo nzira iyo umuntu agerageje guhenda iyo sisitemu, nk’akarorero. mu kurungika ama Bitcoin menshi kuruta ayo bafise mu vy’ukuri canke mu kugerageza gukoresha ayo Bitcoin nyene incuro zibiri.


Kugira ngo turushirize gusobanura neza ico ciyumviro c’uguhurizako, iyo abahinguzi basavye guhindura canke guhindura Bitcoin, amanode aragira uruhara mu kwemera canke kwanka ayo mahinduka. Ivyo babigira mu guhindura porogarama yabo ikaja kuri verisiyo nshasha canke mu kubandanya bakoresha verisiyo ya kera. Ivyo bikorwa akenshi birimwo ibiganiro n’impaka mu muryango wa Bitcoin kugira ngo haboneke ukwiyumvikana. Ivyo bivuzwe, ivyiyumviro vya Bitcoin si ivy’umwirabura n’umweru nk’imashini yo gutora. Abenshi ntibatwara vy’ukuri. Iyo abantu bamwebamwe batemeranya n’iryo hinduka, barashobora gutanguza token nshasha ikomoka kuri Bitcoin. Ubu, Bitcoin y’intango iriho ata mpinduka kandi nshasha iriho ihinduka. Biciye mu kugura no kugurisha, ni abarundi bose bashira ahabona verisiyo babona ko ari yo ifise agaciro kuruta. Ubwo buryo bwo kwumvikana buratuma amahinduka yose akorwa ku masezerano ya Bitcoin yemeranwa n’abanyagihugu bose, bikaba bigora umuntu canke umugwi uwo ari wo wose gukoresha iyo nzira kugira ngo yironkere inyungu.


Ni vyiza kandi kumenya ko node ari igice gusa c’ubuhinga umuntu wese ashobora gukoresha kuri mudasobwa yiwe yo muhira. Igisabwa conyene ni ugukoresha internet kandi, bivanye n’ingene wipfuza kubika Blockchain, ahantu hose kuva kuri 5 gushika kuri 500gb y’ahantu h’ubuntu.


#### Abacukuzi b'amabuye y'agaciro


Ku rundi ruhande, abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro ba Bitcoin barafise uruhara runini mu kubika amakuru, kuko ari bo bajejwe gusaba no kwemeza amafaranga. Kugira ngo ivyo babikore, abacukuzi barakoresha orodinateri zidasanzwe kugira ngo bakore igikorwa citwa hashing. Ata kwisuka mu nitty gritty y’ugukora hashing, wiyumvire nk’abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro bariko barahiganwa kugira ngo bongereko amafaranga mashasha kuri Blockchain, Ledger ya bose y’amafaranga. Mu Exchange kubera igikorwa cabo, abacukuzi barahembwa Bitcoin nshasha yaremwe n’amahera y’ugucuruza ku bikorwa vyose vyakozwe. Ivyo bikoresho vya Mining vyateguwe kugira ngo bibe bigoye, bibe bishobora guhangana n’ibindi, kandi bikaba bikoreshwa mu buryo bw’impfagusa, hakaba hariho gusa umubare mutoyi w’ibitabu bishasha bisohoka buri mwaka, bikaba bituma Supply ya Bitcoin igira aho igarukira kandi agaciro kayo kakagumaho. Iyo abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro batabaho, amafaranga ntiyari gukorwa.


Kubera ko abacukuzi bategerezwa guhiganwa kugira ngo bashobore gukora ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji kandi bagahembwa kubera ivyo, iryo higanwa rigabanya amahirwe y’uko Miner canke ikigo cose coshobora kugenzura urubuga kandi rikavyura abacukuzi gukora ata buryarya no gukurikiza amategeko. Iyo umukinyi wa Miner agerageje guhenda canke kurenga ku mategeko, barashobora gutakaza impembo yabo, rero hariho ikintu gikomeye kivyura umutima wo gukina bisunze amategeko.


#### Abategura


Abahinguzi ni abahinga cane kandi bubaha cane bo mu muryango wa Bitcoin bakorana kugira ngo urubuga rugume rutekanye, rwizigirwa kandi rujanye n’igihe. Bifise uruhara runini mu bidukikije vya Bitcoin mu kubungabunga no kunoza porogarama ziha ubushobozi iyo nzira. Bajejwe gutanga ivyiyumviro no gushirwa mu ngiro amahinduka mu rutonde rw’amakode rwa Bitcoin, gukosora ibibazo, no gutuma ibikorwa n’umutekano bigenda neza.


Iyo hataba abayiteguye, urubuga rwa Bitcoin ntirwoshobora gutera imbere no guhura n’ibintu bihinduka. Bajejwe gutuma iyo nzira igumaho mu kiringo kirekire no kumenya ko iguma ari uburyo bwo kwishura bwizigiwe kandi bushizwe ahantu hamwe mu myaka izoza. Muri make, abahinguzi ni bo mugongo w’ibidukikije vya Bitcoin, baguma bakora kugira ngo batere imbere ubuhinga bushingiye ku rubuga no kugira ngo rubandanye kuroranirwa.


Ubwa nyuma, hariho n’uruhara rumwe twipfuza gushira ahabona: umuryango, ni wo uha Bitcoin agaciro kayo. Umuryango ugizwe n'umuntu wese akoresha urubuga, akora ibikorwa vy'ubudandaji, kandi agatera intege abacukuzi b'amabuye y'agaciro, n'abahinguzi kugira ngo babandanye bakora kuri Bitcoin. Uko umuryango ukura, ni ko n’agaciro k’urubuga rwa Bitcoin gakura.


_**Iciyumviro co ku ruhande:** Ni vyiza gushimika ku vy’uko kamere ya Bitcoin yegerejwe abantu bose ituma umuntu wese, ataravye aho akomoka canke ikibanza afise, ashobora kugira uruhara muri iyo nzira no gufata uruhara urwo ari rwo rwose rukenewe kugira ngo ikore. Ivyo bitandukanya Bitcoin n’amahera ya kera, akenshi agenzurwa n’amabanki nkuru canke intwaro. Mu yandi majambo, Bitcoin isubiza ububasha abantu mu kubashoboza kuba abagira uruhara n'umwete mu rubuga aho kuba abaguzi b'uburyo buhurikiye hamwe._


### Ibikorwa kuva mu ntango gushika mu mpera


Kugira ngo dutahure ingene abo bakinyi bose bakorana, reka twiyumvire igikorwa coroshe co gucuruza Bitcoin hagati y’abantu babiri, Alice na Bob. Alice ishaka kohereza Bob igice kimwe c’igihumbi c’i Bitcoin, hafi \$29 mu gihe c’ukwandika.


#### Gutangura ubucuruzi


Igikorwa cose ca Bitcoin gitangura n'ugutangura kwaco igihe uwurungitse, muri iki gihe, Alice, akora igikorwa kigaragaza uwugihabwa, Bob, n'umubare, 0.00100000 Bitcoin. Ico gice gifatanye n’ico gice ca Alice ca Wallet gica kimenyesha iyo nzira ku rubuga, aho izo nzira zemeza ko ari ukuri, hanyuma kigarungikwa ku bacukuzi kugira ngo bavyemeze.


Muri iki gihe, iyo nzira yinjira mu kizwi nka Mempool, mu vy’ukuri ni icumba co kurindiriramwo amafaranga yiteguriye kwongerwa kuri Blockchain. Wiyumvire ko ari urutonde rw’ibintu bitegerezwa gukorwa, nk’ivyo ubona ku mpapuro z’ikarata yawe y’inguzanyo, vyatanguye ariko birindiriye gukorwa. Iryo soko rimaze gutangura kandi ryicaye muri Mempool, ubu riri mu maboko y’abacukuzi.


#### Kwemeza ubucuruzi


Abacukuzi ubu bafata ivyo bikorwa vyari bitegerejwe, bakabishira mu gice gishasha, maze bagahiganwa kugira ngo bakore igikorwa kinaka cashizweho na porogarama ishigikiye Bitcoin. Uwutsinze amarushanwa aca yongerako igice ciwe n’amahera yashizwemwo kuri Blockchain, agaheza ayo mahera. Uwutsinda arahezagirwa kandi n’igitabu gishasha ca Bitcoin be n’amahera ajanye n’ivyo akora, ivyo bikaba bimutera intege zo kubandanya akora ivyo akora.


#### Kwemeza ubucuruzi


Igihe iyo nzira yemejwe, Bob ubu akwiye kubona 0.00100000 Bitcoin muri Wallet yiwe. Ariko ntibihagarara aho. Ivyo bihimba bica bisuzuma ko Miner yakoze neza igikorwa cavyo be n’uko amafaranga ashizwe muri iyo nzira nshasha ahuye n’amategeko yemeranijwe n’ivyo bihimba. Iyo iyo block inaniwe kubigira, rero iyo block nshasha izokwangwa, maze Miner izotakaza impembo yabo ya Mining.


_**Ikintu giteye umunezero:** Naho inyuma y’aho igikorwa ca Bitcoin cemejwe, ubushobozi bwo guhindura burahari iyo ama node yanse ama blocs. Ariko rero, uko igice gishasha congerewe kuri Blockchain inyuma y’ugucuruza, ubushobozi bwo gusubira inyuma buragabanuka cane. Kugira ngo umuntu agire umutekano mwinshi, amabarabara n’amasakoshi akenshi ashira ahantu kuri Bitcoin yawe gushika hashizweko amabuye menshi akurikira—akenshi ni atatu gushika ku atandatu. Ivyo bikingira amahera kandi bikaba bituma umuntu agira amahoro yo mu mutima._


**Iciyumviro**


Nk’uko vyasiguwe muri iki gice cose, naho Bitcoin ishobora gusa n’uburyo bugoranye bwo gukingira amakuru munsi y’igipfukisho, ni ugukorana gusa hagati y’inshingano zitatu z’ingenzi n’abanyagihugu.



- Nodes, biciye mu kwemeza ibikorwa, zituma urubuga rugira ubutungane n’umutekano mu gukora nk’abacungera amarembo.
- Abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro ni bo bajejwe gusaba no kwemeza amafaranga.
- Abahinguzi ni abantu b’abahinga cane bo mu muryango wa Bitcoin bakorana kugira ngo babungabunge kandi batere imbere porogarama ziha ubushobozi urubuga.
- Umuryango, biciye mu gukoresha Bitcoin, ni wo uyiha agaciro.


Imwe muri izo nshingano ni ngirakamaro kugira ngo Bitcoin ikore neza kandi iroranirwe nk’ifaranga ry’ubuhinga bwa none. Mu kwemera ivyo bikorwa bihambaye abakinyi b’ingenzi, Bitcoin irashobora gukora nk’uburyo butekanye, buboneye, kandi bufise inshingano ku bakoresha bose ba Exchange, bikaba bituma iba ikintu gihambaye mu mateka y’amahera.


## Ni igiki gituma Bitcoin itandukanye na Fiat?


<chapterId>5ef55778-cbcf-5c7e-960d-a2fcdf1a4006</chapterId>


Mu gice ca mbere, twarihweje cane imikorere yihariye ya Bitcoin iyitandukanya n’amafaranga y’agaciro n’ingene Bitcoin ishika ku kimenyetso cipfuzwa co kuba igisata c’abanyagihugu. None, reka duhindure ivyiyumviro vyacu maze turabe ingene Bitcoin itandukanye na fiat mu bijanye n’ibiranga bituma ifaranga rikomeye. Mu gusuzuma ivyo bintu nyamukuru ni ho gusa dushobora gutahura neza igituma Bitcoin ari iyo kwihariza kandi iri mw’isi yiwe bwite ku bijanye n’amahera.


Niba mwibuka mu Gice ca mbere, twaravye ibikorwa n’ibiranga amahera, ivyo bikaba ari:


**Ibibiko vy'agaciro:** Bigumya ubushobozi bwo kugura mu gihe.



- _Iramba:_ Ishobora guhangana n’ugusambuka.
- _Bike:_ Bifise aho bigarukira mu bwinshi.
- _Ibidahinduka:_ Ntibishobora guhindurwa canke guhindurwa.


**Igikoresho ca Exchange:** Gikoreshwa nk’uburyo bwo gucuruza ibintu n’ibikorwa.



- _Portable:_ Biroroshe gutwara canke gutwara.
- _Divisible:_ Bishobora guca mu bice bitobito.
- _Yemewe:_ Yemewe cane kandi yemewe nk’uburyo bwo kwishura.


**Igice ca Konti:** Gikoreshwa mu gupima agaciro.



- _Fungible:_ Ishobora guhindurwa n’ibindi bice vy’ubwoko bumwe.


Reka noneho dusuzume fiat na Bitcoin biciye mu nzira y’ivyo bikorwa n’ibiranga kugira ngo dutahure neza ingene bitandukanye.


#### Ububiko bw'agaciro


Naho amafaranga y’amafiat ashobora gushikirwa n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro kandi mu mateka yerekanye ko atakaza agaciro uko igihe kigenda kirarenga kubera politike za Leta, Bitcoin ifise impera Supply n’uko ifise ububiko bukomeye bw’agaciro budashobora gukoreshwa n’ubutegetsi ubwo ari bwo bwose bwo hagati. Igituma Bitcoin iba ububiko bukomeye bw’agaciro ni uko ari:



- Iramba:** Bitcoin ni digitale kandi, rero, ntishobora kwonona canke ngo ibore nk’amahera y’impapuro canke y’ivyuma. Ikindi kandi, kamere yayo yegerejwe bituma ata n’aho ishobora gutera.
- Scarce:** Supply ya Bitcoin igabanywa cane n’ibiceri vy’imiliyoni 21, ivyo bikaba bituma iba nke cane ugereranije n’amahera y’amahera, ayo intwaro zishobora gucapura ata mpera. Iyi Supply ifise aho igarukira bisigura ko agaciro ka Bitcoin kadashikirwa n’ingorane z’ugutera imbere nk’amafaranga y’amahera.
- Immutable:** Ubuhinga bwa Bitcoin bwa Blockchain buratuma iyo amafaranga yanditswe ku rubuga, adashobora guhindurwa canke guhindurwa. Uwo murongo wo kudahinduka ntushoboka ku mafaranga ya fiat, abona ubuhendanyi bwinshi cane, ukwihenda canke uguhindura amafaranga.


#### Uburinganire bwa Exchange


Naho Bitcoin itararemerwa kw’isi yose nk’amafaranga y’amahera, kamere yayo y’ugukorana n’abandi, ibihe vy’ugucuruza vyihuta, n’amahera make bituma iba uburyo bugenda burakwegera Exchange, cane cane ku bijanye n’ugucuruza hagati y’ibihugu. Ivyo bishoboka kubera ko ari:



- Ishobora gutwara:** Bitcoin, kuba ari digitale, iremesha guhanahana amakuru ata mipaka n'uwubihuza hagati y'abantu, bikaba bituma iba uburyo bwiza kandi bushoboka bwo gukoresha Exchange. Naho amafaranga amwamwe y’ubuhinga bwa none na yo nyene atanga inyishu z’ubuhinga bwa none, abo mu bihugu biri mu nzira y’amajambere canke mu bihugu birimwo intambara boshobora kugorwa no kuronka ibikorwa vya banki bishitsa ivyo bikenewe. Kubera ko Bitcoin ishobora gushikirizwa abantu bose, bituma umuntu wese afise internet ashobora kuyironka, bikaba ari uburyo bushoboka bwo gusubirira uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki mu turere tudashobora kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’ubutunzi.
- Divisible:** Ugucapura cane kwa Bitcoin ni kimwe mu vyiza vyayo nyamukuru nk’ifaranga. Kubera ko Bitcoin yose ishobora kugabanywa gushika ku bice umunani vy’icumi, igice gitoyi kuruta ibindi vyose, ari co Satoshi, gifise agaciro k’agace gusa k’isenti. Bivanye n’uburyo bwo gucuruza, ni ukuvuga Layer imwe canke zibiri, ivyo bituma Bitcoin ishobora guhura cane n’ugucuruza kw’ubunini bwose, kuva ku kugura guto gushika ku gushiramwo amahera menshi.
- Yemewe:** Naho kwemerwa kwa Bitcoin kutarashika kw’isi yose, ukuntu abacuruzi, inzego n’abantu ku giti cabo kw’isi yose bagenda barushiriza kwemerwa, birerekana ko iriko irarushiriza kwemerwa nk’uburyo bubereye bwo kwishura.


### Igice ca konti


Uko Bitcoin yaronse icubahiro nk’umurongo wa Exchange, yaraduze ningoga mu rwego nk’igice co kwizigirwa c’ivy’ibicuruzwa n’ibikorwa, nk’amahera y’amahera. Ariko rero, ikintu gitandukanya Bitcoin na fiat ni ubushobozi bwayo bwo gutanga uburyo bwo gukorana butekanye, buboneye kandi bushizwe ahantu hamwe. Igituma cane cane Bitcoin iguma yemerwa nk’igice c’ikonti ni uko ari:



- Fungible:** Bitcoin yose ntishobora gutandukanywa n’iyindi yose, ivyo bikaba bituma ishobora guhindurwa bitagoranye, ivyo bikaba bidahora ari ko biri ku mafaranga y’umubiri ashobora kuba afise ibimenyetso bidasanzwe canke akaba afise uburyo butandukanye.


### Itunga vs Urubuga


Ushobora kuba warabonye haruguru ko Bitcoin atari gusa umutungo ukomeye wo kubikamwo agaciro, ariko ibiranga bidasanzwe navyo biyigira urubuga rutekanye kandi rukora neza cane rwo gukorana. Ivyo vyoshobora kumvikana nk’ibiteye urujijo gatoyi, reka rero tubisigure. Bitcoin, nka fiat, igizwe n’ibice bibiri:


**Itunga (ryitwa Bitcoin rifise urudome ruto “b”)** – Ivyo ni vyo tugura bishobora gushikwako kuri Wallet yacu. Iyo tubitswe hanze y’amasoko canke amasakoshi, ukwizigira kwacu ku kwizigira kuragabanywa, ahanini kwibanda ku mutekano w’ibikoresho vyacu. Naho ari ukwo, turashobora kugabanya ukwo kwizigira mu gushigikira ata nkomanzi amajambo yacu ya seed canke mu gukoresha uburyo bwo kubika nk’ugushirako umukono mwinshi. Ikindi kandi, turavye ko ingingo iyo ari yo yose igamije guhindura ibiranga nyamukuru vya Bitcoin, nk’umubare wose wa Supply, zigenwa kandi zigashigikirwa n’abanyagihugu, hariho uburinzi bukomeye bwo gukingira ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’amahinduka ashobora gutuma abakoresha bagira ingorane, ni ukuvuga ugusenyura amafaranga biciye mu Supply.


**Ikigobe (citwa Bitcoin gifise urudome runini “B”)** – Ivyo ni vyo bifasha mu gucuruza Bitcoin-the-asset. Iryo shirahamwe ryemerera umuntu wese kohereza, kugenzura canke kwemeza amafaranga. Kamere ya Bitcoin yegerejwe, ishigikiwe n’ibice vyinshi, abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro, n’abategura, bituma habaho imiterere igabanywa aho ata kintu na kimwe gifise ububasha ku kindi. Ivyo bituma umuntu yumva afise umutekano n’ukwizigirwa igihe ariko aragurisha, bikaba bikuraho amaganya yerekeye ukuntu umuntu yoshobora guhindura ibintu, guhakana, guhagarika canke ibindi bintu bishobora kumuhagarika.


Iyo turavye amafaranga y'amahera y'amahera (fiat currencies) mu buryo bw'"umutungo" n'"uruja n'uruza", biragaragara ko dutegerezwa kwizigira cane no kwizigira abandi bantu n'abahuza. Nk'akarorero:


#### **Itunga** - _Amafaranga dukoresha nk'ububiko bw'agaciro (Nk'idolari ry'Amerika, amayero, yen, amafaranga, amapawundi, n'ibindi)._


**Abanki nkuru zigenzura politike y’amahera** – Politike y’amahera yerekeza ku ngingo zifatwa na banki nkuru kugira ngo zicunge inyungu n’amahera yose hamwe Supply ariko arakoreshwa. Iyo banki nkuru igabanyije inyungu canke yongera amahera Supply, yinjiza amahera mashasha mu bukungu, gutyo igatuma agaciro k’amahera yariho ariko arakoreshwa kagabanuka. Ivyo bituma ubushobozi bwo kugura bw'amafaranga bugabanuka, bigatuma haba ugutera imbere kw'ibiciro.


**Leta zigenzura Politike y’Imari** – Politike y’Imari yerekeye ibikorwa vya Leta bijanye n’imisoro n’amahera Leta ikoresha. Nk’akarorero, iyo Leta ifashe ingingo yo gutuma ubutunzi butera imbere mu kugabanya imisoro no gutanga amafaranga yo gutera imbere, bica bituma abanyagihugu bongera amahera bashobora gukoresha, ivyo bikaba bituma bakoresha amahera menshi. Ukwo gukoresha amahera kwongerekana birashobora gutuma ibiciro biduga, bikajana mu gutera imbere kw’ibiciro no kugabanya ubushobozi bwacu bwo kugura uko igihe kigenda kirarenga.


Nk’abanyagihugu, turayoborwa n’ingingo zifatwa n’abajejwe politike y’amahera n’ivy’ubutunzi, kandi dutegerezwa kwizigira ivyiyumviro vyabo. Twizigira Leta yacu n’abakozi ba banki nkuru batatowe ngo bakore ku nyungu zacu, ariko amahitamwo yabo arashobora kugira ico akoze cane ku bushobozi bwo kugura bw’amahera yacu, bigatuma n’ubuzima bwacu bugira ico bukoze. Kandi amateka yaragaragaje incuro nyinshi ko ico cizigiro cahungabanijwe, bigatuma amahera agabanuka.


#### **Ihuriro** - _Imirongo ituma dushobora gukorana n'abandi._


**Igihe ugura ikawa ukoresheje ikarita yacu y’inguzanyo, hariho abahuza bane canke barenga batandukanye** - Ubwa mbere ni banki iyo kafe ikoresha. Ubwa kabiri, ni imihora y’itumanaho ituma amabanki ashobora guhanahana amahera hagati yayo. Inyuma y’aho, hariho ishirahamwe rikora ivyo gucuruza, nka Visa, Mastercard canke Discover. Kandi mu nyuma, hariho ikigo cacu c’amabanki, kigenzura kandi kikandika ivyo bicuruzwa.


**Igihe twohereza amahera, dukora ku bantu bane canke barenga** - Kugira ngo dutangure kohereza amahera, turakeneye guha banki yacu amakuru ya banki y’uwuyakira. Kubera ko banki yacu idashobora guhura ata guca ku ruhande na banki y’uwuyironka, amakuru y’ivyo bikoresho yoherezwa biciye ku rubuga rwa SWIFT (Société mondiale des télécommunications financières interbancaires) hakoreshejwe banki y’abanyamakuru canke y’umuhuza. Izo banki zica zihamagara banki y’uwuzironka kugira ngo zirangize gutanga amahera.


**Inzego zijejwe gucungera amafaranga zigenzura amaboko atandukanye y’inzira z’amahera dukoresha ku musi ku musi** - Iyo ivyiyumviro vyacu vya politike biteye kubiri n’amabwirizwa agenga imirongo y’amahera canke igice ico ari co cose c’urugendo rw’ubuhuza, amafaranga dukora yoshobora kuba ari mu kaga ko guhagarara, kandi itunga ryacu ryoshobora gufatwa. Mu bihe bikomeye cane, twoshobora mbere gushikirwa n’ingorane yo gukurwa mu bijanye n’ivy’ubutunzi burundu.


Ivyo vyoba biteye ubwoba canke bidashoboka? Mu ntango z’umwaka wa 2022, mu gihe c’ihuriro ry’abashoferi b’ibikamyo muri Canada, abantu baratanze amahera yo gushigikira iyo ntumbero. Minisitiri w’intebe Trudeau yatumye bamwe muri abo bantu bafunga amakonte ya banki n’itegeko ryiwe. Utitaye ku ciyumviro umuntu afise ku bijanye n’ico kibazo, kuba itunga ry’abantu ryafashwe kubera ivyiyumviro vyabo bitandukanye, vyoba ari ibendera ry’umutuku.


Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, hariho ivyiza vyinshi cane vyo kutagira gusa uburenganzira bwo kuronka umutungo w’agaciro, udasanzwe, ariko no kuronka urubuga rwo guhindura agaciro rutekanye, rukora neza, Trustless, rwo kw’isi yose, kandi rufise amahera make. Kandi aha niho Bitcoin isumba izindi. Nk’uko vyavuzwe mu buryo burambuye, kamere ya Bitcoin yegerejwe n’ubuhinga bwa none ituma haba urubuga rudasanzwe rwo gukorana vyihuta, bitekanye kandi bitazimvye ata nkenerwa y’abahuza canke abandi bantu. Aha hari ingero nkeyi z’abaronka inyungu ku mutungo n’urubuga rwa Bitcoin bitagira uko bingana:


#### Ubucuruzi


Bitcoin iha abacuruzi ububasha butagira uko bungana ku bijanye n’ibikorwa vyabo, bikaba bituma bashobora guca ku bahuza b’ivy’ubutunzi ba kera nk’amabanki n’amashirahamwe y’amakarata y’inguzanyo. Ivyo bisigura ko amahera menshi aguma mu minwe y’umudandaza aho gufatwa n’amahera menshi y’ugucuruza be n’ibindi bihembo. Hakoreshejwe Bitcoin, abacuruzi barashobora kandi guhitamwo kwemera amahera bavuye aho bari hose kw’isi ataco bakeneye guhindura amafaranga canke abandi bahuza, ivyo bikaba bigabanya igiciro kandi bikongera inyungu. Mu guha abacuruzi ububasha bwinshi ku bikorwa vyabo, Bitcoin iriko irahindura uburyo twiyumvira ku bijanye n’ubudandaji, igaha ubushobozi ubudandaji bw’ingero zose kugira ngo bushobore guhangana n’ubutunzi bugenda buratera imbere kw’isi yose.


#### Ibiciro


Kuva mu mpera z’umwaka wa 2022, hafi [igice c’ isi](https://Elements.visualcapitalist.com/ibihugu-bifise-igipimo-c'ugutera imbere-kirengeye/#:~:text=Iterambere%20riraduga%20hafi%20hose,ugutera imbere kw'ibiciro kw'imibare%20 kwari hejuru cane,20canke%2) bikaba bituma biba ikintu gihambaye cane. Iyo ibiciro vy’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro bigumye kuri urwo rwego mu myaka cumi izoza, bizotuma ubushobozi bwo kugura butakaza 65%. Ariko rero, Bitcoin ubu iraha umuntu wese inzira yo gusohokamwo. Kubera ko ari umutungo udasanzwe vy’ukuri, agaciro kawo ntigashobora gusenyuka biciye mu kwagura Supply, bikaturonsa uburyo bwo guhunga ingaruka mbi z’ugusenyuka kw’amahera.


#### Guhunga ibihugu vyasambuwe n’intambara canke bidatekanye


Bitcoin itanga uburyo bushoboka bwo kwimurira agaciro ku bahunga ibihugu vyasambuwe n’intambara canke bidatekanye. Akenshi, abantu bari muri ivyo bihe ntibashobora kuronka ubufasha bwa kera bwa banki kubera ukubura ibikorwa remezo canke ubugenzuzi bwa Leta ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubutunzi. Bitcoin iremesha abo bantu kubika agaciro mu buryo bwegerejwe kandi butekanye ata nkenerwa y’abahuza canke ivy’umubiri bishobora gushikirwa n’ubusuma canke gufatwa. Hakoreshejwe Bitcoin, abantu barashobora kwikorera ubutunzi bwabo mu mitwe yabo, bajabuka imipaka kandi ata bwoba bafise bwo gutakaza itunga ryabo kubera umuvurungano uwo ari wo wose wo ku mubiri canke wo mu vya politike. Ivyo bitanga urugero rw’umwidegemvyo n’ukwigenga mu vy’amahera bitagira uko bingana mu bijanye n’ubutunzi bwa kera.


#### Kwoherezwa amafranga


Ivyo tuzobivugako mu buryo burambuye cane mu kiganiro gikurikira, ariko ubu, turashaka kuvuga ko Bitcoin itanga abantu ku giti cabo uburyo bwiza kandi butazimvye bwo gusubiza amahera ababo bari mu mahanga. Mu buryo butandukanye n’uburyo bwa kera bwo kohereza amahera, akenshi busaba amahera menshi yo gukoresha be n’igihe kirekire co gukora, amahera yo gukoresha Bitcoin arashobora kurangira ningoga kandi ata mahera menshi.


Mu bijanye n’ivyo, naho Bitcoin, umutungo, ushobora gutanga inyungu nyinshi ku barondera guhunga ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro canke kubika agaciro mu mafaranga afise umutekano mwinshi, turatahura ko abantu benshi bashobora kutabasha kwungukira ku mutungo, ni ukuvuga ko uguhinduka kwa Bitcoin nk’umutungo, bishobora kutaba kuzigama. Igishimishije, urubuga rwa Bitcoin ruzogira uruhara runini hano, cane cane ku bantu ku giti cabo badashobora gushika ku mabanki canke ku mutungo w’amahera, kubera ko inzira zo kwishura z’urwo rubuga zituma umuntu wese afise telefone ngendanwa na internet ashobora gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none.


Bitcoin nayo iriko irihuta kuba umurongo w’agaciro wo gutanga agaciro kuri internet. Kubera ubushobozi bwo gutanga amafaranga make, ibikorwa nk’ugutanga agaciro biratangura kwiyongera, bikaba bihuza abahingura ibintu n’ababumviriza. Na vyo nyene, ubu bushobozi bwo gutanga amakuru ku giciro gito buriko burabona iterambere mu bikorwa vyishyurwa nk’ugupima inguvu, aho abakoresha bashobora kwishura ivyo basaba mu kanya nk’ako gukubita, gutanga amakuru Bitcoin ku giciro c’ugukoresha. Ivyo kwishura bitagiramwo amahane biriko birahindura uburyo abantu bakorana n’ibintu n’ibikorwa biciye mu buhinga bwa none.


**Iciyumviro**


Ibiranga Bitcoin bidasanzwe nk’ububiko bw’agaciro, uburinganire bwa Exchange, n’igice ca konti biyigira ifaranga riri mu mugwi wayo bwite. Ukwegereza kwayo, ukubura, ukuramba, ukudahinduka, ukwitwaza, kwemera, gucapura, n’uguhindura vyose bihurikiye hamwe kugira ngo bivemwo urubuga rukomeye kandi rukora neza rushobora gukoreshwa mu bikorwa vy’ubudandaji bifise iherezo, umutekano, ubushobozi, n’amahera make.


Ikindi kandi, izo kamere zihurikiye hamwe ntizishira gusa Bitcoin nk’igikoresho gikomeye co kubika no kwubaka ubutunzi mu kiringo kirekire (Bitcoin umutungo) ariko kandi zitanga inyungu nyinshi ku barondera gukoresha Bitcoin nk’uburyo bwo gukorana (Bitcoin urubuga). Ivyo bitandukanye cane n’amahera y’amahera, ivyo bikaba bikeneye kwizigirana n’abahuza muri ivyo bihe vyose bibiri. Ivyo bituma Bitcoin iba amahera akwegera abantu ku giti cabo be n’ubudandaji, ata kuraba ko akoreshwa mu kuzigama canke mu gukora amahera.


## Gukorana na Bitcoin


<chapterId>050a95af-e9c2-5ec3-b9c8-55ec174d309c</chapterId>


Bitcoin yatwaye uburyo bw’amahera, ifata umutima w’ibihugu biri mu nzira y’amajambere, abantu bazi ivy’ubuhinga n’abashoramari. Ariko rero, kubera ukuntu iriko irakura cane, benshi baribaza ingene iyo nkuru y’ubuhinga bwa none ishobora guhangana n’uburyo bwa kera bwo kwishura nka Visa na Mastercard. Ikindi, abantu barashaka kumenya ingene boshobora gukorana na Bitcoin.


Muri iki gice, tuzokwihweza mu mice itandukanye y'ugucuruza, haba mu fiat canke Bitcoin. Turaza kandi kuraba uburyo bwiza bwo kubungabunga Bitcoin yawe, harimwo n'akamaro ko guhitamwo Wallet ibereye.


### Ivyumba vya Bitcoin


Blockchain ya Bitcoin igizwe n’amabuye nk’uko izina ryayo rivyerekana. Ivyo bice bifise ubunini burengeye ubw’ibindi vyose bugera kuri megabytes 4. _Ivyo bivuzwe, ubunini bw’ibarabara mu gihe c’ukwandika buza hafi 1.5mb._ Kubera iyo nzira, hariho uburenganzira ku rugero rw’ibikorwa Bitcoin ishobora gukora ku segonda, ni ukuvuga hagati y’ibikorwa indwi n’icumi ku segonda (tps).


Ku bw’ivyo, woshobora kwibaza uti: Ni gute Bitcoin’s Blockchain ishobora guhangana n’amashirahamwe nka Visa canke Mastercard akora amahera ku [1.700 ]. tps](https://ku-buhinga-bw'amakuru.com/ikibazo-c'ugutera imbere-mu-Blockchain-igikorwa-c'ugushaka-visa-nk'umuvuduko-w'ugucuruza-5cce48f9d44)?


Inyishu ni yoroshe. Si uguhiganwa na bo.


Kugereranya Bitcoin’s Blockchain na Visa canke Mastercard ni nk’ukugereranya ubwato mpuzamakungu butwara ibintu n’ugusohora amahera mw’iduka ry’ibikoresho ryo mu karere. Ubwato bw’ibikoresho bugenewe gucuruza ibintu vyinshi bidakunda gushika, mu gihe igikoresho co gusohora amahera cubatswe ku bicuruzwa bikunda gukoreshwa cane kandi bitobito. Naho vyose bijana ibintu, kubigereranya ni nk’ukugereranya amapome n’imiceri.


Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, Bitcoin itanga Trustless, amafaranga ata ruhusha afise n’ugutanga amafaranga y’iherezo, mu gihe Visa na Mastercard zitanga uburyo bwo gukoresha neza no kworoha. Ariko rero, ivyo ntibisigura ko Bitcoin’s Blockchain na yo nyene itatanga ivyo bintu. Ntigerageza gusa kubishikako ku ruzitiro rw’ishimikiro canke ku ruzitiro rw’ishimikiro Layer nk’uko bizwi cane.


Reka dusuzume ico ivyo bisobanura...


Igihe umuntu asuzuma uburyo ubwo ari bwo bwose bwo gukoresha amahera, akenshi hari uburyo butandukanye, canke ibice, vyo gukoresha, uburyo bumwebumwe bwose bugatanga inyungu zitandukanye ku wubukoresha. Ivyiyumviro vy’ugucuruza muri sisitemu y’amahera yacu y’ubu birimwo:


**Layer One:** Ivyo bikorwa bikoreshwa amahera menshi cane ariko bikaba bifise ubushobozi buke bwo gukora, bisobanura ko amahera makeyi gusa ashobora gukorwa mu segonda. Ingero z’ibikorwa vya Layer imwe mu buryo bw’amahera bwa kera ni ugutanga amahera muri banki n’ugutanga amahera hagati y’amabanki na Fed Wire. Ivyo bikoresho bikoreshwa mu bikorwa vy’agaciro kanini, ariko kenshi biragenda buhoro kandi birazimvye, amafaranga yo gutanga amakuru ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi ava ku \$10 gushika ku \$50 n’ibihe vyo gukora bishobora gutwara imisi myinshi. Naho amafaranga y’ubudandaji ya Layer one afise umutekano kandi yizigirwa, yoshobora kutaba ari yo mahitamwo meza ku baguzi bakeneye gukora amafaranga makeyi vyihuta kandi ataco bimaze.


**Layer Kabiri:** Iyi Layer mu bisanzwe irimwo amafaranga make y’agaciro kanini, bikaba bishoboza amafaranga menshi gukorwa mu segonda. Itanga amafaranga yihuta kandi atari make, amafaranga akenshi aba ari hafi 1-3% y’agaciro k’amafaranga. Ingero zisanzwe z’ibikorwa bibiri vya Layer mu buryo bw’amahera bwa kera ni ukwishura n’ikarita y’inguzanyo n’iy’ideni, ibikorwa vyo kwishura kuri Internet, n’ugukoresha ikarita y’ingabirano.


**Ni hehe Bitcoin Blockchain ijyanye n’ibikorwa vya Layer bimwe na Layer bibiri?**


Bitcoin Blockchain ni ubundi buryo bwiza bwo gukoresha Layer imwe. Naho yoba idashobora guhura n’umuvuduko w’ukwishura Visa zibiri za Layer, irashobora gukora amafaranga y’agaciro kanini ku rugero rutoyi rw’umuvuduko n’igiciro c’uburyo bwa kera bwa Layer one. Ikindi kandi, Bitcoin ikora mu buryo butagira uruhusha kandi mu buryo bwa Trustless, bisobanura ko amafaranga ashobora gukorwa ata bahuza.


Ariko naho nyene ifise ivyiza nk’umuti umwe wa Layer, Bitcoin irashobora kandi guhangana na Layer uburyo bubiri bwo gucuruza. Hariho ubuhinga bushingiye ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin, nka Lightning, bufasha ababukoresha gukorana hafi mu kanya nk’ako gukubita kandi ku bice vy’isenti. Izo tekinoloji zishobora kwiyumvirwa nk’imiti ibiri ya Layer ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin. Dufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, nk'uko nyene uburyo bwacu bw'amahera bwa kera bufise Layer imwe n'ibiri, ni ko Bitcoin ifise.


Niba uriko urarondera uburyo bwo kohereza amahera menshi bwihuta (ariko butari ubwo nyene), butazimvye kandi butekanye, rero Bitcoin Layer ni yo nzira nziza cane. Ariko, nimba uriko urarondera gukorana hafi-mu kanya nk’ako gukubita kandi ku bice vy’isenti, uzoshaka kwerekeza umutima wawe kuri bimwe mu bikoresho vyubatswe kuri Bitcoin, birimwo ibintu bishasha nka [Lightning](https://lightning.network/).


Bitcoin Lightning Network ni umuti w’ibipimo bibiri vyubatswe hejuru y’umwe Bitcoin Layer. Ituma umuntu ashobora gukora amafaranga hafi y’aho nyene ataco atanga, ivyo bikaba bituma amafaranga makeyi n’ugugura ibintu bitobito bishoboka.

Kuva El Salvador yemeye Bitcoin nk’amahera yemewe, abantu benshi barakoresha Lightning Network mu gucuruza Bitcoin aho gukoresha Layer isanzwe kubera inyungu zayo. Lightning Network, abayikoresha barashobora kwishura agace k’isenti ku bikorwa hafi vy’aho nyene, bikaba bituma iba nziza cane ku bacuruzi bashaka kwemera kwishura Bitcoin ata mahera menshi n’ibihe vy’ugucuruza bigenda buhoro nk’ibikorwa vya kera vya On-Chain Bitcoin. Ivyo vyatumye vyoroha kandi bishikira abanya El Salvador gukoresha Bitcoin mu bikorwa vya misi yose, ivyo bikaba vyatumye habaho ubushobozi bwo kwemera Bitcoin nk’ifaranga ry’isi yose.


Reka noneho twibande ku co wokora umaze kuronka Bitcoin canke ufashe ingingo yo kugura.


### Gukingira neza Bitcoin yawe


Igituma Bitcoin ihindura ibintu ni uko, ku ncuro ya mbere muri kahise, dushobora kwicungera umutungo w’ubuhinga bwa none. Ico gikorwa gikomeye ntigishobora kurengerwa! Nka kurya nyene dushobora kubika amahera munsi y’umusego wacu, turashobora gukora nk’ukwo nyene na Bitcoin, ariko mu buryo bwa digitale. Ariko rero, urwo rwego rushasha rwo kugenzura amahera yacu ruzanana n’amabanga mashasha. Kugira ngo Bitcoin yacu igume itekanye, dutegerezwa kwiga ingene twoyikingira neza. Ivyo bisigura gutera intambwe zo kwirinda gutakaza, kwiba no kugerageza gutera.


#### Aho wobika Bitcoin yawe


Intambwe ya mbere yo gukingira Bitcoin yawe ni uguhitamwo Wallet ibereye. Tutajanye n’ibintu vyinshi, hariho ahanini ubwoko bubiri bw’amasakoshi ashobora gukoreshwa: ayo kubika n’ayo kutabika.


**Ibipapuro vy'ububiko**

Ivyo ni ibipapuro aho, naho woba ushobora gushika ku Wallet yawe no kwimurira amahera, uwundi muntu abika kandi akabungabunga Bitcoin yawe.


Akarorero kamwe gasanzwe k’ikete ry’ububiko ryitwa Wallet ni konti ya Exchange. Iyo uguze Bitcoin biciye ku Exchange ugasiga Bitcoin yawe kuri Exchange, uba uriko ukoresha Wallet yo kubika. Exchange irafise ububasha bwo kuzigama Bitcoin yawe kandi ni yo ishinzwe kubika no gucungera amahera yawe.


Hariho kandi n’ibindi bisubizo vyinshi vy’ububiko bwa Wallet biboneka ku bikoresho vy’amaboko biguha uburenganzira bwo gukoresha Bitcoin yawe mu buryo bworoshe. Izo nkweto zikoreshwa neza kandi zitanga uburyo bworoshe bwo gucunga Bitcoin yawe, ariko zica zifise imfunguruzo za Bitcoin yawe.


**Ibikoko bitagira ububiko (a.k.a. kwibika)**

Ama wallet atagira ububiko ni ubwoko bwa Bitcoin Wallet aho ari wewe wenyene ubika amafaranga yawe, bisobanura ko ufise ububasha bwose ku mfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga. Imfunguruzo z’ibanga zimeze nk’ijambobanga ry’urupapuro rwawe rwa Wallet kandi zikoreshwa mu gusinya no kwemerera amafaranga. Iyo utazifise, ntushobora kuronka canke gutanga Bitcoin yawe.


Ivyuma bitagira amafaranga y’ububiko bitanga umutekano n’ubuzima bwite kuruta ivy’amafaranga y’ububiko kuko ari wewe wenyene ushinzwe umutekano w’amahera yawe. Ingero z’ibikoresho bitagira ububiko ni nk’ibikoresho nka [Coldcard](https://store.coinkite.com/store/coldcard) na [Trezor](https://trezor.io/), ari ibikoresho vy’umubiri bibika imfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga ata murongo kandi bitanga umutekano w’inyongera GW-27. Ibindi bikoresho bikundwa cane bitagiramwo ububiko ni ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none nka [Sparrow](https://sparrowwallet.com/), [Electrum](https://electrum.org/#home), na [Blockstream Green](https://blockstream.com/Green/), bishobora gukurwa kuri mudasobwa yawe canke kubishira kuri telefone ngendanwa.


\*_Naho tutashobora gusaba Wallet yihariye, turaguhanura cane ko wofata ububasha kuri Bitcoin yawe biciye mu kwizigama canke mu kwizigama hamwe n’abandi, ivyo bikaba birimwo guhitamwo Wallet ihuye n’ivyo ukeneye n’ivyo ukunda. Ni ngombwa gukora ubushakashatsi bwimbitse imbere yo gufata ingingo ku Wallet kugira ngo umenye neza ko ihuye n'ivyo usaba ku bijanye n'umutekano n'ugukoreshwa._


Naho amasakoshi yo kubika yoshobora gusa n’abereye, azana n’ingorane zikomeye. Mu guha uwundi muntu uburenganzira bwo kuzigama imfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga, uba umuhaye ububasha bwo kugenzura amahera yawe. Iyo uwucungera amafaranga ashobora guhomba, akawufata, canke akawufunga, woshobora gutakaza uburenganzira bwo kuronka Bitcoin yawe. Kandi ivyo vyabaye incuro zitari nke, n’ingero zikomeye cane harimwo n’ivy’ubusuma bwa Mt. Gox na QuadrigaCX vyatumye amahera y’abaguzi batakaza, canke FTX, Voyager, BlockFi, na Celsius zishikirwa n’ibibazo bikomeye vy’uguhomba, bituma amahera y’abaguzi babo atakaza. Cane cane ku bijanye no kuzigama, kwimenyereza kwirinda no kwitwararika inshingano yo kurinda Bitcoin yawe ni ikintu gihambaye cane.


#### Impanuro zo gukingira


Iyo umaze gufata ingingo ku Wallet, umunezero n’imikino ntibirahera gusa. Ubu ni igihe co kugabanya ingorane zo gutakaza. Kugira ngo ukinge Bitcoin yawe, zirikana izi ntambwe umaze guhitamwo Wallet yawe:


1. Mbere na mbere, ushire inyuma Wallet yawe igihe ufata uburenganzira bwo kwibungabunga. Ivyuma vy’amafaranga biza n’ijambo ry’ugusubizaho seed, ni ukuvuga amajambo ashobora gukoreshwa mu gusubizaho imfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga mu gihe igikoresho cawe coba carazimiye canke coba cononekaye. Rema kopi y’umubiri, nk’isahani y’icuma seed, y’iri [jambo seed](https://coincodex.com/ingingo/23147/amafaranga-y’ivyuma-meza-y’ububiko- bw’amajambo-seed/) hanyuma ubike mu gitereko. Ni ngombwa ko iri jambo ry’ugukira seed riguma ritekanye. NTUKIGEZE ubisangiza umuntu n’umwe.

2. Igihe urinda umubare munini wa Bitcoin urenze urugero utoshaka gutakaza, birahambaye ko utohoza uburyo bwo gutegura ivy’ubutaka ku kintu kitari gitegekanijwe c’ugupfa kwawe. Ivyo bituma umuryango wawe n’abakunzi bawe bashobora kuronka no gucunga neza urupapuro rwawe rwa Bitcoin.

3. Ube maso ku bijanye n’ukugerageza kwihenda n’ibindi bihendahenda. Akenshi abahendanyi baragerageza kukuhenda ngo ubahe uburenganzira bwo kuronka urupapuro rwawe rwa Bitcoin mu kwigira nk’ishirahamwe canke umuntu wizigirwa. Nta sosiyete izwi cane izokwigera ikusaba imfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga, rero ntukigere usangira imfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga n’umuntu uwo ari we wese, kandi wama ugenzura ukuri kw’urubuga urwo ari rwo rwose canke umuntu imbere yo kohereza Bitcoin.


Naho ukwirinda ari bwo buryo dusaba, turatahura ko bushobora kutabereye umuntu wese. Akira amabwirizwa rusangi yo gufasha kugabanya ingorane:



- Koresha amabarabara kugira ngo ugure Bitcoin, amasakoshi y’amatelefone ngendanwa yo gukoresha mu bikorwa vya misi yose, n’amasakoshi y’ibikoresho kugira ngo ubike amahera yawe y’igihe kirekire ya Bitcoin.
- Fata amafaranga yo guhindura canke amasakoshi agendagenda nk'ama Wallet yawe, ugumye gusa umubare w'ama Bitcoin woshobora gutwara muri Wallet yawe ya misi yose.
- Niwiyumvire ko Hardware Wallet yawe ari konti yawe yo kuzigama. Ni ivy’abantu badakunda gushikako kandi bishira imbere umutekano n’umutekano w’igihe kirekire.


Kandi nimba uriko urakoresha Exchange:


1. Rema ijambobanga rikomeye kandi ridasanzwe. Irinde gukoresha amajambo asanzwe canke amajambo y’ibanga yoroshe gutekereza ku bintu. Niwiyumvire gukoresha umucungerezi w’ijambobanga.

2. Gushoboza ivyemezo bibiri (2FA) igihe cose bishoboka. Ivyo birongerezako Layer y’umutekano mu gusaba kode iva kuri telefone yawe canke ku gikoresho cawe c’ubuhinga bwa none uretse ijambobanga ryawe.


Niba utaramenya neza, turagusavye cane kuraba Ben wo muri [BTCsessions](https://www.youtube.com/c/BTCsessions) kuri YouTube.


Ibuka ko ububasha bukomeye bujana n’inshingano nyinshi, kandi gufata umwanya wo gucungera neza Bitcoin yawe ni ngirakamaro kugira ngo ukinge kazoza kawe k’ivy’amahera.


Mbere yo gufunga iki cigwa, ndashaka kubasiga iciyumviro ca nyuma...


### Kwibira ibwina cane


Niba ushaka kurushiriza kumenya isi ya Bitcoin, hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo kubikora. Nka nka:


1. **Nodes:** Gukoresha node ni inzira nziza cane yo kwinjiramwo ku bashaka kumenya ivyerekeye Bitcoin birenze ibikorwa vy’ishimikiro. Biguha uburenganzira bwo kudatanga umusanzu gusa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin mu kugenzura Blockchain no guhindura ibintu bishasha canke amahinduka ariko bigabanya ukwizigira kandi biguha ubuzima bwite bwongerewe mu kuguha ubushobozi bwo kugenzura amafaranga yawe bwite n’amafaranga yawe. Mu gukoresha urudodo, uba ubaye igice c’urubuga rwegerejwe kandi ugafasha kumenya neza umutekano n’ubutungane bwarwo.

2. **Mining:** Mining ni ubundi buryo bwo gutanga umusanzu ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin kandi ushobora kuronka Bitcoin. Naho bisaba amafaranga menshi gatoyi kuruta gukoresha node kandi bitagira inyungu nk’uko vyari bimeze kera, Mining ni igikorwa gitanga impera ku bakunda ivy’ubuhinga bw’urubuga.

3. **Iterambere:** Niba ufise ubumenyi mu gutegura porogarama kandi ushaka gutanga umusanzu mu gutegura Bitcoin, intango nziza cane ni ububiko bwa Bitcoin [GitHub](https://github.com/Bitcoin/Bitcoin).


Utitaye ku vyo ukunda, hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo kugufasha kumenya vyinshi ku vyerekeye Bitcoin no kwitabira.


### **Iciyumviro**


Naho kenshi twumva ko Bitcoin idashobora kwigera ihangana na Visa canke Mastercard, twizigiye ko iki gice cerekanye ko ico ciyumviro atari ukuri. Aho guhangana n’ayo masosiyete ata guca ku ruhande, Layer y’ishimikiro ya Bitcoin yagenewe gukora neza cane amafaranga y’agaciro kanini kuruta uburyo bwa kera. Ivyo bituma ari uburyo bwiza cane bwo gusubirira inyishu za kera za Layer imwe. Vyongeye, ubuhinga nk’ubwo bwa The Lightning Network, bubatswe hejuru y’ubwo bwa Bitcoin Layer, buratuma umuntu ashobora gukoresha hafi ubwo nyene ku giciro gitoyi gusa c’isenti. Gutyo, Bitcoin irashobora guhangana na Visa na Mastercard, itanga inyishu ku bucuruzi no ku bantu ku giti cabo.


Inyungu nini cane ya Bitcoin ni uko ituma tugira uburenganzira bwo kwibungabunga umutungo w’ubuhinga bwa none, ivyo bikaba bitari bwigere bishoboka mbere. Niwumva urengewe umaze guca muri iki gice, ntuhagarike umutima. Gufata ububasha ku Bitcoin yawe bwite ni intambwe ikomeye ijana ku mwidegemvyo w’amahera, ariko kandi izana n’amabanga mashasha. Ariko rero, ukoze ubushakashatsi bukeyi kandi ugakorana umwete, ayo mabanga mashasha azokwihuta kuba akameremere ka kabiri kuri wewe, kandi uzokwiyumvamwo neza gufata igikorwa co gukingira Bitcoin yawe ata nkomanzi.


## Ivyigwa


<chapterId>1c7b8165-d67b-5f7c-a1cb-b83db58b77c7</chapterId>


None ko mwaciye mu Module "Isuzuma ry'ingene twashitse ngaha" muzobwirizwa kugerageza ubumenyi mushasha muronka kugira ngo mumenye neza ko mwatahuye ibice vya nyuma. Tuzotangura n’Ibibazo vyinshi vyuguruye hanyuma dukore ikibazo gitoyi.


1. Ni ibihe vyiyumviro mufise ku ciyumviro ca Trustless n’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none yegerejwe ata ruhusha nka Bitcoin? None mubona bigereranywa gute n’uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amahera?

2. Woba wemera ko Supply y’agaciro gatoyi ya Bitcoin, ifise ibiceri vy’amamiliyoni 21 gusa, biyiha agaciro kandi bikayigira umuntu yipfuzwa cane? Kubera iki canke kubera iki?

3. Ushingiye ku makuru yatanzwe ku bijanye na Satoshi Nakamoto, woba wibaza ko ari ngirakamaro kumenya akaranga nyakuri k’umuremyi wa Bitcoin? Kubera iki canke kubera iki?

4. Woba wemeranya n’ivyo Satoshi Nakamoto avuga ku bijanye n’uburyo bwo gukoresha amabanki ahuriweko n’ukwizigirana gukenewe mu mafaranga asanzwe? Kubera iki canke kubera iki?

5. Ibaze ko uba mu gihugu gifise inflation nyinshi. Ni gute Bitcoin yoshobora gutanga umuti wo kuzigama ubushobozi bwawe bwo kugura?

6. Rimbura ikintu cobaye aho ukeneye kohereza amahera uwo mu muryango wawe ari mu gihugu gitandukanye. Ni gute kamere ya Bitcoin y’urunganwe n’amahera make yoshobora kukugirira akamaro muri iki gihe?


# Gushikama hagati mu kavuyo - Intangamarara ku Tether & Isi y'Ibiceri Bishikamye


<partId>60b1f3c4-e161-53fe-84ca-88d8cd62aa75</partId>


## Intangamarara ya Tether n'isi y'ibiceri bikomeye


<chapterId>427a72b5-8af7-503e-bc45-bb8b95483993</chapterId>


Nk’uko twabibonye, ​​amahera amaze imyaka ibihumbi ari ikintu gihambaye cane mu bantu. Yaradufashije kugura ibintu n’ibikorwa, yaradushoboje gucuruzanya, kandi yaradufashije mu kubika ubutunzi.


Ariko uko ikibano cagenda kiratera imbere, ni ko n’ubucuti dufitaniye n’amahera bwahindutse. Kuva ku biceri gushika ku mafaranga y’impapuro no ku makonti ya banki y’ubuhinga bwa none gushika ku Bitcoin, amahera yacu yabwirijwe kujana n’ibihe.


Mu myaka mirongo iheze, internet yarahinduye cane uburyo dukorana, kandi amahera yacu yategerezwa gutera imbere iruhande rwayo. Amafaranga y’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none, nka Bitcoin, yaraserutse, kandi naho yarakunzwe cane kandi agatanga umuhango ku bacitse intege n’uburyo bwacu bw’amahera bwo muri iki gihe, yaragaragaje kandi aho amabanki ya kera afise aho agarukira.


Kubera ko Bitcoin ari ubuhinga bwa digitale, yama yuguruye ku bucuruzi, ikora amasaha 24 ku musi, imisi 365 ku mwaka, abantu bakagura no kugurisha buri segonda y’umusi wose. Hagati aho, hari abantu benshi cane kw’isi yose badashobora kuronka ubufasha bwo mu mabanki. Ivyo ku ruhande, mbere n'igihe umuntu afise amahirwe yo "gushirwa mu banki", banki isanzwe ikora igice c'umusi, ikadusiga ahanini ku mbabazi z'amasaha yabo y'ibikorwa.


Biroroshe kwirengagiza ivyo bintu gushika utanguye gucapura imibare.


Ica mbere, [ica kane c’abantu kw’isi yose) c’abantu kw’isi yose babonwa ko batagira amabanki. Ivyo bisigura ko hari abantu barenga miliyaridi imwe badashobora gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none, n’ukuzigama ata nkomanzi.


Kandi ica kabiri, turavye ko hari amasaha 8760 ku mwaka kandi ko banki rusangi ikora gusa kuva isaha cumi n’imwe z’ijoro gushika isaha zitanu z’ijoro kuva ku wa mbere gushika ku wa gatandatu kandi igafunga ku misi y’Imana no ku misi mikuru, banki rusangi ikora gusa amasaha 2100 gusa ku mwaka. Ivyo ni 24% gusa vy’igihe!


Rero, hanze y’amamiliyaridi y’abantu badashobora kuronka amabanki n’amabanki yo kuri Internet adasaba imfashanyo, kuronka amahera neza kandi ku gihe biracari ingorane kuri benshi.


Ikibi kuruta, kiretse dufashe amahera, amahera yacu yose arashikirwa n’ingorane z’amabanki ya kera. Ivyo biratera ingorane nyinshi iyo Leta yacu itegetse ivugurura ry’amabanki ry’agahomerabunwa, nk’uko vyabonetse mu gihe Leta y’Ubugiriki yariko irasenyuka mu 2015.


Muri ico gihe c’amagorwa, amabanki yarafunzwe, amahera yakurwa mu ma ATM yari ageze ku madolari 67 gusa ku musi, kandi inyuma y’ivyo vyose, Leta yaracariko irakura [igice] kinini (https://cointelegraph.com/news/greek-banks-deposit-yo-gukura-amahera-mu-mabanki-y’abaguzi-babo-ku giti cabo. ukutagira inshingano.


Naho amahera yoshobora gutanga umuti w’ingorane nk’izo, kwizigira amahera y’umubiri mw’isi aho gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none ari ngombwa si umuti w’igihe kirekire.


Ivyo bituma haba ikibazo: Kubera ko hariho ukutumvikana n’amabanki ya kera be n’uko uguhinduka kw’igihe gito kwa Bitcoin gushobora kubonwa nk’intambamyi ku bafise amahera make bazigamye, twoshobora gute gukorana n’abandi mu buryo butekanye mu gihe c’ubuhinga bwa none tutahanganye n’ivyo bibazo n’ivyo bibazo?


Turakeneye amafaranga aboshe ku kintu c’agaciro gatoyi, gifise ubuhinga bwa digitale kandi kiboneka igihe cose tuyakeneye, tutaravye isaha canke umusi w’indwi.


Kandi aha niho Tether yinjira.


#### None Teteri ni nde?


Mu bijanye n’uguhinduka kw’amafaranga y’amahera, Tether yaraserutse nk’umukinyi w’agaciro, arongowe n’iyerekwa ryo Address ivyipfuzo vy’amahera vy’isi ya none. Uko amafaranga y’imigenzo aguma arwana no kujana n’ivyo ubutunzi bwacu bw’isi yose bugenda burahinduka vuba, kandi uguhinduka kw’igihe gito kwa Bitcoin gutuma bigorana abatagira ubushobozi bwo kuzigama, abashinze Tether baremeye akaryo ko gukorana n’izo si.


Tether ni "umuhungabanya uburyo busanzwe bw'ivy'ubutunzi kandi ni umurongozi mu gukoresha amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none." Intumbero yabo nyamukuru ni ugutuma Bitcoin yemerwa mu guhuza isi y'ivy'ubutunzi n'isi y'ubuhinga bwa none ya Bitcoin. Ivyo babishikako biciye mu gutanga ibimenyetso bitandukanye vy’ubuhinga bwa none, akenshi vyitwa “stablecoins,” bifise agaciro kubera umugozi wavyo—nta n’akajambo k’uruyeri bigenewe—ku bintu vyo mw’isi y’umubiri. Tether kandi ishiramwo amafaranga muri Bitcoin Mining, uburezi bwa Bitcoin, ibikorwa remezo vyo kwishura Bitcoin, n’ubushakashatsi n’iterambere ry’ubuhinga bwa Bitcoin.


#### Igiceri gikomeye ni iki?


Stablecoins, nk’uko twabibonye haruguru, ni ibimenyetso vy’ubuhinga bwa none vyagenewe kuguma bifise agaciro kadahinduka ku bijanye n’ikintu amasoko y’ubu yemera ko gifise agaciro, nk’inzahabu canke amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none nk’idolari ry’Amerika. Batanga uruvange rw’izo si zompi - ibiranga ukwizigama kw’ubuhinga bwa none kwa Bitcoin, n’imiburiburi ku rugero runaka, n’ugushikama kw’igiciro c’igihe gito c’amahera ya kera.


Tether’s Stablecoins, nka USDt, ishigikiwe n’amadolari y’Amerika, canke XAUt, ishigikiwe n’inzahabu, itanga akamaro kadasanzwe ku mafaranga asanzwe kuko akora yigenga, hanze y’intambamyi z’amasaha y’amabanki asanzwe n’imipaka. Ivyo bituma umuntu ashobora kuyaronka 24/7, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kugenzura cane amahera yiwe no guhindura uko abona ibintu.


Ivyo bishitse mu muzirikanyi, abantu barashobora gukorana n’abandi ku buryo bwabo bwite, ataco bafatiye ku kuba banki yabo yuguruye, kandi barashobora kuronka urugero rw’umutekano uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki budashobora guhura na bwo. Iyo habayeho ivugurura ry’amabanki ryategetswe na Leta, nk’iryo mu Bugiriki mu 2015, amafaranga adahinduka arashobora gutanga uburyo bwo kwirinda ingorane zijanye n’uko amahera yawe aguma mu nzira za kera z’amabanki. Iyo umuntu akoresheje amafaranga adahinduka, arashobora kuguma afise ububasha ku mahera yiwe, mbere no mu bihe bidatomoye.


#### Ni gute amashikanwa ya stablecoin ya Tether atandukanye n’amahera ya Bitcoin canke fiat?


Udakunze Bitcoin, agaciro kayo, ku nyungu canke ku kaga k’uwuyifise, gashobora guhinduka cane mu gihe gito, amafaranga atandukanye ya Tether, nk’uko izina ribivuga, agerageza gutanga ugushikama kw’igihe gito mu gaciro. Ivyo bituma baba uburyo bwiza bwo gufatanya isi ya kera y’amafaranga ya fiat n’isi iguma ihinduka ya Bitcoin mu guha abakoresha ubushobozi bwo kwinjira no kuva muri Bitcoin batasubiye ku nzira za kera z’amabanki, ikintu kidashoboka imbere ya Tether.


Kugira ngo ivyo bishoboke, Tether irakora vyose kugira ngo token yose y’ubuhinga bwa none ishigikirwe n’ingwati (hamwe n’izina ryayo), kandi amafaranga yo gucuruza arashobora kworoha biciye ku buryo butandukanye bwo gukorana n’abandi, harimwo n’ama blockchains y’ayandi mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none. Ivyo bituma habaho uguserukira abantu mu mucyo kandi ntihagire nkenerwa y’abahuza nk’amabanki. Ivyo ntibituma gusa abafise internet bashobora gukoresha ibikorwa vya banki, ariko bituma umuntu ashobora gukora amafaranga yihuta kandi ataco atwara, ashobora gukorwa 24/7, imisi 365 mu mwaka, ata kuraba amasaha y’amabanki asanzwe canke imisi mikuru.


Amaze kuvuga ivyo, stablecoins zitangwa na Tether, nka USDt, na zo nyene ziratandukanye n’amahera ya fiat ya kera. Naho baguma bafise agaciro k’itunga nk’amadolari y’Amerika, si amafaranga asohorwa na Leta kandi nta budahemuka bafise ku gihugu na kimwe. Ico kiranga kibaha akamaro kadasanzwe, cane cane mu bihugu bihanganye n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro, aho kuronka amafaranga ahamye nk’amadolari y’Amerika bishobora kuba bigoye. Mu buryo butandukanye n’amahera y’umubiri, kuronka USDt canke ibindi bice vy’amahera bihoraho biciye ku rubuga rwa Exchange bisaba gusa ko umuntu akoresha interineti, bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kuyaronka ataravye aho aba. Rero, itandukaniro nyamukuru hagati y’amahera atandukanye ya fiat n’aya Tether riri mu kutagira ico bitaho kw’ubutungane: ikora ata nkomanzi hirya no hino y’imipaka, igatuma isi yose ishobora kuronka amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none ashikamye. Ikindi kandi, stablecoins zitanga inyungu nk’ugugabanya amafaranga y’ugucuruza, ugucuruza vyihuta kujabuka imipaka, n’ugushiramwo amafaranga menshi, bikaba bituma ari uburyo bwiza bwo gusubirira amafaranga y’agaciro ya kera.


#### Ni ubwoko bungahe butandukanye bw’ibiceri bihoraho?


Inyuma y’aho Tether iza, ayandi mashirahamwe menshi n’imigambi myinshi yaratanguje ibintu bisa n’ivyo vya Stablecoin. Ivyo bigeragezo vyinshi bishobora gushirwa mu bwoko butatu nyamukuru: amafaranga ashigikiwe na fiat, ashigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa, n’amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none.



- Ivyuma bikomeye bishigikiwe na Fiat**, nka USDt ya Tether, bishigikiwe n’amafaranga y’agaciro nk’idolari ry’Amerika canke Euro, kandi agaciro kavyo karaboshe ata guca ku ruhande n’agaciro k’amahera ya fiat ashingiyeko.
- Ibiceri bishigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa** bishigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa nk’inzahabu canke amavuta, ni ukuvuga, ibiceri bikomeye vy’inzahabu vya Tether, XAUt,
- Ivyuma bikomeye vy’ubuhinga** vyishingikiriza ku mategeko canke ubuhinga kugira ngo bigumye bifise agaciro. Ivyo bivuzwe, turacariko turabona stablecoin y’ubuhinga bwa algorithme gusa ishobora kuroranirwa mw’isoko.


Mu gusozera, uko igihugu cacu gikomeza gutera imbere kandi ubuhinga butera imbere, ni ko n’ubucuti dufitaniye n’amahera butera imbere. Kuva ku biceri gushika ku mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none, twabonye uguhinduka mu buryo dukorana n’amahera no mu kuntu tuyakoresha. Naho uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki bufise aho bugarukira, Tether, biciye mu guhitamwo kwayo stablecoin, itanga umuti ushoboka w’izo ngorane. Mu gutanga ugushikama kw’igihe gito kw’amafaranga y’agaciro n’uguhinduranya no kuronka amafaranga y’ivya kera, amafaranga yabo ashikamye atanga abakoresha ububasha bwinshi ku mafaranga yabo. Waba udashobora kuronka ibikorwa vya banki, uhanganye n’ugushikirwa na Leta canke ukeneye gusa gukorana hanze y’amasaha ya kera y’amabanki, stablecoins nka USDt zishobora kuguha ubundi buryo bwo kwizigirwa. Ivyo bituma vyihuta kuba igice nyamukuru c’urutonde rwacu rw’ivy’ubutunzi.


_**Iciyumviro co ku ruhande:** Ntuhagarike umutima nimba amwe muri aya majambo adafise insiguro nziza. Tuzokwihweza buri nsiguro mu buryo burambuye muri iki kiganiro cose._


## Amateka y'ibiceri bikomeye


<chapterId>174e2cab-ef14-5e14-99c8-8457b6fc5fee</chapterId>


Stablecoins zacitse ikiganiro gikundwa cane mw’isi y’amahera y’amahera, zitanga uburyo butari bwinshi bwo guhinduka mu gihe gito ku mafaranga y’amahera nka Bitcoin. Nk’uko vyavuzwe mu ntangamarara y’iki kiganiro, stablecoins ni itunga ry’ubuhinga bwa none rifatanye n’itunga ridahinduka nk’amahera ya fiat canke ivyuma vy’agaciro, vyagenewe kuguma bifise agaciro kadahinduka. Reka rero twihweze amateka y’ibiceri vy’amahera bikomeye maze twihweze neza bimwe mu biceri bikomeye vya mbere, harimwo na Tether’s USDt, ibiceri bikomeye bizwi cane kandi bikoreshwa cane.


_**Ikintu giteye umunezero:** Igihe iki kinyamakuru candika, USDt ya Tether igera kuri \$20 miliyaridi mu bijanye n’amahera akoreshwa ku musi. Ivyo birenze igitigiri ca Bitcoin iherutse gukoresha ku musi c’amadolari 15 miliyaridi. Ikindi, USDt yicaye mu kibanza ca gatatu ku bijanye n’isoko rinini inyuma ya Bitcoin na Ethereum._


Iciyumviro c’amahera akomeye kiva mu misi ya mbere y’amahera y’amahera, n’iciyumviro c’amahera y’amahera akomeye ashigikiwe n’itunga ryashikirijwe mu 2012 n’umugambi wa Mastercoin. Ariko rero, haciye imyaka mikeyi niho stablecoins zaronka inguvu, n’imigambi nka Bitshares na NuBits yatanguye mu 2014.


Bitshares yashizeho stablecoin ya mbere yitwa “bitUSD,” yari igenewe gufatwa n’idolari ry’Amerika, agaciro ka bitUSD imwe kaguma kangana n’idolari rimwe ry’Amerika. Ivyo vyasobanura ko bitUSD yashigikiwe n’amadolari y’Amerika yari mu bubiko, bikaba vyatuma agaciro kayo kaguma gashikamye mu bihe vy’uguhinduka kw’isoko. Ku rundi ruhande, NuBits yakoresheje Supply n’ubuhinga bwo gusaba kugira ngo igumye iri ku rugero rwayo ku dolari y’Amerika. Ariko ivyo tuzobivuga mu kigabane gikurikira.


Naho ivyo vyageragejwe mbere, niho Tether’s USDt yatangura mu 2014 niho stablecoins zaronka ivyiyumviro vyinshi. USDt, nka bitUSD, ni stablecoin igenewe gufatwa n’idolari ry’Amerika, agaciro ka USDt imwe kangana n’idolari rimwe ry’Amerika. USDt yaremewe n’ishirahamwe ryitwa Tether Limited, ishirahamwe ryaryo ry’umuvyeyi na ryo nyene rifise amafaranga y’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none yitwa Exchange Bitfinex.


Mu ntango, Tether yakoreshwa cane cane n’abacuruzi kugira ngo bashire amahera hagati y’amahinguriro ataco bakeneye guhindura mu mafaranga y’amahera. Ariko rero, uko abantu benshi batangura gukoresha Tether, ni ko yaronse inkomezi zayo bwite kandi irakundwa cane. Ubu, Tether ni stablecoin ikoreshwa cane kw’isi yose, ikora amadolari arenga \30 miliyaridi ku musi. Kugira ngo ushire uwo mubare mu buryo bubereye, [MasterCard](https://www.cardrates.com/advice/umubare-w'inguzanyo-ku musi-umwaka/#:~:umwandiko=4%20miliyaridi%20inguzanyo%20yari%20yatunganijwe,a%20%inguzanyo y'Ikiyapani%2) [Visa](https://urubuga.ubucuruzi-bumwe.com/gukora-24000-ibikorwa-vya-visa-ku-segonda-ingene-bikora e/#:~:text=VisaNet%2C%20ikarita%20y'urubuga%20yishura,24%2C000%20Visa%20ibikorwa%20ku%20segonda.) igikorwa, ku [mwayeni](https://www.statista.com/imibare/279249/ugugura-ibikorwa-ku-makarita-y'intumbero-rusangi-isi yose/), \amadolari 8,1 miliyaridi na \amadolari 12 miliyaridi ku musi, hakurikijwe uko bigenda. Mu vy’ukuri, 50% vy’amadolari y’Amerika akoreshwa ku musi ku musi ku USDt kurusha Visa na Mastercard vyose hamwe.


Naho Tether ikoreshwa cane, ntiyigeze igira impaka. Mu mwaka w’2017, Tether na BitFinex, zompi zifise iFinex Inc, zagirijwe ko zatumye igiciro ca Bitcoin kiduga. Ivyo birego vyari bifitaniye isano n’ikirego c’uko Tether na BitFinex zariko zitanga amafaranga mashasha y’amadolari y’Amerika ata madolari y’Amerika angana n’ayo zifise yo kuyashigikira. Ivyo vyokwongerera Supply ya USDt, iyo na yo ikaba yakoreshejwe mu gutuma igiciro ca Bitcoin kiduga mu buryo bw’ubuhinga.


Tether yagumye ahakana ivyo birego. Nkako, igenzura ryigenga ryakozwe mu 2017 ntiryabonye ikimenyamenya c’ukugerageza guhindura ibiciro. Ikindi kandi, zirikana iki: iyo Bitfinex ifise umugambi wo gukoresha USD bisa n’aho ataco iri kugira ngo yongere agaciro ka Bitcoin mu buryo bw’ubuhinga kandi itere imbere agaciro kayo bwite, ntivyoba vyoroshe kubigira mu bwiherero kandi bihakanwa mu makonti yayo bwite y’imbere mu gihugu, bikaba bituma gutahura bigorana cane kugereranywa na GW3. USDt?


Ariko rero, abayinegura baracariko baribaza nimba Tether ifise amadolari y’Amerika ahagije yo gushigikira USDt yose iriko irakoreshwa. Kugira ngo Address ivyo bibazo no kwongera uguseruka, Tether ubu isohora raporo z’ububiko bw’amahera zikorwa n’ishirahamwe mpuzamakungu ry’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga BDO. Izo raporo zitanga amakuru arambuye yerekeye amafaranga Tether yazigamye. Naho bamwe bakigira amakenga ku migenzo ya Tether yo gucungera amafaranga, utwigoro iyo sosiyete igira two gutuma habaho uguseruka kwafashije mu kwubaka ukwizigirana n’abakoresha bayo be n’abanyagihugu benshi bakoresha amafaranga y’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none.


Ivyo bivuzwe, mu gihe c’izo mpaka n’ibibazo ku bijanye n’ibizigamirwa vyayo, USDt yarashoboye kuguma ihagaze neza kw’igiciro kuva yatanguye. Ivyo vyatumye iguma ari yo stablecoin izwi cane kw’isoko, mbere n’aho hari n’izindi nyinshi zaserutse zigahiganwa kugira ngo zironke umugabane w’isoko. Muri iki gihe, hariho amafaranga menshi cane adahinduka, imwe yose ikaba ifise uburyo bwayo bwihariye bwo kuguma ifise agaciro kadahinduka.


Ikindi kandi, uko isoko ry’amahera y’agaciro ryagenda rirakura, Tether yaraguye aho ishika kugira ngo igere ku vyo abantu basaba. Mu ntango, Tether yatanga gusa USDt kuri Bitcoin Blockchain ikoresheje “metaprotocol” ya Omni, ariko uko isoko ryakura kandi ibibazo bijanye n’uguhindura On-Chain bikagenda biragaragara, yaratanguye [gutanga] Algorand, n’abandi. Uyu musi, hariho ubushakashatsi n’iterambere bikomeye vyo kwongera amahera ya Tether ku Bitcoin, biciye ku [RGB] (https://www.rgbfaq.com/faq/ico-ari-RGB) na [Pear Inguzanyo](https://tether.to/ru/inguzanyo-y’imbogo-n’ijambo-rimwe-ri-gutanguza-inguzanyo-y’amapera-inguzanyo-ya-P2P-uburyo-bw’inguzanyo/). Tether kandi yashizeho ibintu bishasha vy’amahera y’agaciro bishingiye ku mafaranga atandukanye nk’ama euro, yen, n’ama yuan y’abashinwa.


Mu gusozera, stablecoins zaje kure cane kuva zatanguye. Kuva mu misi ya mbere ya bitUSD na NuBits gushika ku gukundwa cane kw’ibicuruzwa vya Tether no ku guseruka kw’izindi stablecoins, isoko rya stablecoin ryarateye imbere cane. Naho impaka zikikuje Tether zatumye habaho ivyiyumviro ku bijanye n’uguseruka no kubazwa n’abatanga amafaranga, isoko ry’amafaranga riguma rikura, ritanga ikiraro c’isi yose kandi gishobora guhinduka kuri Bitcoin. Ariko rero, ivyo vyiza biza bivuye ku kwongerekana kw’ugushira hamwe no kwizigira ukwizigirana.


## Ibirango vy'ibiceri bikomeye


<chapterId>21765df7-53fd-58af-9df6-7208027a0c3a</chapterId>


Nk’uko bikwiye kugaragara ubu, stablecoin ni ubwoko bwa token bwa digitale bwagenewe kuguma bufise agaciro gakomeye bushingiye kuri pegged asset iri munsi yayo. Ivyo bintu bishobora kubamwo amafaranga y’agaciro, ivyuma vy’agaciro, ibicuruzwa, canke ivyo vyose bihurikiye hamwe (nk’igiseke c’amafaranga y’agaciro).


Intumbero y’igiceri gikomeye, nka USDt, ni ugutanga ububiko bw’agaciro buhamye cane ugereranije n’uguhinduka kw’amahera atari ayandi mafaranga y’amahera gusa ariko n’ayandi mafaranga y’amahera nk’ipeso ya Argentine, yatakaje [97%](https://www.statista.com/statistics/316750/ hagati y’umwaka wa 2012 n’uwa 2022.


Mu vy’ukuri, stablecoin ikora nk’ikiraro hagati y’itunga rya kera na Bitcoin, igatuma abakoresha bashobora gukorana n’ukwizigira kwinshi kandi bashobora kumenya imbere y’igihe.


Naho ingene bagumya igiciro, reka turabe...


Ivyinshi mu bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none (stablecoins) akenshi bihitamwo gukoresha amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none nk’ibara ryavyo, idolari ry’Amerika rikaba ari rimwe mu mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none azwi cane umuntu ashobora gukoresha. Kubera iyo mpamvu, tuzobanza kwisuka mu bice vy’amahera bishigikiwe na fiat. Ariko rero, hari ubwoko bwinshi bw’amahera agumaho, nk’ayo ashigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa n’ayo ashingiye ku buhinga bwa algorithme, na yo nyene tuzoyitohoza.


### Fiat-Ishigikiwe


Stablecoins zigenewe kuguma zifise agaciro gakomeye ugereranije na pegged asset. Ku bijanye n’amahera ashigikiwe na fiat, nka USDt, uburyo bworoshe bwo gutuma token iguma ifise agaciro ni uko uwutanga token afata amafaranga token ishinzweko mu kigereranyo ca 1:1.


Bimeze nk’ibitera urujijo gatoyi? Ntutinye. Aha niho akarorero:


Twibaze ko ufise \$50 US kandi ushaka kohereza ayo mahera abagenzi n'umuryango wawe ukoresheje USDt. Kugira ngo utangure iyo nzira, winjira muri Exchange yawe yo kuri internet maze ugacuruza amadolari yawe \$50 y'Amerika ku \$50 USDt. Ariko rero, iyi Exchange ntiyishura gusa \$50 USDt nshasha. Ahubwo, mu bihe bitandukanye, iyo amafaranga y’amadolari y’Amerika ya Exchange agabanutse, uwutanga, muri iki gihe, Tether, atanga amadolari mashasha y’amadolari y’Amerika (USDt) ya Exchange mu gusubiza amadolari y’Amerika. USD irashigikira ivyo bimenyetso bishasha vyaremwe vya USDt. Ivyo bituma buri \$1 USDt igendagenda ishigikirwa n’amahera angana n’ayo canke amahera angana n’ayo.


Ivyo ubifise mu muzirikanyi, iyo uronse USDt, si igitabu gishasha. Ahubwo, mu gihe c'imbere, Exchange yahinduye USD ku USDt, ubu uriko uraronka kuri Exchange. Uko igihe kigenda kirarenga kandi abakoresha benshi bagura USDt, amafaranga Exchange ifise aragabanuka mu gihe amafaranga afise USD agenda aragwira. Ivyo bituma Exchange yongera kuvugana na Tether ku generate USDt y’inyongera mu Exchange ku USD.


Ubu buryo bwo "gushigikira" amafaranga y'ibiceri n'ububiko bw'itunga bugenewe gutanga ugushikama n'ukwizigira abakoresha, kuko bituma agaciro k'ibiceri bigumye kaboshe n'itunga rigaragara. Mu gihe umuntu wese afise USDt yofata ingingo yo Exchange ibimenyetso vyiwe ku madolari y’Amerika, amafaranga Tether afise akwiye kuba ahagije kugira ngo ashobore gupfuka ivyo asaba no kubuza gutakaza agaciro k’amadolari y’Amerika.


None, birabereye kumenya ko amafaranga yose agumaho ataremwe angana. Bimwe, mu bijanye n’imikorere, bikora mu buryo butandukanye, mu gihe ibindi bishobora kuba bifise ingero zitandukanye z’ugushingira intahe canke kwegereza ubutegetsi, ivyo bikaba bishobora kugira ico bikoze ku gushikama kwavyo no kwizigirwa nk’ububiko bw’agaciro. Utitaye kuri ivyo, bose bariko baragerageza gushika ku ciyumviro kimwe: igiciro gikomeye.


Naho vyinshi muri ivyo bigo bigenzurwa cane kandi bikagenzurwa kugira ngo bimenyekane ko ari ivyo kwizigirwa, iyo nzira y’ugushira hamwe irashobora gutera ingorane.


Nk’akarorero, kuko izo stablecoins zidashingiye ku muntu azitanga gusa ariko kandi zishingiye ku bigo vy’imari kugira ngo zicunge amafaranga afise mu bibanza vy’ububiko, iyo imwe muri izo nzego ishobora kunanirwa, hariho ubushobozi bwo kugabanya agaciro k’izo stablecoin kandi abantu bose bagatakaza icizigiro ku muntu azitanga.


Rimbura USDC, igice ca kabiri gikundwa cane inyuma ya USDt. Igihe banki ya Silicon Valley [yasenyuka] muri Ntwarante 2023, USDC yaratakaje mu gihe gitoyi igiciro cayo ca 1:1 ku madolari y’Amerika, maze icuruzwa ku giciro gito cane c’amadolari y’Amerika. [\$0.88](ivy'amahera y'amahera y'amahera y'amahera). Ivyo ni ugutakaza 12% vy’ubushobozi bwo kugura mw’ijoro rimwe, ivyo bikaba bihangayikishije ku kintu gishaka guhagarara neza mu giciro.

Impamvu y’ivyo biciro ni uko Circle, itanga USDC, yari yabitse igice c’amahera yayo muri banki ya Silicon Valley. Ivyo vyatumye abantu bafata, batangura kugurisha amafaranga yabo ya USDC kubera ubwoba bw’uko Circle itazoshobora kwubahiriza ibisabwa vyose vyo gucungura. Amahirwe kuri Circle, ni uko ikigo ca Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika n’Ishirahamwe ry’Ubwishingizi bw’Ibizigamirwa (FDIC) vyavyifashemwo maze bitanga ingwati ku bizigamirwa vyose vya banki. Ivyo vyasobanura ko Circle itazotakaza amafaranga yayo, kandi USDC ica yihuta gusubira ku \$1. Ariko rero, vyari gushobora guca mu yindi nzira bitagoranye, bikasiga USDC ari ikisigazwa ca kahise. Ivyo ubifise mu muzirikanyi, birahambaye gukora ubushakashatsi ku mahera atandukanye ashobora gukoreshwa imbere yo guhitamwo gushiramwo amahera canke gucuruza.


Naho hariho izo nkeka, amafaranga menshi yizigirwa ashigikiwe na fiat. Ivyuma nka Tether’s USDt bikoresha ubu buryo bwo gushigikira kandi bihora bigenda \$5 miliyaridi canke birenze ku musi.


Reka noneho turabe ubwoko bukurikira bw'amahera y'agaciro...


### Ibicuruzwa-Bishigikiwe


Nka kurya kw’ibiceri bishigikiwe na fiat, ibiceri bishigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa biratuma ibintu bifatika bibonwa ko bifise agaciro mw’isi y’umubiri bishobora kwinjira mw’isi y’ubuhinga bwa none.


Ariko rero, bitandukanye n’amahera ashigikiwe na fiat, yizigira amahera ya Leta nk’infashanyo, amafaranga ashigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa akoresha itunga nk’ivyuma vy’agaciro, amafaranga y’ubutunzi canke mbere n’amazu.


Ku bijanye n’igiceri gikomeye gishigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa, uwugitanga, mu bisanzwe afatanije n’ikigo c’ivy’imari, yoronka ivy’umubiri, akabigumya nk’ibizigamirwa mu gihe atanga ibiceri bikomeye bingana n’agaciro k’ivyo bintu. Uwufise stablecoin arashobora rero gucuruza ibimenyetso vyiwe ataco akeneye gukorana n’umutungo w’umubiri canke, mu bihe bimwebimwe, Exchange ibimenyetso vyiwe ku kintu c’umubiri iyo bikenewe.


[Inzahabu ya Tether](https://inzahabu.tether.to/) (XAUt) ni akarorero k’igiceri gikomeye gishigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa aho Tether ifata ounce imwe y’inzahabu y’inzahabu ku token yose isohotse. Ivyo bituma igiciro caco kigenda kijanye n’igiciro c’ikintu gishingiyeko, muri iki gihe... inzahabu.


Ikintu gishimishije kumenya kuri XAUt ni uko abafise token bashobora gukurikirana inzahabu iyo sosiyete ifise kugira ngo habeho uguseruka, bagabanye inyifato mbi iyo ari yo yose. Ikindi kandi, barashobora Redeem ibimenyetso vyabo vy’inzahabu igihe cose, bikaba bitanga umutekano wongereweko n’uguhinduranya.


Mu bijanye n’ivyo, muri Exchange ku bijanye n’ingorane nyinshi z’abagenzi, XAUt itanga inyungu nyinshi ku nzahabu y’umubiri.


Ica mbere, XAUt itanga uburyo bworoshe kandi bushikira bwo gushiramwo amahera mu nzahabu, kuko ari ivy’ubuhinga bwa none kandi bishobora gucuruzwa no kubikwa mu buryo bworoshe mu bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Ivyo bituma ata nkenerwa yo kubika ibintu vy’umubiri be n’amahera yo gutwara inzahabu y’umubiri.


Ubwa kabiri, rituma habaho Ownership y’ibice, ivyo bikaba bituma abashoramari bashobora kugura inzahabu ntoyi cane.


**Kubera iki umuntu yoshobora gushaka ivyo?** Mw'isi y'umubiri, kugura ounce yose y'inzahabu ku \$1900 vyoba ari ukudashobora gushika kuri benshi. Ariko 1/1000th y’inzahabu ubu irashikwako biciye mu gucapura ibimenyetso. Mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwa none, kwitwaza ko umuntu afise inzahabu Dust birashoboka—ikintu kidashoboka mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwa none.


Ubwa nyuma, XAUt akenshi iba ari Liquid kuruta inzahabu y’umubiri, ivyo bisigura ko ishobora guhindurwa bitagoranye ikaba fiat canke Bitcoin, bikaba bituma abashoramari bashobora gusesa vuba amafaranga yabo iyo bikenewe.


Ariko rero, nk’uko nyene amafaranga ashigikiwe na fiat, amafaranga ashigikiwe n’ibicuruzwa yizigira ikigo kimwe ku bikorwa vyayo, ivyo bikaba bituma ashobora gushikirwa n’intege nke nyene. Ikindi, izo stablecoins zitegerezwa gufata mu muzirikanyi ibiciro vyo kubika kuko ibintu vy’umubiri nk’inzahabu n’amazu bifata umwanya. Ku bw’ivyo, ukwiye kwitega ko uzoriha amahera makeyi kubera iyo nsiguro.


Reka noneho turabe uburyo bwa gatatu bw'amahera y'agaciro...


### Ubuhinga


Igiceri gikomeye c’ubuhinga bwa algorithme ni ubwoko bwa nyuma bw’igiceri gikomeye tuzovugako kandi, nk’ibindi, gigenewe kuguma gifise agaciro kadahinduka.


Mu buryo butandukanye n’ibindi biceri bikomeye bishigikiwe n’ibintu vy’umubiri, ibiceri bikomeye vy’ubuhinga bwa algorithme bikoresha amafomula canke ubuhinga bw’imibare—kenshi bifatanijwe n’ibintu bimwebimwe—kugira ngo bitunganye Supply yavyo mu bijanye n’ivyo bisabwa kugira ngo igiciro kigume gishikamye.


Ku batazi ijambo algorithm, urashobora kwiyumvira ko algorithm ari amategeko gusa akwiye gukurikizwa. Ivyo bishobora kumvikana nk’ibitera urujijo, rero reka turabe ubwoko bumwe bw’uburyo bwo gushikama kw’ubuhinga bwa algorithme, bwitwa uburyo bwa rebase, nk’akarorero.


Reka tuvuge ko dusohora igiceri gishasha c'ubuhinga citwa AlgoCoin gikoresha uburyo bwo gusubiramwo kugira ngo igiciro kibe \$1. Mu gihe nk’ico, AlgoCoin yoca ihindura ubwo nyene Supply y’ibimenyetso kugira ngo igiciro kigume gishikamye. Ivyo vyoshikwako mu kwongera canke kugabanya Supply y’ibimenyetso bishingiye ku mpinduka y’igiciro ca token.


Iyo igiciro ca AlgoCoin kiba hejuru ya \$1, iyo algorithm yokwongerera Supply y'ibimenyetso, igabanura neza igiciro ca token yose. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo igiciro ca AlgoCoin cari munsi ya \$1, iyo porotokole yoshobora kugabanya Supply y'ibimenyetso kugira ngo yongere igiciro ca token yose.


Ubwo buryo bwotuma igiciro ca AlgoCoin kiguma gihagaze mu gihe kirekire mu gihe kiguma cemera uguhinduka kw’ivyo isoko risaba.


Ubu, birahambaye kumenya ko kugabanya Supply igendagenda ya token, nk’akarorero, mu kuyigura ubwayo ku giciro c’isoko canke mu gusenya Supply zimwe zimwe n’amahera canke amafaranga yo kubika, vyose ataco bibangamiye akamaro kayo kandi rero n’ivyo isaba, si ikintu gitoyi nk’uko bishobora gusa n’ibisanzwe. Iyo amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa algorithme yizigiye amategeko agoranye kugira ngo agume afise igiciro gikomeye, ivyo bituma ashobora gushikirwa n’ingorane z’ubuhinga n’ivy’amahera. Ivyo, iyo ukurikije ikibanza, birakoreshwa ubudasiba.


Muri Rusama 2022, abacuruzi bamwebamwe barakoresheje ubugoyagoye buri muri TerraUSD (UST), kimwe mu bice bikomeye vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Ivyo vyatumye agaciro ka UST kagabanuka cane kuva ku madolari 18,7 miliyaridi gushika munsi y’amadolari 100 miliyoni mu kwezi kumwe, ivyo bikaba bigereranya ugugabanuka guteye ubwoba [99,5%](https://www.coingecko.com/coins/terraclassicusd).


Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, naho amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none (algorithmic stablecoins) yaronse ukwitwararika kubera ubushobozi bwayo bwo guhindura uburyo twiyumvira ku bijanye n’agaciro gakomeye mw’isi y’ubuhinga bwa none, birahambaye kumenya ko akiri iciyumviro gishasha kandi ko yari afise ubushobozi bwo gutera ibibazo n’ubugoyagoye. Kubera ko ari igice gusa, canke rimwe na rimwe, bidashigikirwa n’ibintu vy’umubiri kandi bishingiye cane ku bategura n’ugukora amakode, hamwe n’ukugerageza gukomeye kw’ubuhinga bw’ivy’amahera, turahimiriza kwiyubara no gukora ubushakashatsi bwimbitse imbere yo gukoresha amafaranga yose y’ubuhinga bwa none.


Mu gusozera, stablecoins itanga ikiraro hagati y’isi ya kera na Bitcoin, bikaba bishoboka ko habaho uguhuza gutandukanye hagati y’ubusegaba n’ibikorwa. Naho hari ubwoko butatu nyamukuru bw’amahera y’agaciro—ayo ashigikiwe n’amahera y’agaciro, ivyuma vy’agaciro canke ubuhinga bwa algorithme—amahera y’agaciro ashigikiwe n’amahera y’agaciro ni yo akundwa cane.


Naho stablecoins akenshi zifatwa nk’izitekanye kubera kamere zazo “zidahinduka”, birahambaye kwibuka ko zidafise ingorane zose. Kubera ko stablecoins zishingiye ku batanga amafaranga, ni ukuvuga Tether, n’ibigo vy’imari, hariho ubushobozi bwo gutakaza. Kugira ngo ivyo bibazo bigabanuke, birahambaye cane ko umuntu akora ubushakashatsi bwimbitse ku bijanye n’amahera atandukanye agumaho imbere y’uko ashiramwo amahera. Niwabigenza gutyo, urashobora gufata ingingo uzi neza ibintu kandi ugagabanya ivyo woshobora gutakaza utavyiteze.


## Inyungu z’amashikanwa ya Tether


<chapterId>a6806b45-b92e-5791-8f5f-804098a522b2</chapterId>


Hura na Adanna, umugore akiri muto aba mu gisagara co mu misozi yo muri Afirika aho amafaranga CFA, yatakaje ubushobozi bwo kugura buteye ubwoba [99,5%] (https://bitcoinmagazine.com/culture/Bitcoin-a-faranga-y’ugukuraho ubukoloni) mu myaka 70 iheze, ibidashoboka.


Adanna yama akunda cane iciyumviro co kugira ububasha ku mahera yiwe, ariko vyagumye ari indoto idashoboka gushika ubu. Amafaranga akoresha agenzurwa n’abantu bagaragaje ko badafise inyungu z’abantu babo ku mutima, kandi aho aba mu ntara y’i burasirazuba bituma adashobora gukoresha amabanki. Ku bw’ivyo, Adanna nta kindi akora atari ukwizigira amahera y’umubiri, ivyo bikaba bimusiga ari mu kaga k’ubusuma n’ugutakaza uretse n’ugusenyuka kw’ubushobozi bwo kugura.


Ariko ivyo vyose ni vyo bihinduka.


Umusi umwe, umugenzi wiwe yamumenyesheje Bitcoin na USDt, ayo mafaranga mashasha y’ubuhinga bwa none akora ataco akora ku buryo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki. Naho Adanna yemera akamaro ka Bitcoin, ukuntu ihinduka biratera intambamyi. Kubera amahera makeyi azigamye be n’ingorane z’amahera afise, ubu ntabwo ari uburyo bushoboka kuri we. Ariko rero, akoresheje USDt, amenya ko adashobora gukoresha amadolari y’Amerika gusa, amahera ahagaze neza cane, ariko ko ashobora kwizigama amahera yiwe kandi, afise internet y’ishimikiro, ashobora gukorana n’umuntu uwo ari we wese aho ari ho hose ata na rimwe akeneye kuja mw’ishami rya banki.


Ivyo ni uguhindura urukino kuri Adanna. Kubera ko afise ubushobozi bwo kubika neza amahera yiwe no kuyaronka, ntagikeneye kwiganyira ku bijanye n’ingorane zijanye n’ugutwara amahera canke ugucika intege kw’agaciro k’amahera birenze urugero. Kandi ikiruta vyose, ubu arashobora kugura ibintu kuri Internet no kohereza amahera abo mu muryango wiwe bo mu bindi bice vyo muri Afirika ataco akora ku ngorane z’amabanki ya kera.


Uko abandanya gutohoza ubushobozi bw’amadolari y’Amerika, Adanna abona ko ubu buhinga bushobora guhindura ubuzima bw’abantu bari mu bihe nk’ivyo. Kubera USDt, umuntu wese arashobora kuronka umwidegemvyo w’amahera n’umutekano vyari bitari vyiza cane kuri benshi cane.


Ivyo ni bibiri gusa mu vyiza vyinshi bijanye n’amahera y’amahera, nka USDt:


1. **Ihitamwo ry’Ivy’Imari:** Stablecoins itanga akaryo ko guhindura ubuzima bw’abantu nka Adanna baba mu ntara z’ivyaro badashobora kuronka ubufasha bwo kwizigirwa bwa banki. Iyo umuntu afise internet y’ishimikiro, arashobora gukoresha amafaranga y’agaciro (stablecoins) kugira ngo ashobore kuronka amafaranga yihitiyemwo, nk’idolari ry’Amerika, maze ashobore guhunga amafaranga yabo yo mu gihugu ariko arasenyuka ningoga. Ivyo bisigura ko bashobora kugira ububasha bwinshi ku mahera yabo ata na rimwe bahagarika umutima ku bijanye n’ukudashikama kw’amahera.

2. **Banking the Unbanked:** Stablecoins zitanga umuti ukenewe ku bantu batagira amabanki, harimwo n’ababa mu turere twa kure canke bafise ingorane zo gufungura amakonti ya banki asanzwe. Mu gutuma umuntu ashobora kuronka amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none, amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none aratanga uburyo bwiza kandi bubereye bwo gukoresha amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none no kw’isi yose, bikaba biha ubushobozi abantu mbere batagira ayo mahirwe.

Rero, reka turabe ayandi mahirwe twahawe kuva Tether’s stablecoins zisohotse.


#### Amafaranga yoherezwa


Iyumvire gatoyi ko wavukiye kandi ukurira muri Tonga. Ariko uko ukunda igihugu cawe, ukiri muto, urabona ko mu karere iwanyu hariho akazi gatoyi. Rero, ukimara kwimuka, ufata ingingo yo kuva muri Tonga ukaja mu gihugu gifise akazi kenshi. Mu kubigira, ubu urashobora gufasha neza umuryango wawe igihe wohereje igice c’amahera y’umushahara wawe i muhira.


Naho ivyo bintu vyoshobora gusa n’ibidashoboka, mu vy’ukuri ni ukuri ku bantu amamiliyaridi bo kw’isi yose, na canecane abo muri Tonga. Kuva mu 2021, amahera yoherezwa, ni ukuvuga igikorwa co gusubiza amahera abakundwa kugira ngo bafashe, vyari bitangaje cane . [45.5%](https://www.ubutunzi bw'isi yose.com/Tonga/amafaranga_yoherezwa_ijana_jana_mu gihugu/#:~:text=Amahera yoherezwa%20nk'ijana%20 y'umudugudu wa20&text=Agaciro ka%20 ka%20ka%20ka%20Tonga,171%2020%60%20) Umusaruro wose w’igihugu ca Tonga (GDP).


Kumbure uriko uribaza uti: Ingorane iri hano ni iyihe?


Gusubiza amahera mu mahanga biciye ku nzira yo kohereza amahera nka Western Union si ubuntu. Bitwara amahera, kandi si make gusa, ni amahera menshi cane.


Kurungika \$100 y'Amerika muri Tonga bitera igiciro c'amadolari 12.61(\$12.61]() hamwe n'ibindi bihombo vy'amadolari 8.60 kubera igiciro kitari ciza ca Exchange. Ivyo bisigura ko amafaranga arenga 21% y’amahera yose yoherezwa aja muri Western Union, ishirahamwe ry’ibihugu vyinshi. Ivyo bituma amahera menshi cane yari gushobora kuba ari mu minwe y’imiryango y’Abanyatonga ibereye, ahera mu mifuko y’uwo mugwi utanga amahera.

Woba ushobora kwiyumvira ivyiza vyo kuronka 21% vy’inyongera ku mahera winjiza?


Ikindi kandi, turavye ko umusaruro w’igihugu ca Tonga wari [\$469](https://tradingeconomics.com/tonga/gdp) miliyoni mu 2021, kandi 45,5% vyawo biva ku mahera yoherezwa, amafaranga arenze urugero asabwa kugira ngo umuntu yohereze amahera mu gihugu bisigura ko Tonga ibura miliyoni y’inyongera\4. Ivyo bihembo vyohinduka 9,6% vy’ukwiyongera kw’umusaruro w’igihugu iyo hataba ayo mahera.


Kandi nimba wiyumvira ko Tonga ari yo yonyene muri ivyo, wongere wibaze.


Aha niho hari akarorero k’ingene Western Union [isaba] amahera yo kohereza \$100 y’amadolari y’Amerika mu bindi bihugu bimwebimwe bikomeye:



- Ubushinwa:** \$21.21 amafaranga + \$2.60 Exchange igiciro c'ugutakaza (23.81% y'ugutakaza)
- Canada, Amerika, Mexique:** \$16,86 amafaranga + \$1,20 Exchange igiciro c'ugutakaza (18,06% y'ugutakaza)
- Ubwongereza, Alubaniya, Bosniya, Seribiya, Siloveniya:** \$17,92 y’amahera + \$3,10 Exchange y’igiciro c’ugutakaza (21,02% y’ugutakaza)
- Oceanie na Aziya y’amajepfo:** \$12,61 y’amahera + \$8,60 Exchange igiciro c’ugutakaza (21,21% y’ugutakaza)

Aya ni amahera atangaje cane ubu ari mu maboko y’amashirahamwe akomeye yo muri Amerika. Kandi niho USDt yinjira, kuko itanga umuti w’ikibazo c’amahera menshi yo kohereza.


Udakunze ibikorwa vya kera vyo kohereza amafaranga, USDt ni amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none, ku ntumbero yo gukoresha, agenda ku nzira za Blockchain. Kubera ko bitasaba abahuza nk’amabanki canke abarungika amahera, amafaranga y’ugutanga ni make cane. Ikindi kandi, uko amafaranga akoreshwa kuri Blockchain ya bose, ivyo bituma habaho uguseruka cane be n’ubuzima bwite. Ivyo bisigura ko abantu bashobora kohereza amahera abo bakunda mu bindi bihugu hafi mu kanya nk’ako gukubita, ata nkomanzi, kandi ku giciro gito cane.


Nk’akarorero, USDt, ikora canecane ku nzira z’amabarabara za Ethereum na Tron, yaragize 1000. [\$1.02]( https://ycharts.com/ibimenyetso/amafaranga_asanzwe_y'ugucuruza#:~:umwandiko=Amahera y'ugucuruza%20 ni,20.90%25%20kuva%20mwe%20%20iheze.) [\$0.000005](https://bitpowr.com/blog/ingene-worungika-amafaranga-atari-mu-mafaranga-a-tron) amafaranga y’ugucuruza, hakurikijwe, mu mwaka uheze, ata kuraba amahera yoherejwe— amafaranga aguma ari imwe haba wohereje \$5 canke \0.0.000. Kandi uko tuvuga, abahinguzi bariko barakora ku [stablecoins](https://www.coindesk.com/tech] Bitcoin ya Lightning Network, iyo yobona amafaranga agera kuri [\$0.0003]


Hakoreshejwe USDt, Abanyatonga, hamwe n’abandi bose bohereje amahera mu miryango yabo, barashobora kuronka amahera menshi cane bohereje, ivyo bikaba bishobora gutuma ubuzima bwabo butera imbere cane, bigatuma ubutunzi bw’igihugu cabo butera imbere.


Reka turabe ingene amashikanwa ya Tether’s stablecoin atanga ugushikama ku baba mu bihe bidashikamye.


#### Gushikama


Nk’uko inkuru ya Adanna yerekanye, ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro ni ikintu kibabaje ku bantu batagira uko bangana kw’isi yose, canecane ababa mu bihugu bifise ubutunzi budashikamye.
