Ariko naho nyene ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro gukomeye kwari ingorane gusa mu bihugu biri mu nzira y’amajambere, mu myaka ibiri iheze, ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro kwariyongereye incuro zibiri mu bihugu biteye imbere. Ivyo bisigura ko, kuva mu kwezi kwa Gitugutu 2022, [81](https://www.visualcapitalist.com/mapped-ibihugu-bifise-ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro/) ubu biriko biratanga raporo y’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro kw’imirongo ibiri. Ivyo ni hafi igice c’ibihugu vyose bitanga raporo y’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro!


Kugira ngo tugaragaze ingaruka z’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro kw’imirongo ibiri, ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro kw’ibice 10%, nk’uko vyashikiye Uburayi mu kwezi kwa Gitugutu 2022, vyoba bisobanura ko ubushobozi bwo kugura butakaza 61,5% mu myaka cumi.


![image](assets/3.webp)


_**Igishushanyo:** Ingaruka z'Iterambere ry'Ibiciro ku Gugura [Ububasha](https://anilsaidso.gumroad.com/)_


Ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro ntigusiga gusa abantu amamiliyoni bagorwa no gukurikirana n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro vy’ibintu n’ibikorwa vya misi yose, ariko kandi biratuma ubushobozi bwabo bwo kugura bugabanuka, bigatuma bigorana cane kuzigama amahera yo gukoresha muri kazoza. Vyongeye, akenshi bitera cane abakene cane, harimwo imiryango ifise amahera make, abakukurutse bafise amahera adahinduka, be n’abantu badashobora kuronka amahera menshi.


Na none, aha ni ho amashikanwa ya Tether’s stablecoin ashobora gutuma habaho itandukaniro rikomeye.


Kubera ko amafaranga yabo agumaho ashingiye ku gaciro k’itunga ry’ishimikiro, nk’idolari ry’Amerika canke inzahabu, igiciro cabo kiragumaho ugereranije n’ayandi mafaranga ariko aratera imbere cane. Ivyo bituma zitanga uburyo bushoboka bwo gusubirira abantu baba mu bihugu bifise amahera adashikamye. Baha abo bantu uburyo bwo kwimurira amahera yabo mu mafaranga adashobora guterwa n’ibipimo vy’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro nk’ivyo mu mafaranga yabo yo mu gihugu. Ivyo birashobora kubafasha kuguma bafise agaciro k’amahera bazigamye no kwikingira ugusenyuka kw’ubushobozi bwo kugura bitewe n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro.


Ariko rero, ivyo biratuma umuntu yibaza ati: Bimeze gute igihe amafaranga nka Amerika ariko arashikirwa n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro?


Hejuru y’amadolari y’Amerika, Tether itanga XAUt—ishigikiwe n’inzahabu—itanga uburyo bukomeye kuruta ku bantu barondera guhunga ibiciro vy’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro.


Inzahabu yabaye ububiko bwizigirwa bw'agaciro mu binjana n'ibindi, bivuye ku kubura kwayo no ku gushikama kw'igiciro. Ariko rero, gushika ubu, ntivyari bishoboka gukoresha inzahabu nk’uburyo bwo kwishura biciye ku buhinga bwa none. XAUt, ishigikiwe n'inzahabu, itorera umuti ico kibazo mu gutanga uburyo bwo gucuruza mu nzahabu ataco ikeneye Ownership. Ivyo bituma abantu bashobora kurinda ubushobozi bwabo bwo kugura ataco bafatiye ku mafaranga yabo canke USD iriko irashikirwa n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro.


Ushobora kuvuga uti: Ariko none e-gold yo mu myaka ya 90?


Ica mbere, imiterere y’ibikorwa n’ububiko bwa eGold yari ihuriwe cane kandi ntiyari ifise uguserukira kw’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none nka XAUt. Ku bw’ivyo, haradutse amakenga ku bijanye n’inzahabu y’ukuri ishigikira ibimenyetso vya eGold.


Ubwa kabiri, eGold yatanguje igikorwa cayo mu kiringo isoko ry’amahera y’amahera ryari ritaratera imbere cane. Ku bw’ivyo, ryararwanye kugira ngo ryemerwe abantu benshi. Izo ngorane zose hamwe zatumye eGold ihura n’intambamyi zikomeye z’amategeko be n’ingorane z’amategeko, amaherezo bituma itemba.


Mu buryo bunyuranye, ibintu nka XAUt kuva ico gihe vyaranesheje izo ntambamyi, vyungukira ku mirongo ngenderwako y’amahera y’ibanga, ubukerebutsi bwaronswe mu kunanirwa kwa kera, na Commitment ku guseruka cane.


Ivyo bituma amafaranga y’inzahabu ashobora gukoreshwa neza kandi yizigirwa ku barondera gukingira ubutunzi bwabo ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro canke mu bihe vy’ukudatekana kw’ubutunzi.


Mu mpera, stablecoins itanga umuti ukomeye ku bantu baba mu bihugu bifise ukudatekana canke inflation nyinshi. Mu gutuma abantu bashobora kuronka amafaranga ahamye cane canke mu kwemera ko umuntu ashobora gukoresha amafaranga yiwe mu nzahabu, amafaranga ahamye aratanga uburyo bwo kurinda agaciro k’amahera bazigamye no guhunga ingaruka mbi z’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro. Uko abantu benshi bamenya ivyiza biva ku bice vy’amahera bihoraho, birashoboka ko ukumenyekana kwavyo kuzobandanya gukura nk’uburyo bwo gutanga ugushikama kw’ivy’ubutunzi mw’isi idatomoye.


#### Ugukoreshwa neza


Hakurikijwe ivyo twakoze vyose gushika ubu, mfise inyiyumvo y’uko utanguye gutahura ingene stablecoins itanga uburyo bwo gukoreshwa kurushiriza ku mafaranga ya kera. Ariko kugira ngo tuvyizereko, reka dukubite ingoma gatoyi.

Ivyo Tether itanga vyahinduye isi y’ivy’ubutunzi mu gutanga urugero rw’ugukoreshwa amafaranga y’agaciro adashobora guhura.


None mvuze ko umuntu ashobora gukoreshwa cane, ndashaka kuvuga iki? Reka twinjire muri zimwe mu nyungu z’intango maze turabe igituma stablecoins zabo ziriko zirakura cane.


Ica mbere, **ukwizigama** bituma dushobora gufata Ownership y’amahera yacu tutari twizigiye ibikorwa vya banki zihurikiye hamwe. Ivyo bisigura ko dufise ububasha bwose ku mahera yacu kandi ko dushobora kuyaronka igihe cose dukeneye, ata muntu wo hagati dukeneye. Ntituzosubira kurindira ko banki yacu ikuraho amahera canke ngo twiganyire ko konti yacu ishobora guhagarara ata mvo— n’amahera adahinduka, ni twebwe tubishinzwe. Ivyo bivuzwe, ntitwakuyeho burundu ubugenzuzi bushingiye hagati mu gufata uburenganzira bwo kwibungabunga. Ivyinshi mu bice vy’amahera, harimwo n’ivya Tether, bitangwa n’amashirahamwe yubatswe ku bice vy’amahera nka Ethereum na Tron. Ni co gituma dushira urugero rw’ukwizigira rwo mu mashirahamwe n’izo nzira.


Ica kabiri, kubera ko amafaranga adahinduka, nka USDt na XAUt, ari **ivy'ubuhinga bwa none**, turashobora gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none, 24/7. Ntituzosubira kwiganyira ku masaha y’ugufungura amabanki canke ugucererwa bitewe n’amasaha atandukanye— n’amahera adahinduka, turashobora gukoresha amahera igihe cose bidubereye, turi aho turi hose kw’isi.


Amafaranga agabanutse, nk’uko twabibonye haruguru, ni ikindi ciza gikomeye c’amahera ya Tether. Udakunze amafaranga y’agaciro, USDt, hamwe n’ibindi vyose batanga, birafise abahuza bakeyi bagira uruhara mu bikorwa vyose, ivyo bisigura ko tuguma dufise ubushobozi bwo kugura bwinshi cane— n’ama stablecoins, turonka aho tuguma dufise vyinshi mu vyo turonka.


Ubwa nyuma, stablecoins zitanga **ubugenzuzi bugabanutse**, bisobanura ko dufise umwidegemvyo mwinshi wo kuyobora amahera yacu aho tubona ko bikwiye. Udakunze amafaranga y’agaciro, afise ubwoko bwose bw’amategeko n’imipaka, amafaranga y’agaciro ameze nk’amahera, bisobanura ko abahuza bake cane ari bo bagira uruhara mu gucuruza. Ivyo bituma turonka umwidegemvyo mwinshi wo gutwara amahera yacu mu buryo bworoshe ataco twiganyira ku bijanye n’ukugenzura kwa Leta canke ubuhinga bwo gukoresha amahera.


Muri rusangi, amafaranga atandukanye ya Tether atanga urugero rwo guhindura n’umwidegemvyo amafaranga y’agaciro adashobora guhura. Kubera ko umuntu yizigamira, akoresha ubuhinga bwa none, amafaranga agabanuka, n’ukugenzura agabanuka, ntibitangaje ko abantu benshi bariko barahindukira bakaja ku mahera yabo y’ubutunzi nk’uburyo bwizewe kandi bwizewe bwo gukoresha no kubika ubutunzi.


#### Ukwongerekana kwa Bitcoin


Ivya nyuma ariko bitari ivya nyuma, Tether iriko iragira uruhara runini mu kwongerera ukwemerwa kwa Bitcoin mu gukora nk'ikiraro hagati y'amabanki ya kera n'amabanki yegerejwe, Trustless n'amabarabara atagira uruhusha ya Bitcoin.


Imbere y’uko haza stablecoins, nka USDt, gukoresha no gusohoka muri Bitcoin vyari igikorwa kigoye kandi giteye akaga. Twabwirizwa kurondera umuntu yipfuza guhindura Bitcoin yiwe n’amahera yacu canke tukarondera banki ishobora gukoresha Bitcoin canke Exchange. Ivyo vyatuma bigorana kugura no kugurisha Bitcoin, cane cane iyo tuba mu gihugu cari gifise urwanko kuri ayo mahera y’amageza ya internet. Kandi naho tworonka uburyo bwo gukoresha no gusohoka, twabwirizwa kwizigira cane urwego rwa kera rw’amabanki no kwizigira ko batazohagarika konti yacu canke ngo bagahungabanye ubushobozi bwacu bwo kugura canke kugurisha Bitcoin.


Kubera ko amafaranga atandukanye ya Tether yariko araduga, ibintu vyarahindutse. USDt na XAUt ubu zitanga uburyo bwo kwizigirwa bwa Exchange buhuza amabarabara ya kera y'amabanki n'amabarabara yegerejwe n'amabarabara ya Trustless ya Bitcoin. Mu gukoresha izo stablecoins, abantu ubu barashobora gukoresha no gusohoka muri Bitcoin bitagoranye kandi ataco basubira ku nzira za kera z’amabanki. Ivyo vyatumye abantu barushiriza kwemera Bitcoin, kuko ubu abantu bashobora gukorana n’abandi ataco bitwararika ku bijanye n’intambamyi ziterwa n’uburyo bwa kera bwo gutanga amafaranga.


Nk’akarorero, dufate ko uwukoresha ashaka kugura Bitcoin. Muri ivyo, barashobora gusa kugura USDt kuri Exchange hanyuma bagakoresha iyo stablecoin kugira bagure Bitcoin ataco baciyeko, bikaba bituma badakeneye gutanga amahera biciye muri banki. Canke iyo bakeneye kugurisha Bitcoin, barashobora kuyigurisha Exchange ku USDt batabwirizwa kuyihindura bagasubira mu mafaranga yabo yo mu gihugu.


Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, stablecoins ziriko zirahindura ingene dukorana n’itunga ry’igihugu, nka Bitcoin, mu gutanga ikiraro kitagira umurongo kandi coroshe gukoresha hagati y’amabanki ya kera n’isi y’ubuhinga bwa none yegerejwe. Uko kwemera amafaranga y’amabanki bikomeza gukura, turashobora kwitega kubona mbere n’ukwemera gukomeye kwa Bitcoin uko abantu benshi bamenya ko ata nkenerwa yo gusubira kwinjira mw’isi ya kera y’amabanki, bitewe n’uko amafaranga y’amabanki akoreshwa n’ubuhinga bwa none.


Mu gusozera, amashikanwa ya Tether’s stablecoin afasha umwidegemvyo w’amahera n’umutekano ku bantu ba misi yose gusa ariko no ku baba mu bice vya kure canke bidatekanye badashobora kuronka ibikorwa vy’amabanki vyizewe.


Fata nk’akarorero inkuru ya Adanna, yerekana ingene USDt ishobora gufasha abantu nka we guhunga amafaranga yabo yo mu gihugu ariko arasenyuka ningoga, maze bakagira ububasha bwinshi ku mafaranga yabo ata kwigera bahagarika umutima ku bijanye n’ukudashikama kw’amafaranga canke ukuntu USDt itanga umuti uhambaye ku bantu batagira amabanki, bituma umuntu ashobora kuronka amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none. utugyo.


Kandi nimba ivyo bidahagije, izo stablecoins ntizituma amafaranga y’agaciro akoreshwa gusa, zifasha kugabanya amahera ajanye no kohereza amahera, bikaba bituma abantu bashobora gusubiza amahera abo bakunda ataco baciye.


Muri rusangi, amafaranga adahinduka, nka USDt na XAUt, arafise ubushobozi bwo guhindura ubuzima bw’amamiliyaridi mu kubaha uburenganzira bwo kuronka ibikorwa vy’ivy’ubutunzi bihuye n’abantu bose kandi bikenewe cane.


## Ivyigwa


<chapterId>1294d874-6edb-5feb-b070-0ead1836bd0b</chapterId>


None ko mwaciye mu Module "Stability Amidst Chaos" muzobwirizwa kugerageza ubumenyi bushasha mwaronse kugira ngo mumenye neza ko mwatahuye ibice vya nyuma. Tuzotangura n’Ibibazo vyinshi vyuguruye hanyuma dukore ikibazo gitoyi.


1. Ni ivyiza ibihe n’ibibi ibihe vyo gukoresha amafaranga y’amafranga ashigikiwe na fiat ugereranyije n’amafaranga y’amafaranga y’amafranga nk’idolari ry’Amerika?

2. Mu vyiyumviro vyawe, ni inyungu izihe zishobora guterwa n’amadolari y’Amerika (USDt) ku bantu ku giti cabo badashobora kuronka ubufasha bwa banki?

3. Mu vyiyumviro vyawe, uruhara rw’ama stablecoins ruhambaye gute mu kurinda abantu ingaruka mbi z’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro? Mbega vy’ukuri ama stablecoins yoshobora gutuma amahera aguma ahagaze mw’isi idatomoye?

4. Ni gute wibaza ko stablecoins zishobora gufasha mu gushiramwo amafaranga no guteza imbere ubutunzi mu bihugu biri mu nzira y’amajambere?

5. Mu vyiyumviro vyawe, ni ingingo izihe abatanga amafaranga y’ama stablecoin bakwiye gufata kugira ngo amafaranga yabo y’ama stablecoin aguma ahagaze kandi yizewe? Ni ngombwa gute ko abatanga amafaranga y’amafaranga (stablecoin) bagaragaza neza ingene bakora mu bijanye n’ububiko bwabo kandi bagatanga raporo zidasanzwe?


# Gutsinda Amakenga - Gukuraho Ivyiyumviro Bitari vyo n'Ibikoresho vy'Isi Nyakuri


<partId>246a7dc0-a203-5b2e-ae13-9c8f08e6bfad</partId>


## Ivyiyumviro bitari vyo


<chapterId>4da9319d-6306-500f-adbb-5fa31c673cd2</chapterId>


Bitcoin yarakikujwe n’ugusubira inyuma, ugunegura n’ivyiyumviro bitari vyo kuva yavuka mu 2009. Naho yariko irakura mu gukundwa no mu kwemerwa, benshi baracaribona ko ari igihu kirindiriye guturika. Muri iyo mirongo nyene, amafaranga y’amahera agumaho yarakwegereye abantu nk’ako nyene be n’ugukekeranya. Iciyumviro c’uko amafaranga ashigikiwe n’umutungo udahinduka kirumvikana ko ari ikintu gitanga umuhango, ariko abantu benshi ntibatahura neza ingene amafaranga adahinduka akora be n’ingaruka yoshobora kugira ku bijanye n’ivy’ubutunzi.


Muri iki gice, tuzoca irya n’ino bimwe mu vyiyumviro bitari vyo bikunze kuvugwa ku bijanye na Bitcoin n’amahera y’amahera. Tuzokwihweza ukuri kuri inyuma y’ivyo vyiyumviro bitari vyo maze dushire ahabona ivyo vyatumye abantu bavyura urujijo n’ugukekeranya cane. Kuva ku ciyumviro c’uko Bitcoin ihinduka cane ku buryo idashobora kuba ifaranga rishobora gukoreshwa gushika ku bijanye n’ikoreshwa ry’inguvu zayo, tuzosuzuma ikibazo cose kugira ngo ushobore kwishingira iciyumviro cawe. Mu mpera z’iki gice, uzoba ufise ugutahura gukomeye cane ku bijanye n’izo tekinoloji be n’uko hariho ivy’ukuri biri inyuma y’ivyo bisubizo.

Bitcoin Ivyiyumviro bitari vyo

Naho hariho ivyiyumviro vyinshi bitari vyo bikikuje Bitcoin, reka dukore ku bintu icenda bihambaye kuruta ibindi vyose:


1. Bitcoin ni igihu kirindiriye guturika

2. Bitcoin irahinduka cane ku buryo idashobora kugira agaciro

3. Bitcoin ntaco imaze kuko ntaco ishigikiye

4. Ubuhinga bwa Bitcoin buramaze guhera

5. Bitcoin irateba cane kandi irazimvye cane ku buryo idashobora kuba uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha Exchange .

6. Bitcoin ikoreshwa cane cane mu bikorwa bitemewe n’amategeko .

7. Umuntu wese arashobora kwisubiriza kode ya Bitcoin, akayigira ubusa .

8. Bitcoin ikoresha inguvu nyinshi cane


Reka twibike muri...


Iciyumviro kitari co ca mbere: Bitcoin ni igihu kirindiriye guturika

Kuva yatanguye, Bitcoin yaravuzwe ko yapfuye mu binyamakuru vyinshi (Kuva muri Ntwarante 2023), yamara irabandanya gukora ata neza ata gasembwa.


Ivyo bituma umuntu yibaza ati: None Bitcoin ituma abantu biyumvira ko ari igihu kirindiriye guturika?

Mu mateka yose, iyo ikintu cadutse cane mu giciro, na co nyene gikunda kubona igiciro giteye akaga, kuko ico gici- ro kidashobora kuramba kandi akenshi kivyurwa n’ugutekereza ku bintu n’ukunzi w’inda. None, ni igiki gituma Bitcoin itandukanye?


Ica mbere, Bitcoin ifise Supply y’ibiceri vy’imiliyoni 21, ivyo bisigura ko, bitandukanye n’amahera ya fiat ya kera, idashobora gukurwako agaciro n’ukwaguka kw’amahera. Ukwo kubura, hamwe n’ukwiyongera kw’ukwemera kwa Bitcoin kw’isi yose, vyatumye agaciro kayo kagenda karaduga ariko gahinduka uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Ivyo bitandukanye n’ibindi bintu vyose, aho uko ibiciro biduga, ni ko na Supply iduga. Ivyo bisigura ko Supply izorengera ivyifuzo mu gihe kanaka, kandi ibiciro bizobwirizwa gusenyuka.


Ubwa kabiri, yubatswe muri kode ya Bitcoin ni ikintu citwa Halving. Nk’inyuma y’imyaka ine yose, ico kintu kiragabanya impembo ya Mining n’igice, bikagira ico bikoze ku mahera abacukuzi bashobora kuronka. Keretse igiciro ca Bitcoin kigabanutse kabiri, abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro baragabanuka cane mu vyo baronka. Ivyo vyatumye Bitcoin igaragazwa nk'ubuhinga bwa "umubare uzamuka", kuko iyo nzira itera umukazo wo kuduga ku giciro inyuma y'imyaka ine kugira ngo abacukuzi bashobore kuronka indishi ihagije kubera gukingira Blockchain. Ku bw’ivyo, turabona ivyo bihinduka vy’ibiciro bihinduka hafi inyuma y’imyaka ine.


_**Iciyumviro co ku ruhande:** Niba wararize ivy'amahera, ushobora kuba wararumvise ivy'"theorem y'isoko ryiza," yubatswe ku ciyumviro c'uko amasoko akora neza ata gatotsi kubera inyifato ibereye. Ivuga rero ko ibiciro vy'itunga mu masoko y'ivy'ubutunzi vyerekana amakuru yose ariho, bikaba bidashoboka gushika ku nyungu zirengeye izo mu gusuzuma amakuru y'akahise canke ayandi makuru y'isoko._


_Ariko rero, iyo nyigisho iribagira ko amasoko agizwe n’abantu ku giti cabo, kandi kamere y’umuntu ikaba ari iyo mu kameremere katagira ishingiro kandi ikaba ikozweko n’inyiyumvo. Ukwo kutagira ishingiro bituma umuntu agira ivyiyumviro bitari vyo, inyifato y’umukumbi, n’amakosa yo mu bwenge, bigatuma ibiciro biva ku gaciro kavyo nyakuri. Nk’akarorero, mu bijanye n’ibintu vya Bitcoin vya Halving, amasoko afise ivyiyumviro akwiye kwitega no kwerekana Supply izogabanywa muri kazoza mu giciro ca Bitcoin c’ubu. Ariko rero, ukuntu ibiciro vyiyongera mu bihe bitandukanye birerekana ko abaje muri iyo nama batagira ico bavuze kuri ayo makuru. Ukwo kutagira ishingiro kwagaragaje ko gutanga ingororano nyinshi z’amahera ku barwayi bafise igihe kirekire._


Ica gatatu, Bitcoin irafise ubushobozi bwo guhindura cane Exchange kw’isi yose. Ku ncuro ya mbere muri kahise, turafise uburyo bwo gukorana mu buryo bwa Trustless, ata ruhusha kandi bushingiye ku rwego rwo hejuru. Nk’uko twabibonye mu ntango z’iki cigwa, ivyo nta co bigereranywa kandi biratuma ibihugu vyateye imbere n’ibiri mu nzira y’amajambere bironka inyungu nyinshi cane.


Ubwa nyuma, agaciro k’isoko kose ka Bitcoin kari ku rugero rw’amadolari 550 miliyaridi y’amadolari y’Amerika. Ivyo bishobora gusa n’amahera menshi cane gushika ubonye ko inzahabu, bivanye n’ingene umuntu ayiharura, iri ahantu hose kuva ku madolari \10 trillion gushika ku madolari 20 trillion. Ivyo bisigura ko naho Bitcoin itanga ivyiza vyinshi nk’ivy’inzahabu, icuruzwa ku gice ca 1/40 c’agaciro. Kandi iyo turavye ibindi bintu, iyo ntandukaniro irarushiriza kuba nini.



- Isoko ry'ivy'ubutunzi kw'isi yose: [\$124.4 trillions](www.sifma.org/ibikoresho/ubushakashatsi/igitabu-cy'amakuru/)
- Isoko ry'inyungu zidahinduka/impapuro z'ideni kw'isi yose: \$126.9 trillions
- Isoko ry’amazu n’ibindi bibanza kw’isi yose: [\$326.5 trillions](https://www.savills.com/ingaruka/imigenderanire-y’isoko/agaciro-kose-k’amazu-y’isi yose.html)
- Isoko ry’isi yose ry’ibikomoka ku bindi: Rigereranywa ko rirenga [\$1 quadrillion]


Muri vyose, iyo abantu bita Bitcoin igihu, canke:


1. Ntibakoze ubushakashatsi kugira ngo batahure inyungu zayo nyinshi n’ingene zikoreshwa.

2. Canke ntibatahura neza ingene Bitcoin ikora be n’agaciro kose kabitswe mu bintu biri hejuru aho Bitcoin ishobora gufata umugabane w’amasaha y’inyongera.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca kabiri: Bitcoin irahinduka cane ku buryo idashobora kugira agaciro


Abanegura kenshi bavuga ko uguhinduka kwa Bitcoin bituma iba uburyo bubi bwo gushiramwo amahera, ariko iyo mpamvu irirengagiza ibintu bikeyi bihambaye ku bijanye n’igituma Bitcoin iriko irashikirwa n’uguhinduka nk’ukwo.


Ica mbere, uguhinduka kwa Bitcoin ni ikiganiro ca Hot kandi vyatumye bamwe banegura uwo mutungo kubera uguhinduka kw’igiciro kwawo gukomeye. Twemera ko ivyo ari ukubona ibintu mu buryo bukeyi ku bijanye n’uguhinduka nk’uko uguhinduka gupima ingene igiciro c’umutungo gihinduka, atari ukugabanuka kwaco gusa. Abafise ubukomezi bwo gufata neza Bitcoin biciye mu guhinduka kwayo barahezagiwe cane. Fata nk’akarorero ivy’ubutunzi A na B. Itunga A ryiyongera ku rugero rwa mwayeni n’ibice 10% ku mwaka n’ugukevya kw’ibice 15%, mu gihe umutungo B wiyongera n’ibice 5% ku mwaka n’ugukevya kw’ibice 10%. Naho umutungo B ufise ubushobozi bwo guhinduka buke kuruta umutungo A, umutungo A urarusha umutungo B mu gihe kirekire. Utegerezwa kuba witeguye guhangana n’uguhinduka kugira ngo wimbure ivyiza vy’uguhinduka kw’ibiciro vya Bitcoin. Ikindi kandi, USD ishobora kuba idahinduka cane ku musi ku musi. Ariko rero, nimba warafise ayo mafaranga mu myaka 100 iheze, uba waratakaje [96%](https://www.visualcapitalist.com/ubushobozi-bw’ugugura-bw’idolari-ry’Umurundi-mu-gihe/) bw’ubushobozi bwo kugura.


Ubwa kabiri, uguhinduka ni ikintu gisanzwe iyo bije ku bijanye no gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none. Iyo ubuhinga bushasha buje, nta gukeka ko haba ukudakeka n’ugutekereza ku bijanye n’ubushobozi bwabwo, ivyo bikaba bituma ibiciro bihinduka. Ubwenge bukorano (AI) ni akarorero nyamukuru k’urwego ruhinduka cane. Kuva mu [2021 gushika mu 2022](https://www.ubushakashatsi bw'imbere \$119 billion. Ariko naho AI ishobora guhinduka, inyungu zo gushiramwo amahera muri AI ntizishobora kwirengagizwa Kuva ku modoka zitwara umuntu ku giti ciwe gushika ku buvuzi bugenewe umuntu ku giti ciwe, ubushobozi bwo gukoresha AI ni bwinshi cane Rero, nimba ukunda AI, ntushobora gutakaza amahirwe yo guhinduka.


Ikindi kandi, ukuntu Bitcoin ihinduka si ikintu kimwe gusa. Amasoko y’ivy’ubutunzi asanzwe na yo nyene arashikirwa n’uguhinduka kw’ibiciro vy’itunga, nk’isoko ry’ivy’ubutunzi, isoko ry’ibicuruzwa, eka mbere n’amahera. Nkako, uguhinduka kwa Bitcoin birashoboka ko ataco bimaze kuruta ibindi bintu vyinshi.


Ubwa nyuma, imvo y’uko Bitcoin ihinduka cane irananirwa kwihweza umuce uhambaye: agaciro kayo ubu kaboshe n’amahera y’amahera. Ivyo bihinduka bigaragara mu gaciro ka Bitcoin biterwa ahanini n’ukudashikama kw’ingero y’ishimikiro, nk’idolari canke ayandi mafaranga. Nk’uko Lawrence White abivuga neza mu gitabu ciwe [Amahera meza](https://amzn.to/3NZnCTm), ivyo bihinduka vy’ibiciro ahanini biva ku bantu barondera uburyo bwo kwikingira ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro. Mu buryo butandukanye, muri systeme yacu y’ububiko bw’amahera bugenzurwa n’amabanki akomeye, abari mu bibanza vy’ubutegetsi barafise ubushobozi bwo guhindura Supply y’amahera ariko aragendagenda. Ivyo bituma iyo bakoze politike y’amahera, nk’ugutuma amahera agenda neza, ibiciro vy’itunga biduga, iyo bakomeje, ibiciro bikagabanuka. Ivyo bishobora gutuma habaho ukudakeka n’ukudatekana kw’amasoko y’ivy’ubutunzi. Ku bw’ivyo, gusuzuma ukuntu Bitcoin ihinduka bishingiye ku nyifato yayo hakurikijwe urugero rwa fiat birazimiza. Mu vy’ukuri, birerekana gusa ukuntu amafaranga y’amahera ahinduka.


Mu buryo butandukanye n’ubwo, Bitcoin ikorera ku rubuga rwegerejwe, aho Supply igumye kandi idashobora gukoreshwa n’ubutegetsi bukuru. Naho ivyo bisigura ko hoshobora kubaho uguhinduka kw’igihe gito, ukubura n’ugushobora kumenya imbere y’igihe Supply ya Supply bizogabanya cane uguhinduka no kwongera ugushikama mu gihe kirekire.


Kugira ngo ivyo tubigereranye:


1. Mu mwaka w’2018, inyigisho zibiri zigenga zakozwe na Charles Schwab na Grayscale Investments zagaragaje ko uguhinduka kwa Bitcoin kwagabanutse cane hagati ya 2011 na 2013.

2. Raporo ya Bitwise Asset Management mu mwaka w’2019 yerekanye ko uguhinduka kwa Bitcoin kwagabanutse cane kuva mu mwaka w’2014, ubu bikaba bigereranywa n’ibindi bikoresho vya kera nk’amafaranga y’ubutunzi.

3. Icigwa casohowe na Coin Metrics mu mwaka w’2020, cerekanye ko uguhinduka kwa Bitcoin kwagabanutse cane mu myaka ibiri iheze.


Dufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, birahambaye ko tubona ukuntu Bitcoin ihinduka mu buryo bw’ubutunzi bwagutse, ntituvyirengagize gusa nk’akaga. Ubushobozi bwa Bitcoin nk’ububiko bw’agaciro n’uburyo bwa Exchange ntibukwiye gugabanywa bishingiye ku guhinduka kw’ibiciro mu gihe gito.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca gatatu: Bitcoin ntaco imaze kuko ataco ishigikiye


Bitcoin akenshi irakurwaho kubera ko idashigikiwe n’ikintu na kimwe c’agaciro, nk’inzahabu canke amahera ya leta. Iciyumviro c’uko, kubera ko Bitcoin idashigikiwe n’ikintu na kimwe gifatika, itegerezwa kuba ata co imaze, ni ikinyoma.


Agaciro ni umuntu yiyumvira kandi kari mu jisho ry’uwuriko arabona. Ikintu gifise agaciro kubera ko abantu bemera ko ari co.

Fata akarorero k’ubuhinga. Igishushanyo ni igitambaro gusa n’irangi, yamara hari ibice bimwebimwe bifise agaciro k’amamiliyoni y’amadolari. Kubera iki? Kuko abantu bahagije barabaha agaciro cane gutyo. Utitaye ku vyo abandi biyumvira, ibishushanyo biratanga agaciro kuri nyen’ivyo bishushanyo, ni co gituma babiguze.


Ivyo ni ko biri no kuri Bitcoin. Abantu barayiha agaciro kuko ari amafaranga yegerejwe abantu bose ata leta canke banki iyo ari yo yose igenzura. Ni gake, ifise Supply nke, kandi iratekanye kubera ubuhinga buri inyuma yayo. Abantu bamwe bamwe boshobora kutabona ko ivyo biranga ari ugutanga agaciro, kandi ivyo ni vyiza. Ariko ivyo ntibisigura ko ata co bimaze.


Igiciro ni ikimenyetso c’ico abantu biteguriye kwishura ku kintu. Iyo Bitcoin iba ataco imaze vy’ukuri, kuko ataco ishigikiye, rero yoba iriko iragurishwa ku \$0, kuko ata n’umwe yoba yiteguriye Exchange amahera yabo yaronse Hard kubera yo.


Vyongeye, iciyumviro c’uko amahera ategerezwa gushigikirwa n’ikintu c’agaciro n’ikinyoma. Amafaranga ya Fiat, nk’idolari ry’Amerika, ntashigikiwe n’inzahabu canke ikintu cose gifatika. Ahubwo agaciro kavyo gashingiye ku kwizigira Leta ibitanga no ku kwizera ko bishobora guhindurwa n’ibintu n’ibikorwa. Ku bijanye na Bitcoin, agaciro kayo gashingiye ku kwizigira ubuhinga buyishigikiye no kwizera ko bushobora gukoreshwa mu kubika agaciro canke ibintu n’ibikorwa vya Exchange.


Amaherezo, iciyumviro c’uko ikintu kigomba gushigikirwa n’ikindi kintu c’agaciro kugira ngo kibe c’agaciro ni izina ribi. Agaciro ni ikintu umuntu yiyumvira kandi gishingiye ku vyo abantu baciyemwo n’ivyo bemera. Kubera ko umuntu umwe abona ikintu ata co kimaze ntibisigura ko bose babibona, n’ibihushanye n’ivyo.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca kane: Ubuhinga bwa Bitcoin buramaze guhera


Reka noneho twinjire mu mpamvu zisubirwamwo zivuga ko Bitcoin itagikoreshwa, dusenyure igituma ivyo bidashobora kuba kure y’ukuri.


Ica mbere, mw’isi y’amahera y’amahera, hariho iki ciyumviro citwa Blockchain trilemma. Mu vy’ukuri, hariho ibiranga bitatu vy’intango amafaranga y’ibanga akunda kwibandako:


1. Ugushobora gukwiragizwa

2. Umutekano

3. Kwegera ubutegetsi


Ata kwisuka mu catsi kibi, mu karere k’amahera y’ibanga, ingorane zitatu ziza igihe amafaranga y’ibanga ategerezwa kumenya inzira yayo n’agaciro kayo. Iryo faranga ry’amahera rishobora gusa gushiramwo imbere ibintu bibiri muri bitatu twavuze haruguru, bikaba bigomba gufata ingingo zigoye be n’uguhinduranya.


Bitcoin ihitamwo gushira imbere kwegereza ubutegetsi abaturage n’umutekano kuruta gutera imbere. Naho ari ukwo, iyo nzira yo gutera imbere iracariho. Ivyo ibigira gusa biciye mu buryo bundi (Biravugwa mu ciyumviro kitari co gikurikira). Ariko rero, ayandi mafaranga y’ibanga akenshi ashira imbere ubushobozi bwo gutera imbere, ariko mu kubigira, aratanga ugusenyura ubutegetsi, bikaba bituma ashobora guterwa canke ntaco atandukaniyeko n’amafaranga y’ibanga canke umutekano.


Ica kabiri, Bitcoin yubatswe ku kwumvikana, bisobanura ko naho woba uri nde canke aho uba kw’isi, mu gukoresha igice ca porogarama, urashobora kugira ijambo mu bijanye na Bitcoin. Ivyo bisigura ko uko isi itera imbere, Bitcoin ishobora kumenyera ibidukikije vyayo bihinduka. Ivyo bigaragazwa n’ibintu vyinshi vyahinduwe kuri Bitcoin mu myaka iheze, nka SegWit, vyatumye ishobora gukoreshwa neza, na Lightning Network, ituma umuntu ashobora gukoresha amafaranga yihuta kandi ataco amaze.


Ubwa nyuma, naho hariho ibihumbi vy’ibindi bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none bitanga inyungu zitandukanye, Bitcoin ntiriko iragerageza kuba ibintu vyose ku bantu bose. Ahubwo, iriko iragerageza gukora ikintu kimwe neza cane: kuba amafaranga yegerejwe, Trustless, kandi ata ruhusha afise. Kandi... ivyo ibikora neza kurusha uwundi wese, nk’uko bigaragazwa n’isoko ryayo, ari ryo ry’incuro nyinshi z’iyindi cryptocurrency yose.


Ariko rero, birakenewe kumenya ko ikibanza c'"cryptocurrency" gikunda kuba cuzuye amajambo y'uruyeri, menshi muri yo ashingiye ku vyiyumviro vyashikirijwe, bigeragezwa, hanyuma bigaheba n'abahinga mu vy'amafaranga y'ibanga ba OG n'abahinguzi ba Bitcoin. Ingero nyinshi zirerekana iyo ngendo: Ubuhinga bwa none buzwi cane (ZK) bwasanze Genesis yayo mu biganiro vyakozwe na Satoshi ubwiwe mu 2010 na Gregory Maxwell mu 2013. Bitcoin, Elements na Liquid. Iciyumviro co "gufatanya"—gufatanya canke gufatanya iminyororo myinshi ya Blockchain kugira ngo umuntu ashike ku nyungu canke ibikorwa bimwebimwe—cari carashikirijwe mu ntango n'abahinguzi ba Bitcoin nk'umuti ushobora gutorera umuti ingorane zimwe zimwe zo gutera imbere no gukorana neza kandi ubu gikoreshwa na Kaspa, Hederano, Byte na Kaspa, Byte. Inkomoko y'ubuhinga bushasha bwinshi bwa "NFT" isubira inyuma mu bikorwa vy'ubutsimvyi vya Bitcoin mu 2013/14/15. Mbere n'"Ikimenyamenya c'Igice," camenyekanye cane biciye ku Peercoin, Bitshares, NXT, na Ethereum, ni iciyumviro cazutse kivuye mu nzira ya kabiri ya Wei Dai y'amahera b, yatanguye gutegurwa mu 1998-naho Satoshi amaherezo fa-W G40 yavyirukanye. Naho kwinjira mu bintu vyose bitari ngombwa, biragaragara ko "ubuhinga bushasha" bushingiye ku biceri vyinshi vy'ubundi buryo bushingiye ku guhinduka kwa Bitcoin ubwayo.


Rero, na none, imvo y’uko Bitcoin itagikoreshwa nta shingiro ifise. Bishobora kuba bitatunganye kuri bose, ariko birabandanya gutera imbere no gutera imbere.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca gatanu: Bitcoin irateba cane kandi irazimvye ku buryo idashobora kuba uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha Exchange


Niwibuka mu Gice ca Kabiri Igice ca Kane, Blockchain ya Blockchain igizwe n’amabuye, imwe yose ikaba ifise ubunini burenze nk’ubw’1mb. Kubera ubunini buke bw’ibarabara, Bitcoin’s base Layer ifise urugero rwo hejuru rwo gukora amafaranga agera ku ndwi ku segonda (tps), ruri hasi cane y’imihora nka Visa canke Mastercard, ikora amafaranga 1.700 tps. Gutyo Bitcoin akenshi ivugwa ko iteba cane ku buryo idashobora gukora nk'uburyo bushoboka bwo gukoresha Exchange.


Ariko rero, birahambaye cane kuvuga ko Bitcoin itariko iragerageza guhangana na Visa canke Mastercard. Ahubwo, isa cane na Layer imwe, ishobora gukora ibikorwa vy’agaciro kanini ariko ni agace k’umuvuduko n’igiciro c’uburyo bwa kera bwa Layer imwe mu gihe kandi ari Trustless, idafise uruhusha kandi itanga ibikorwa vy’agaciro kanini.


Ariko Bitcoin nayo irahiganwa na Layer uburyo bubiri bwo gukorana, n’ubuhinga nka Lightning bubatswe hejuru ya Layer imwe. Umuravyo utuma umuntu ashobora gukora amafaranga hafi y’aho nyene ataco atanga, ivyo bikaba bituma amafaranga makeyi n’ugugura ibintu bitobito bishoboka. Kuva El Salvador yemeye Bitcoin nk’ifaranga ryemewe, abantu muri rusangi barakoresha Lightning mu gucuruza na Bitcoin kubera inyungu zitagira uko zingana, nk’ibihe vyo gucuruza hafi mu kanya nk’ako gukubita n’amahera y’agace k’isenti. Ivyo bituma iba nziza cane ku bacuruzi batobato no ku bantu ku giti cabo.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca gatandatu: Bitcoin ikoreshwa canecane mu bikorwa bitemewe n’amategeko


Naho inyigisho nyinshi zigaragaza ko ivyo bivugwa ko ari ibinyoma, Bitcoin iracariko iranegurwa kenshi ko ikoreshwa canecane mu bikorwa bitemewe n’amategeko. Na none, ivyo ntivyari gushobora kuba kure y’ukuri.


Icigwa kimwe (https://cryptoforinnovation.org/resources/Analysis_of_Bitcoin_mu_vy'amahera_atemewe) cakozwe n'uwahoze ari umuyobozi wungirije wa CIA casanze "ivy'ugukoresha Bitcoin mu vy'amahera atemewe birenze cane." Nkako, kuva mu 2016, ibice bitari munsi ya 1% vy’amahera yose Bitcoin yagurishije vyakoreshejwe mu bikorwa bitemewe n’amategeko. Mu kugereranya, "bamwe bashira ubutunzi bwo mu mpisho ku bice 11% gushika kuri 12% vy'umusaruro wose wo mu gihugu ca Amerika," ivyo bikaba ari vyo vyinshi bifasha idolari ry'Amerika.


Kandi nk’uko bigaragara muri raporo ya Chainalysis mu mwaka w’2020, ibikorwa bitemewe n’amategeko bifise gusa nk’ibice nka [0,34%](https://www.


Ariko rero, naho nyene ivyo bimenyamenya biriho, amajambo azimiza arabandanya guvugwa n’abafise ububasha, nk’uko umunyamabanga mukuru w’itunga rya Amerika Janet Yellen [avuga](https://home.treasury.gov/news/press-releases/jy0023), “Amafaranga y’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none yarakoreshejwe mu gucuruza ibiyayuramutwe ku rubuga rwa interineti; iterabwoba."


Naho inyigisho zitari nke zihakana ivyo vyiyumviro vy’ikinyoma, biragaragara ko abantu bamwebamwe bafise umugambi kandi biyemeje kwubaka inkuru mbi kandi zitari zo zikikuje Bitcoin. Ukuri ni uko Bitcoin ifise ubushobozi bwo kuzana ihinduka ryiza rikomeye kw’isi, kuva ku gutanga uburyo bwo kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’ubutunzi ku bantu batagira amabanki gushika ku kugabanya amafaranga y’ugucuruza no kwongerera umwidegemvyo w’ivy’ubutunzi.


Mu bijanye n’ivyo, naho ata n’umwe ahakana ko ibikorwa bitemewe bibaho mw’isi ya Bitcoin, ibimenyamenya vyerekana ko ari ukwihenda kwizera ko ari co gikoreshwa ca mbere. Nkako, ijana kw’ijana ry’amahera ya Bitcoin akoreshwa mu bikorwa bitemewe n’amategeko ni rito cane ugereranije n’ivy’amahera ya kera.


Ariko rero, birahambaye ko udasigira inyifato zose zitemewe n’amategeko n’ibara rimwe. Ibikorwa bimwe bimwe bibonwa ko "bitemewe" mu ntara imwe bishobora kubonwa nk'uburenganzira bw'ishimikiro mu bundi. Nk'akarorero:



- Ivyo amadini atari ay’ubuyisilamu akora muri Arabiya Saudite,
- Ubukwe bw’abasangiye igitsina mu bihugu nk’Uburusiya na Irani,
- Canke kuronka uburezi ku bakobwa bo muri Pakistani .


...bifatwa nk’ibitemewe n’amategeko mu bihugu vyavyo. Ivyo bishimika ku vy’uko ivyo bibonwa ko bitemewe n’amategeko atari ivy’umwirabura canke ivy’umweru. Hariho isano rikomeye hagati y'insobanuro z'amategeko n'agaciro gatandukanye gashigikirwa mu turere dutandukanye.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co c’indwi: Umuntu wese arashobora kwisubiriza kode ya Bitcoin, akayigira ata co imaze .


Iciyumviro c’uko kode ya Bitcoin ishobora gukoporwa bitagoranye, rero ko ata co kimaze, kirabura umuce uhambaye w’igituma Bitcoin igira agaciro. Naho ari ukuri ko kode ya Bitcoin ari inkomoko yuguruye kandi ishobora gukoporwa, agaciro ka Bitcoin ntikava gusa ku ntumbero itanga.


Kimwe mu bintu bihambaye cane vya Bitcoin ni uruja n’uruza rwayo. Bitcoin imaze kubaho kuva mu 2009 kandi yubatse urufatiro rw’abakoresha benshi mu gihe c’igihe. Iyi nzira y'abakoresha irimwo abantu ku giti cabo, ubucuruzi n'ibihugu vyashize amahera muri Bitcoin kandi bikayikoresha nk'ububiko bw'agaciro canke uburyo bwa Exchange.


Iyi nzira ituma abantu babandanya bakoresha Bitcoin. Naho token nshasha yoba yaremwe ifise ubushobozi nk’ubwa Bitcoin, ntiyogira urugero rumwe rwo kwizigirwa no kwemerwa. Ivyo ni kubera ko vyobura urubuga rwashinzwe rw’abakoresha n’amateka y’ibikorwa.


Mu mvugo yoroshe, nk’uko nyene udashobora guhindura Facebook nshasha ejo maze ukitega ko izogira agaciro nk’aka Facebook y’intango, token nshasha ntishobora gusa kwisubirako urubuga rwa Bitcoin mw’ijoro rimwe. Agaciro ka Bitcoin si mu mategeko yayo gusa ahubwo kari mu kwizigira no kwemerwa yubatse uko igihe kigenda kirarenga.


Mu ncamake, naho kode ya Bitcoin ishobora kuba ari inkomoko yuguruye kandi ishobora gukoporwa, agaciro kayo kava ku rubuga rwayo rw’abakoresha n’ukwizigira n’ukwemerwa yubatse uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. token nshasha ifise ubushobozi nk'ubwa Bitcoin ntiyogira urugero rumwe rw'ukwizigirwa n'ukwemerwa, rero ntiyoshobora gusubirira Bitcoin.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co Umunani: Bitcoin ikoresha inguvu nyinshi cane


Bitcoin kenshi iraba ikintu abantu bayivuga nabi, bavuga ko ikoresha inguvu nyinshi kuruta ibihugu bitobito canke ko izoteka inyanja. Ariko rero, abo banegura bararengagiza neza ingero zigereranywa zivuye mu bindi bikorwa bitwara inguvu kugira ngo batange ivyerekeye.


Birabereye kandi kumenya ko ivyo abantu banegura ku bijanye n’ikoreshwa ry’inguvu za Bitcoin akenshi biva ku bantu bo mu bihugu bifise agateka kandi biteye imbere. Abo bantu mu bisanzwe bararonka uburenganzira bwo gukoresha amabanki, barakoresha ibikoresho vy’ukwumisha impuzu, bizigira ibikoresho vy’ugushushanya canke gukonjesha, barashaza inzu zabo n’amatara ya Noweli, kandi barakunda kuja mu biruhuko vyo mu mahanga canke vyo kugenda kure. Ivyo vyose bifata inguvu.

Dufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, turashaka kuganira ku ngingo zitatu:


1. **Ubuhinga bw'agaciro:** Kubera iki ata kintu co gukoresha inguvu "vyinshi cane". Ingero y’inguvu zikoreshwa n’igikorwa canke inganda yinaka yerekana agaciro abantu bayiha. Iyo ikintu gisaba inguvu kugira ngo gikore, ni kubera ko hariho ugusaba n’inyungu umuntu abona ko gifitaniye isano n’ico kintu.

2. **Gukoresha amafaranga y’inguvu mu buryo butaziguye ku ncuro ya mbere muri kahise.

3. **Ibigereranyo bibereye:** Mu kugereranya ikoreshwa ry’inguvu rya Bitcoin n’iry’izindi nzego, turashobora kuronka iciyumviro kiringaniye no gusuzuma ukuri kw’ivyo bivugwa kuri yo.


Ariko mbere, reka twishure ikibazo gikomeye: **Kubera iki Bitcoin ikoresha inguvu?**


Cokimwe n’ingene inguvu zikoreshwa mu nzahabu y’umubiri Mining, abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro ba Bitcoin barakoresha inguvu mu gukurikirana kuronka Bitcoin. Ico gisabwa c’inguvu z’isi nyakuri gishingira intahe umutungo w’ubuhinga bwa none udafatika kw’isi y’umubiri. Ikindi kandi, kubera uruja n’uruza runini rw’abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro kw’isi yose bakoresha inguvu kugira ngo bacunge uruja n’uruza rwa Bitcoin, gukoresha inguvu kugira ngo umuntu aronke Bitcoin bikora nk’uburyo bukomeye bwo kwikingira ugushira hamwe n’ugukoreshwa nabi bidakwiye. Kubera iyo mpamvu, biragoye cane ko ibigo bihurikiye hamwe bifatanya n’abandi gutora iyo nzira canke gukoresha amategeko kugira ngo bibafashe, kuko vyobwirizwa gutsinda abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro batagira uko bangana bari kw’isi yose.


Mu bijanye n’ivyo, reka turabe ingingo zitatu zivugwa haruguru.


#### Ubuntu bw'agaciro


Hari igihe woba warahuye n’imvugo ivuga ko Bitcoin ata gaciro k’imbere ifise, ivyo bikaba bituma wibaza igituma ikwiye kwemererwa gukoresha inguvu.


Nk’uko vyavuzwe mu ciyumviro kitari co ca gatatu, agaciro k’imbere mu mutima ni ikintu umuntu yiyumvira kandi kivana n’ivyo umuntu akeneye be n’ivyo akeneye. Nk’akarorero, niwiyumvire uri mu bugaragwa bushushe, umuntu akaguha ijaketi y’impuzu y’impuzu y’impuzu y’impuzu. Vyoba ari ubusa. None, wiyumvire ko uri mu karere k’ubukonje ka Cold Arctique. Mu kanya nk’ako gukubita, iyo jacket iragira agaciro kanini cane. Ivyo vyerekana ko agaciro katari mu kintu ahubwo ko kagenwa n’aho ikintu kimeze, ibintu vyihariye be n’akamaro ico kintu giha umuntu mu gushitsa ivyo akeneye. Ariko rero, ugushingira intahe ntigushika gusa ku gaciro. Bishika no ku gukoresha inguvu. Iyo ikintu gisaba inguvu kugira ngo gikore, vyerekana neza ko abantu bacironkeramwo agaciro, kuko biteguriye kugitanga umwanya wabo, ubutunzi bwabo n’inguvu zabo.


Buri musi, turabona ingero zitari nke z’ugukoresha inguvu zivuye ku gaciro abantu babona k’ibikorwa bimwebimwe canke inganda zimwezimwe. Ikoreshwa ry’inguvu rifitaniye isano n’ugutuma habaho agaciro, kuva ku gukoresha ibikoresho mu ngo zacu gushika ku Bitcoin Mining gushika ku nguvu zikenewe kugira ngo zihe ubushobozi ibikorwa remezo bininibinini bitwara ubutunzi bwacu.


Rimbura iterambere ryabayeho mu vy’ubuhinga bwa none, mu vy’ugutwara abantu n’ibintu be no mu vy’ukwinezereza uko igihe cagenda kirarengana. Ivyo bintu bishasha akenshi bisaba inguvu nyinshi cane, yamara vyahinduye cane ubuzima bwacu kandi biratuma tugira agaciro kanini cane. Bitcoin ntaco bitandukaniyeko. Yaba ari ukuntu umuntu ashobora gutwara ibintu mu buryo bubereye, amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none akoreshwa n’abandi, canke umunezero uva ku buryo butandukanye bwo kwisamaza, ivyo bintu n’ivyiza biva ku gukoresha inguvu.


Dufise ivyo mu muzirikanyi, birahambaye kwemera ko ukuntu abantu babona agaciro bitandukanye hagati y’abantu n’imiryango. Ivyo umuntu umwe yobona ko ari ugukoresha inguvu bifise akamaro, uwundi yoshobora kubona ko ari ibirenze urugero canke ko bidakenewe. Ariko rero, iyo nzira y’ugushingira intahe ibintu ntikwiye kugabanya ukwemera ko ugukoresha inguvu bifitaniye isano n’agaciro abantu baha ibikorwa bimwebimwe.


Nk’akarorero, abantu benshi babona ko Bitcoin ari uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha inguvu kubera ubushobozi bwayo bwo gutanga uburyo bwo gukorana n’abantu bose, Trustless, kandi ata ruhusha rwo gukoresha ata bahuza. Naho abantu bamwebamwe bo mu bihugu vyateye imbere boshobora kutamenya neza iyo ngingo y’agaciro, irafise akamaro kanini cane ku baba mu bihugu aho ubugenzuzi bwa Leta bubuza abantu gukora kandi n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro bikaba vyinshi. Mu bihe nk’ivyo, ifaranga nka Bitcoin ritanga agaciro kanini cane, ivyo bikaba bituma abantu bari muri ivyo bihe bitegurira gutanga inguvu zabo n’ubutunzi bwabo kugira ngo bashigikire ibikorwa vyaryo.


#### Guhindura amafaranga y'inguvu


Kera, amahinguriro y’amashanyarazi, amatongo akoresha izuba, ibidengeri vy’amazi n’ibindi bisa n’ivyo vyari bishingiye ku kugurisha inguvu zavyo ku rubuga rw’inguvu, ku bantu ku giti cabo canke ku bucuruzi kugira ngo zironke amahera. Ariko rero, ukwo kwizigira abaguzi bo mu karere kenshi kwatuma inguvu zitakoreshwa zitakara igihe ata baguzi bahagije bariho. Ku bw’ivyo, iyo nkuru iratuma haba ico abantu benshi bita inguvu zitagira aho zigarukira, aho inguvu zikorwa ariko zitagira uwundi ntumbero canke uwuzigura, amaherezo zigapfa ubusa. Umuntu yoshobora gutanga iciyumviro co kubika inguvu zirenga urugero mu mabati, ariko ikibabaje ni uko ubuhinga bw’amabati bufise aho bugarukira, ivyo bituma ivyo biba umuti udashoboka.


Kandi niho Bitcoin yinjira.Ku ncuro ya mbere muri kahise, Bitcoin irashoboza gukoresha inguvu mu buryo butaziguye.


Abahingura inguvu ubu barashobora guhindura inguvu zitagira aho zigarukira zija kuri Bitcoin Mining, bikaba bituma bashobora kuronka Bitcoin ku nguvu zitakoreshejwe. Ubwo buryo bushasha ntibugabanura cane gusa inguvu zikoreshwa ubusa, ariko kandi buratuma habaho inyungu z’inyongera mbere zitari zishobora gushikwako. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo nyungu nshasha ifasha kugabanya igiciro c’inguvu muri rusangi ku bandi bose, nk’uko mw’isoko ry’inguvu ry’agaciro, igiciro c’inguvu kirimwo n’igiciro c’inguvu zitagira aho zigarukira. Kubera iki? Mu gukoresha Bitcoin Mining kugira ngo bakoreshe amahera muri izo nguvu mbere zitakoreshwa, abahingura inguvu barashobora gusubiza inyuma ivyo bakoresha maze bagashikana inyungu ku baguzi, bikagabanya ibiciro vy’inguvu.


Mu kwagura ico ciyumviro, uruzitiro rwacu rw’inguvu rwagenewe gukora n’ubushobozi burenze urugero, mu bisanzwe rukoresha gusa 40-60% vy’inguvu rushobora gutanga mu gihe ico ari co cose. Iryo tegeko ryo kwirinda rituma uruzitiro rushobora kwihuta kwakira ivyuka vy’inguvu bitari bitezwe mu gihe c’ibintu nk’ibihe bikomeye cane, nk’imipfunda y’ubushuhe canke ibihe vy’ubushuhe bwa Cold, igihe abantu bakoresha cane ibikoresho vyo gutuma umuyaga ugera mu nzu canke ibikoresho vyo gushushanya. Kubera ko abahingura inguvu badashobora guca bongera umusaruro wabo kugira ngo bashobore guhura n’ukwiyongera kw’abazisaba bukwi na bukwi, gutanga ingufu zirengeye biraba ngombwa, bikaba bizana amafaranga menshi y’itunga be n’ubushobozi bwo gukoresha ingufu ubusa.


Kandi ivyo gusesagura ntibisa n’ibizotera imbere vuba. Uko inkomezi z’umuyaga zihinduka, kandi uburemere bw’izuba bugabanuka iyo ibicu bipfutse, inguvu z’umuyaga zica zikikuje . [15-30%](http://anemoiservices.com/amakuru-y'inganda/umuyagankuba-ukora-ungahe/#:~:text=Igihe%20hariho%20umuyaga20ugenda buhoro,ku%20hafi%2015%39,2020) inguvu z’izuba ziza hafi [16-24%](inguvu z’izuba zikora neza cane) zikora neza. Hakurikijwe imigambi yacu yo guhindukira tuja mu kwizigira 100% inkomoko z’inguvu zishobora gusubirwamwo, biraba ngombwa ko tugira ubushobozi bw’inguvu nibura incuro zitatu z’ivyo uruzitiro rukeneye. Ubwo bushobozi burengeye burakenewe kugira ngo uruzitiro rugumye ruhagaze neza iyo Supply ihagaze, bigabanye ingorane zo kuzima. Ariko rero, ivyo bisigura kandi ko igice kinini c’inguvu dukora kizohagarara igihe cose! Izo nguvu nta kindi zifise. Nta n’umwe afise umutima ukunze wo kuyigura.


Ariko ubu abahingura inguvu barafise uburyo bwo gukoresha neza izo nguvu zicitse intege, zikaba zari guca ubusa. Mu gukoresha amahera y’inguvu zisigaye biciye ku Bitcoin Mining, abahingura inguvu barashobora gutuma ibikorwa vyabo bigenda neza, bakavyungukirako mu vy’amahera, maze amaherezo bagabanura ibiciro ku muntu wese ari ku rubuga.


Ubwa nyuma, abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro ba Bitcoin baravyurirwa umutima wo kurondera ingufu zitazimvye kuko inyungu zabo zivana n’igiciro c’inguvu. Ku bw’ivyo, bararondera n’umwete inguvu zipfutse canke ubundi bwoko bw’inguvu iyo zitakoreshwa. Akarorero kamwe gahambaye ni gaze y’umuriro, iyo gaze isohoka iyo amashirahamwe y’amavuta ya peteroli akuye amavuta mu butaka. Gaz y’umuriro ni ikintu kiva muri iyo nzira kandi akenshi iraturirwa kubera amahera menshi ajanye no kuyifata. Uwo mugenzo uzwi kw’izina ry’ugusha, ntutuma gusa umuntu atakaza inguvu, ariko kandi urarekura metane n’ibindi bidukikije bitandukanye mu kirere.


![image](assets/4.webp)


_**Igishushanyo:** Igikoresho co gutera umuriro [Gaz](2022/09/ugutera umuriro-mu-inganda-ya-amavuta-nti-gikora-bike-kuru-kw'inyigisho-y'ivyiyumviro/)_


Ariko rero, kubera Bitcoin, abahinga barateguye uburyo bwo gukoresha iyo gaze kavukire ubundi yari gutakaza ubusa mu kuyihindura inguvu zo guha ubushobozi abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro ba Bitcoin. Iryo terambere ntiritanga gusa inyungu z’inyongera kuri ayo mashirahamwe, ariko kandi rirafise akamaro kanini ku bidukikije. Mu gukoresha gazi y’umuriro ku muyagankuba wa generate ku Bitcoin Mining, ayo mashirahamwe arashobora [kugabanya ivyuka bihumanya ikirere](https://batcoinz.com/kugereranya-ingaruka-zo-gukoresha-metane-ifatanye-ku-muyagankuba-wa Bitcoin. Mu vy’ukuri, Bitcoin ni carbone-negative muri iki gihe mu gutanga uburyo bwo kugabanya ivyuka bihumanya ikirere no gukoresha neza inkomoko z’inguvu zari zatawe mbere.


Muri vyose, kubera ko abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro ba Bitcoin baremeshwa kurondera amasoko y’inguvu ataco atwara, akenshi bagakunda inguvu zishobora gusubirwamwo, Bitcoin irashima kimwe mu [vyinshi . n’inguvu zivanze hagati y’inganda mbere n’ibihugu. Rero, igihe kizoza umuntu azovyura ivyiyumviro ku bijanye n’ibirenge vya Bitcoin ku bidukikije, urashobora gusubiza n’ukwizigira ko Bitcoin iri imbere mu migenzo y’inguvu ziramvye.


Kandi ubwanyuma...


#### Igereranyo ryiza


Turashaka gutangura tuvuga ngo: **Ibintu vyose bifata inguvu**, twaba tubibona canke tutabibona. Mbere n’igikorwa coroshe, nk’ukwirukana n’imbwa yawe, birasaba ko wewe ubwawe wiha amavuta be n’uwo mufatanije ubwoya. Wewe n’imbwa yawe muri abakoresha inguvu.


Ubu rero umugambi wacu si uwo kunegura izindi nganda kubera uko zikoresha inguvu kuko nk’uko twabibonye haruguru, gukoresha inguvu bisobanura agaciro abantu basanga mu bikorwa canke mu bicuruzwa bitangwa. Ariko rero, ni ngombwa ko umuntu abona neza ingene Bitcoin ikoresha inguvu. Rimbura ibi bikurikira [ibigereranyo] (https:



- Imashini zo gumesa zirarya [18%](https://energypedia.info/wiki/Isi_yose_yo_kuzigama_mu_mashini_yo_mu_rugo#:~:text=Uyu musi%2C%20840%20miliyoni%20y'amazi yo mu rugo,hafi%2%20m20k. inguvu kuruta Bitcoin.
- Inzahabu Mining n’amabuye y’agaciro bikoresha inguvu nyinshi incuro cumi kuruta Bitcoin.
- Ugutwara abantu n’ibintu mu kiyaga bikoresha inguvu zirenga incuro 51 kuruta Bitcoin.
- Uruganda rw’ivy’ubutunzi n’ubwishingizi rukoresha inguvu zitangaje incuro 62 kuruta Bitcoin.
- Kandi igitangaje ni uko urwego rw’inyubako rukoresha inguvu zitangaje incuro 457 kuruta izo Bitcoin zikoresha.


Dusuzumye izo ngero zigereranywa, biragaragara ko imbere yo guca urubanza ku bijanye n’inguvu za Bitcoin, dutegerezwa kurimbura ingufu zikoreshwa n’izindi nganda. Ukwo kubona ibintu bituma umuntu ashobora gutahura neza cane ivyerekeye inguvu zagutse.


Ikindi kandi, iyo turimbuye ivyiza vyinshi Bitcoin itanga, harimwo:



- Ugushikira amabanki ku banyagihugu batagira amabanki
- Ibikorwa vy'ubucuruzi kw'isi yose hagati y'urunganwe n'urunganwe ata bahuza
- Uburyo bwo kohereza amahera buzimvye ku bantu ku giti cabo kugira ngo bohereze amahera imiryango yabo
- Trustless n'uburyo bw'amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none ata ruhusha
- Uburyo ababa mu ntwaro z’agahomerabunwa boshobora kuzigama no gutwara agaciro ata nkomanzi
- Guhindura amafaranga y'inguvu zitagira aho zigarukira


Turaronka ugutahura kwimbitse kw’igituma abantu batabona gusa agaciro kanini cane muri Bitcoin ariko kandi bakaba biteguye gukoresha inguvu zabo mu gukora kwayo.


Kugira ngo dusozere, twizigiye ko ivyo vyiyumviro bitari vyo vya Bitcoin vyaguhaye ugutahura kwimbitse kuri Bitcoin birenze ivyo kunegura ku rugero rwo hejuru kenshi ironka. Ubu rero iyo umuntu asuzumye neza, vyoshobora kugaragara ko vyinshi muri ivyo bintu binegurwa vyerekana ko ata shingiro bifise. Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, ni igihe co gukuraho ivyiyumviro bitari vyo vyerekana Bitcoin, tukabishira ku gutahura neza uburyo bw’ivy’ubutunzi bwagutse. Mu kubigira, turashobora gukora kugira ngo haboneke uburyo bubereye kandi buringaniye, bufitiye akamaro bose, atari abafise ububasha gusa.


Reka noneho twibande ku vyiyumviro bitari vyo abantu benshi bafise ku bijanye n’amahera y’amahera...


### Ivyiyumviro bitari vyo vyerekeye Stablecoin


1. Ivyuma vyinshi bihoraho ntibishigikirwa bimwe bishitse n’ibizigamirwa .

2. Mbere n’ivyo bikomeye kuruta ibindi vyose vy’amahera bikomeye depeg .

3. Kubera ko amafaranga menshi aguma ari ahantu hamwe, uwuyatanga arashobora guhagarika amafaranga yawe

4. Uzotakaza amahera yawe iyo uruzitiro ruri munsi rwamanutse .

5. Bitcoin na stablecoins zompi zifasha abatunzi bo mu bihugu biri mu nzira y’amajambere .


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca mbere: Ivyuma vyinshi bihoraho ntibishigikiwe bimwe bishitse n’ibizigamirwa .


Igihe umuntu atahura amafaranga y’ibiceri, ni ngombwa kwemera ko amafaranga y’ibiceri vyose akora hakurikijwe ingingo ngenderwako n’imirongo ngenderwako yihariye. Imigambi imwimwe y’amahera y’agaciro yerekana umwete udasanzwe n’uguseruka mu gutanga amakuru arambuye yerekeye amafaranga yabo yazigamye no gusohora ubudasiba ivyemezo bibigenzura.


Nk’akarorero, Tether ishigikira cane uguseruka kuboneka mu bimenyetso vyabo, bishobora gushikwako kugira ngo umuntu aronke ubumenyi ku bijanye n’ugushigikira kwabo kw’ububiko hano. Ivyo bimenyetso bikora nk’igihe c’ikimenyamenya c’uko Commitment yabo ishira imbere umukiriya.


Ariko rero, ivyo si ko biri ku bice vyose vy’amahera bihoraho, aho vyinshi bitatanga urugero rumwe rw’uguseruka. Ntidushobora rero gushimika ku kamaro ko gukora ubushakashatsi bwimbitse imbere y’uko twizigira ubutunzi buhambaye igiceri ico ari co cose gikomeye. Ikindi, hariho urugero rw’ukwizigira uwukoresha ategerezwa gushiramwo uwutanga stablecoin, ataravye urugero rw’uguseruka.


Ikindi kintu gikunze kunegurwa ni uko amafaranga y'amahera akenshi adashigikirwa n'amahera ahubwo "amahera n'amahera angana na yo." _Iri ni ijambo ry'ubuhinga ry'amahera n'ibisigazwa bimeze nk'amahera bishobora guhindurwa bitagoranye bikaba amahera_. Ariko rero, birahambaye ko turimbura ingingo zibiri:


Ica mbere, abatanga stablecoin kenshi bashiramwo amahera angana aho gufata amahera, kuko amahera ashobora kugira ingaruka zikomeye ku rutonde rw’amahera y’uwutanga stablecoin. Kubera amategeko agenga amabanki ariho ubu, umutungo wose wo mu gitabu c’amahera, nk’amahera, urashobora gutakaza iyo ushobora gusenyuka, kandi ishirahamwe ry’ubwishingizi bw’amafaranga y’igihugu (FDIC) ritanga gusa ubwishingizi bushika ku madolari 250.000 y’Amerika, amahera arenga iyo nzira akaba ari mu kaga. Kugira ngo ivyo bigabanywe, amafaranga y’amahera agumaho afise intumbero yo kurinda abayakoresha ibintu bitari bitezwe, akenshi ashira amahera mu mafaranga y’itunga atangazwa na Leta. Mu gushiramwo amafaranga nk’amatunga, ntibitanga umwimbu gusa, ivyo bintu bishobora gufatwa nk’ivy’ubutunzi bitari mu gitabu c’ubutunzi. Ivyo bituma abatanga amafaranga y’amahera y’agaciro (stablecoin) bashobora kurinda amahera yabo iyo banki yoba yacitse intege, kuko ayo mafaranga yoshobora gusubirwamwo umukiriya. Ikigereranyo gikomeye c’ivyo cabaye muri Ruhuhuma/Ntwarante 2023, kirimwo Silicon Valley Bank (SVB) na Circle, ishirahamwe riri inyuma y’amahera y’i USDC. Iciyo gihe, Circle yari ifise amahera menshi cane [\$3.3]. miliyari](www.coindesk.com/ubucuruzi/2023/03/11/uruziga-rwemeza-33b-y'amafaranga-yabitswe-ya-usdcs-yafashe-ku-silic-yananiwe on-valley-bank/#:~:text=Igiceri%20gitanga%20Umuzingi%20wavuze%20cerewe,ububiko%20bushigikiye%20Igiceri%20Umuzingi%20USDC.) mu mafaranga yashizwe muri SVB. Kandi rero, SVB yaracitse intege. Kugira ngo FDIC ntihagire icago c’amahera, yarafashe ingingo yo gukiza Circle n’izindi sosiyete zashikiwe n’ico kiza mu gupfuka amahera yari yabuze. Ariko rero, ivyo si vyo bimenyerewe. Ico kintu kitari bwigere kiba, ni co cabaye ubwa mbere muri kahise ibintu nk’ivyo vyabaye. Iyo FDIC itagira ico ikoze, Circle na yo nyene yari gushobora gusenyuka.


Ubwa kabiri, kenshi turanegura abatanga amafaranga y’amafaranga (stablecoin) kubera ko bashiramwo amahera mu bintu bitari amahera, yamara uburyo bwacu bwo gukoresha amabanki buriho bukora ku buryo bw’ububiko bw’ibice. Mu majambo yoroshe, amabanki ntagira amahera ahagije kugira ngo ashobore gutanga amahera abakiriya bayo basaba. Iyo igice kinini c’abanyagihugu cacu bakura amahera yabo, urwego rw’amabanki rwoca rusenyuka ningoga. Nkako, kuva mu mwaka w’2020, igisabwa co kubika amahera muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika cashizwe kuri [zero](https://www.federalreserve.gov/monetarypolicy/reservereq.htm), bisobanura ko amabanki adategetswe kubika **IYO YOSE** y’abaguzi.


Turashaka gusobanukirwa neza. Ivyo vyiyumviro ntibisigura ko dukwiye kwirengagiza ivyiyumviro vyerekeye amafaranga y’amafaranga asubirira amafaranga y’ibizigamirwa n’itunga ryoshobora gutakaza agaciro, bikaba bishobora gutuma amafaranga y’amafaranga adahinduka. Ahubwo, dukwiye kwemera ko hariho ingingo ngenderwako zibiri hagati y’ivy’ubutunzi bwa kera n’ubuhinga bwa none.


Muri vyose, naho hariho ivyiyumviro bitari vyo ku bijanye n’ibiceri bikomeye, kandi bikaba bibereye mu bihe vyinshi, birahambaye kwemera ko ibiceri vyose bikomeye bikora mu buryo bwihariye, bifise ingero zitandukanye z’uguseruka n’umwete. Mu gukora ubushakashatsi bwimbitse ku stablecoin iyo ari yo yose uhisemwo kubikamwo agaciro, urashobora kugabanya imitego myinshi isanzwe ijana n’amahera y’ibanga.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca kabiri: Mbere n’amahera akomeye cane depeg .


Ku bijanye n’iciyumviro kitari co c’uko mbere n’isoko ry’amahera ry’agaciro kuruta ayandi yose ryitwa stablecoins depeg, birahambaye gutandukanya isoko ry’intango n’iry’inyuma.


Isoko rya mbere ririho hagati y’uwutanga amafaranga y’agaciro, ni ukuvuga Tether, n’amahinguriro y’intango afise ubushobozi bwo Redeem umutungo w’agaciro, nk’amadolari y’Amerika, canke gutanga amafaranga y’agaciro kugira ngo igiciro kigume gishikamye. Ivyo bikorwa vy’isoko ry’intango bituma igice c’ifeza kiguma gifatanye cane n’agaciro kaco kagenewe.


Ku rundi ruhande, isoko rya kabiri riri hagati y’abaguzi n’abagurisha. Aho niho abantu ku giti cabo bashobora kugura no kugurisha stablecoins, haba mu gucuruza, mu gushiramwo amahera canke ikindi cose umutima wabo wipfuza.


Depeg ibaho iyo stablecoin itagifise amafaranga akenewe kugira ngo ishobore gushitsa ivyo abayifise basaba canke iyo habaye hack ishobora gutuma stablecoin ihungabana. Ariko rero, birahambaye kumenya ko uguhinduka kw’ibiciro kw’igihe gito gushikirwa n’ibiceri bihoraho bitagaragaza ko hariho depeg. Ahubwo kenshi biva ku bibazo vy’amahera.


Reka tubisigure. Twibaze ko Exchange ntoyi cane idafise ubushobozi bwo Redeem umutungo w’agaciro, kandi hariho umukazo ukomeye wo kugurisha uva ku bantu barondera gukuraho umutungo w’agaciro ushigikiye stablecoin. Muri ivyo, igiciro c’ico gice c’ifeza coshobora kugwa munsi y’igiciro caco ciza. Ukwo guhunga kw’igihe gito kuva ku nkoko ni ikintu kiba mu gihe gito kandi gikwiye gusubira mu buryo busanzwe igihe Exchange imaze kuronka ivy’ishimikiro bikenewe kugira ngo ishobore gushitsa ivyo umukiriya wayo akeneye. Ukwo guhinduka kw’igiciro kw’igihe gito ntikwerekana ko stablecoin yananiwe kandi iriko irasenyuka. Ahubwo, vyerekana ingero z’amahera ziri hasi zigira ingaruka ku bushobozi bw’abakoresha bwo gukura amahera ku gihe.


Ku ruhande rumwe, birashoboka kandi kwihweza ubudandaji bw’amahera y’agaciro hejuru y’igiciro cabo. Ivyo bishika iyo ivyipfuzo vy’amahera y’agaciro birenze ubushobozi bwa Exchange bwo gushitsa ivyo abakiriya basaba. Mu bisanzwe, ico kintu kiba ku masoko mato mato atagira isano ry’ukuri n’igiceri gikomeye kandi igihe umutungo w’ishimikiro ufise agaciro kanini, bikaba bituma abantu bariha amahera y’imbere kugira ngo bawuronke. Nk’akarorero, rimbura ikintu cobaye aho abantu baba mu gihugu c’ubutegetsi bw’agahomerabunwa gifise ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro gukomeye barondera ubuhungiro mu bice vy’amahera bihoraho nk’amadolari y’Amerika. Muri ivyo bihe, abantu boshobora kwemera kwishura amahera y’imbere kugira ngo bashobore kuronka amadolari mu buryo bwa USDt. Uwo mutima ukunze uva ku gutahura ko iyo batabigira vyotuma ubushobozi bwabo bwo kugura bugabanuka cane bitewe n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro.


Mu bijanye n’ivyo, uguhinduka kw’ibiciro kuri hanze y’amaboko y’abatanga stablecoin, nka Tether, kuko badakora Interface ataco baciyeko n’umukiriya. Ahubwo abakiriya baronka USDt biciye mu guhinduranya. Ni co gituma bizigira Exchange kugira ngo bagumane amafaranga ahagije y’amahera y’imbere mu gihugu kugira ngo bashobore guhabwa ivyo abakiriya babo bakeneye.


Mu ncamake, igihe kizoza stablecoin icuruzwa hejuru canke munsi y’igiciro cayo gitegekanijwe, menya neza itandukaniro riri hagati y’uguhinduka kw’igiciro mu gihe gito bitewe n’ibibazo vy’amahera n’ikintu nyakuri co gukuraho amahera.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca gatatu: Kubera ko amafaranga menshi aguma ari ahantu hamwe, uwuyatanga arashobora gufunga amahera yawe


Mu gutorera umuti iciyumviro kitari co c’uko amafaranga y’ama stablecoins ashobora guhagarika amafaranga yawe kubera ko ari ahantu hamwe, birahambaye ko ushimika ku ntandukaniro iri hagati y’ibigo bishizwe hamwe n’ibigo bishizwe ahantu hamwe, kimwe cose kikaba gifise ivyiza n’ibibi vyaco. Naho dushigikira cane imitungo yegerejwe nka Bitcoin, ivyo ntibisigura ko amafaranga yegerejwe atagira agaciro canke inyungu.


Kimwe mu vyiza nyamukuru vyo gushiramwo ibintu vyose hamwe ni ubushobozi bwo kwinjiramwo igihe ari mu nyungu z’abakoresha n’ugushikama kw’urutonde muri rusangi. Naho ari ukuri, abatanga amafaranga y’ama stablecoins barafise ubushobozi bwo guhagarika amafaranga. Mu bihe vyose, ivyo ntibikoreshwa nk’igitero kibi ku wufise stablecoin. Ahubwo ni mu gufatanya n’abajejwe gukurikiza amategeko kugira ngo bakingire abaguzi. Akarorero gakomeye ni akajanye n’ugusenyuka kw’indege ya FTX Exchange. Mu gukorana n’abajejwe gukurikiza amategeko, Tether yahagaritse [\$46 millions](https://www.coindesk.com/business/2022/11/10/) y’amadolari y’Amerika kugira ngo ikingire amafaranga y’abaguzi.


Iyindi nkuru yerekana inyungu z’ugufasha mu rwego rwo hejuru yabaye inyuma y’aho [KuCoin hack](https://cointelegraph.com/news/tether-freezes-150-million-in-usdt) ikorewe muri Nzero 2020. Izo ngero zirerekana ingene amafaranga y’amahera ashizwe hamwe, mu bihe bimwebimwe, ashobora kwishura ningoga abakora ivy’ububisha no kurinda inyungu z’abayakoresha.


Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, naho dushira imbere Bitcoin ku kuzigama kw’igihe kirekire kubera ukubura abahuza canke abantu bashobora gukorana n’urubuga, amafaranga y’amafaranga ashizwe hamwe aracari afise inyungu nyinshi, ni ukuvuga mu gihe kamere y’amafaranga ashizwe hamwe ishobora gutuma amafaranga ashobora gukonja kandi ashobora gukoreshwa nabi mu gukingira abakoresha.


#### Iciyumviro kitari co ca kane: Uzotakaza amahera yawe iyo uruzitiro ruri munsi yayo rumanutse .


Kimwe mu vyiyumviro bitari vyo abantu benshi bafise ku bijanye n’amahera y’amahera ni uko uzotakaza amahera yawe iyo uruzitiro rw’inyuma rw’amahera y’amahera rugenda rumanuka. Twebwe rero, twumva ko ari ngirakamaro gusigura ingene amafaranga adahinduka akora ku nzira zayo zo gutwara Layer, nka TRON, Ethereum, na Algorand, n’izindi. Naho mu ntango vyoshobora gusa n’ibiteye ubwoba gutakaza uburenganzira bwo kuronka amafaranga yawe igihe uruzitiro ruri munsi rwarashikiwe n’ingorane, uzonezerwa kumenya ko hariho ingingo zihari zo kurinda amafaranga yawe.


Fata nk’akarorero USDt. Benshi bagwa mu mutego wo kwiyumvira ko USD ishigikira USDt yicaye ku nzira y'ugutwara abantu Layer. Mu vy’ukuri, USD ifatwa mu bubiko bwa Tether atari mu buryo butaziguye n’uruzitiro ruri munsi yayo. Rero, iyo uruzitiro ufiseko USDt rushikiwe n’ikibazo, ntibisigura ko amafaranga y’ububiko bw’amadolari y’Amerika atakaye. Ahubwo, kimwe muri ivyo bintu bibiri birashobora gushika:


1. Akenshi, uguhungabana kw’uruzitiro ruri munsi y’uruzitiro ni uguhungabana kw’igihe gito, kandi uruzitiro ruzosubira gukora vuba. Ivyo bicitse intege kenshi biratorwa umuti, bikaba bituma abakoresha basubira kuronka amafaranga yabo agumaho.

2. Mu bihe bikomeye cane, nk’ugusenyuka gukomeye canke ukunanirwa kw’uruzitiro, Tether irashobora gufata ingingo yo gukosora. Bashobora gushinga urubuga rwo gutegura abafise USDt z’uruzitiro rudakora. Biciye kuri uru rubuga, abakoresha barashobora rero kwemeza Ownership y’ibimenyetso vyabo vya USDt bakoresheje imfunguruzo zabo z’ibanga. Ownership imaze kwemezwa, Tether irashobora guturira ibimenyetso vya USDt bitakora bifiswe n’abakoresha maze ikabisubiramwo ku ruhererekane rukora. Ivyo bimenyetso vya USDt vyasubiwemwo bica birungikirwa ababikoresha, bikaba bituma amahera yabo abandanya.


Ivyo bishizwe mu muzirikanyi, hariho ingingo zihari ko naho uruzitiro ruri munsi y’amahera y’agaciro rwohura n’ingorane, abatanga amafaranga y’agaciro barafise intambwe bashobora gutera kugira ngo ushobore gusubirana amahera yawe.


Mu ncamake, naho ari ibisanzwe kugira amaganya yo gutakaza uburenganzira bwo kuronka amahera yawe iyo uruhererekane rw’ishimikiro rw’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera y’amahera.


Imbere yo gutera imbere, turashaka gushimika, kandi, ko stablecoin yose ikora mu buryo butandukanye. Ni ngombwa rero ko ukora ubushakashatsi ku bijanye n’amahera yose ushaka gukoresha kugira ngo umenye neza ingingo zo gukingira amahera y’abaguzi.


**Iciyumviro**


Kugira ngo duheze... Nimwibuke, Bitcoin n’ibiceri bikomeye bitera intambwe mu buryo busanzwe imiterere y’ububasha n’ubukuru bwa Leta vyashinzwe, ivyo bikaba bituma abantu basubira inyuma. Vyinshi muri ivyo birwanya akenshi biva ku bwoba bwo guhungabanya uburyo bw’ivy’ubutunzi buriho no gushidikanya ku kuntu intwaro zigenzura amafaranga n’ingingo mfatirwako z’ivy’ubutunzi. Ivyo bivuzwe, ivyo vyose ivyo gusubira inyuma ntibishingiye ku vy’ukuri. Ni ngombwa rero kwegera ivyo binegura dufise umutima wo kunegura.


Mu gusuzuma ataco wishimikije ikintu cose cogusubiza inyuma, urashobora guca neza mu kiyaga c’ugunegura ata shingiro. Fata ingingo yo kwigisha ku bijanye n’ibintu bigoranye vya Bitcoin n’ibiceri bikomeye, winjire mu buhinga bwavyo, kandi urushirize gutohoza ubushobozi bwavyo bwo guhingura ibintu bishasha mu vy’amahera no gutanga ubushobozi.


Mu mpera, kazoza k’ivy’ubutunzi bwegerejwe abantu bose kari ku bashaka gukora ibintu birenze urugero rw’amasezerano, bagatera umukono ku vyiyumviro vyari vyarashizweho, no gusuzuma amakuru ataco bishimikije. Niwihatire gufata ingingo zishingiye ku bumenyi bubereye no gutahura neza ubushobozi bwazo n’aho zigarukira.


## Roya Mahboob


<chapterId>0b6f7ce6-69be-5735-b34c-b1822ff23356</chapterId>


Mu isi y’ubu y’isi yose, kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’ubutunzi ni ikintu gihambaye cane mu bijanye no kugira uruhara mu vy’ubutunzi no kwigenga. Naho ari ukwo, abantu benshi cane baracari hanze y’uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki, abagore bakaba ari bo akenshi bikorera umutwaro w’ukwo hanze. Igiteye ubwoba ni uko naho [ica kane] c’abantu bo kw’isi yose kidakenewe kiguma kitagira amabanki, mu bihugu nka Arabiya Saudite, [36.5%](https://ibirimwo.11fs.com/ingingo/ubushobozi-bw'ivy'amahera-n'itandukaniro-ry'uburinganire-mu-burasirazuba-hagati#:~:text=Mu%20myaka%20iheze,63.5%25%20%2D%0ft20 abagabo. ibikorwa vy’ishimikiro vy’amabanki, bikababuza kugira uruhara rwuzuye mu bukungu n’imibano y’igihugu cabo.


Akira ingero nkeyi gusa z'ibintu abagore bo kw'isi yose bakihanganira n'ubu:


1. Amategeko agenga gufungura konti muri banki: Mu bihugu [72](https://www3.weforum.org/docs/WEF_GGGR_2020.pdf) kw’isi yose, abagore ntibemerewe gufungura konti muri banki mw’izina ryabo bwite. Ivyo bisigura ko badashobora kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’amahera, kuzigama amahera canke kwigenzura mu buzima bwabo bw’ivy’amahera.

2. Gushingira ku ncuti z’abagabo: Mu bihugu vyinshi vy’abavyeyi, abagore baravyifatamwo neza mu ncuti z’abagabo kugira ngo babafashe mu vy’amahera. Ivyo bisigura ko badashobora kwifatira ingingo z’ivy’amahera kandi akenshi baba bari ku mbabazi z’incuti zabo z’abagabo. Nk'akarorero, muri Afghanistan, abagore kenshi bategerezwa kwizigira abagabo bo mu muryango kugira ngo babafashe mu vy'amahera, kandi bashobora kutaronka ubufasha bw'amahera ata ruhusha rw'umugabo abarera.

3. Uguhagarika akazi: Mu bihugu bimwebimwe, abagore ntibemerewe gukora hanze y’urugo, ivyo bikaba bituma bagorwa no kwigenga mu vy’amahera. Nk’akarorero, muri Siriya, Iraki, Afghanistan, Alijeriya, Palestina, Yorodani na Irani, abagore bagize gusa hagati ya [15 - 18%](ibihugu-aho-abagore-bashobora-kwinjira-mu-gikorwa-gikora.html).

4. Kubura uburenganzira bw’umutungo: Haracariho [75](https://blogs.worldbank.org/opendata/aho-isi-abagore-bakiri-bahanganye n’intambamyi-zijanye n’amategeko zo kwitunga no gutwara-itunga) kw’isi yose aho abagore badafise uburenganzira bwo kwitunga nk’uko ubushobozi bwabo bwo kwitunga bugarukira. Ivyo bituma bibagora gutangura ubudandaji canke kuronka inguzanyo, kuko ata n’ingwati bafise botanga. Nk'akarorero, mu bice bimwebimwe vyo mu buhinde, abagore ntibemerewe kugira umutungo, kandi bashobora kutaronka inguzanyo ata ruhusha rw'incuti y'umugabo.


Izo ni ingero nkeyi gusa z’ubwoko bw’intambamyi abagore bo mu mibano myinshi yo muri iki gihe bakiriho mu bijanye no kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’amahera no gushika ku kwigenga mu vy’amahera.


Ukwo kutaronka ibikorwa vy’ishimikiro bituma abo bagore bagorwa cane no kwigenga mu vy’ubutunzi no kwigenzura mu buzima bwabo bw’ubutunzi. Ariko rero, hariho icizigiro kiri imbere. Kuva Bitcoin itera imbere, abo bagore ubu barafise umuti w’ico kibazo. Biciye ku nzira yoroshe ya internet, ubu barashobora gukoresha Trustless, uburyo butagira uruhusha kandi bushizwe ahantu hamwe bw’ubuhinga bwa Exchange, ubwo inganda za kera z’amabanki zananiwe gutanga. Bitcoin iriko iraha ubushobozi abagore basigaye inyuma n’ubuhinga bwa kera bw’ivy’ubutunzi.


Reka turabe akarorero kamwe nk'ako k'ingene Bitcoin yahinduye ubuzima bw'abagore...


Afghanistan ni igihugu kimaze imyaka mirongo gishikiwe n'intambara, kandi ivy'abagore muri ico gihugu biragoye cane. Intwaro y'agahahazo y'abatalibani, yatwaye kuva mu 1996 gushika mu 2001, yambuye abagore uburenganzira bwabo bw'ishimikiro, harimwo uburenganzira bwo kwiga n'uburenganzira bwo gukora. Naho aba Taliban bamaze gutemba, abagore bo muri Afghanistan barabandanya guhura n’ingorane zikomeye, harimwo ukuntu badashobora kwiga no kuronka akazi, be n’ukuntu badashobora kwigenga mu vy’amahera.


Ariko mu myaka iheze, Bitcoin yaraserutse nk’igikoresho gikomeye co guha ubushobozi abagore mu vy’amahera, cane cane abagore bakunda gushirwa ku ruhande. Umuntu umwe yakoresheje neza ubushobozi bwa Bitcoin ni [Roya Mahboob](https://twitter.com/royamahboob), umucuruzi w’umunya Afghanistan yakoresheje amafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none kugira ngo afashe abagore bo mu gihugu ciwe kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’ubutunzi no gusubira kuronka icubahiro cabo.


Mu gihe isi yose yariko iraraba n’ubwoba bwinshi igihe aba Taliban bafata ubutegetsi bwa Afghanistan mu 1914. 1996, kuba mu mutima w’intambara. Yari afise imyaka indwi gusa, yasanze afashwe n’umuvurungano n’ukudakeka kw’intambara igihe igisagara ciwe c’amavukiro cariko kiraterwa n’Abatalibani maze kigafatwa. Naho yari afise akaga n’amagorwa, hejuru y’uko atashobora kuja kw’ishure, Roya yaranse gutsindwa. Ahubwo yaciye afata inyigisho nk’uburyo bwo gutsinda imipaka yari yamushizeko kubera ukuntu ivyari vyifashe.


![image](assets/5.webp)


\***Igishushanyo:** [Roya Mahboob]


Roya Mahboob ni umuhinga mu vy’ubuhinga n’ubudandaji muri Afghanistan. Si we gusa yashizwe mu rutonde rw'abantu 100 bafise akosho kanini kw'isi mu mwaka w'2013 inyuma y'aho yubakiye amashure yisumbuye yo kuri internet mu mashure yisumbuye muri Afghanistan. Yashinze kandi ishirahamwe ry'ubuhinga bwa none ryitwa Afghan Citadel Software Company mu mwaka w'2010, rigamije "guha akazi abaherutse gusozera amashure yisumbuye cane cane abagore." Kandi iyo ivyo bitahagije, yaciye abandanya atanguza ikigega c’abanyagihugu ca Digital. Iryo shirahamwe ritagira inyungu rikora ivyo guha ubushobozi abagore n’abana bo mu bihugu biri mu nzira y’amajambere biciye mu buhinga bwa none.


Ariko rero, muri urwo rugendo rwose, Roya ntiyari wenyene. Bitcoin yerekanye ko ari igikoresho c’agaciro kanini mu gikorwa ciwe co guha ubushobozi abagore. Naho yari afise intambamyi nyinshi, harimwo n’intambamyi z’amategeko zibuza abagore gukora no gufungura amakonti muri banki, Roya yari yiyemeje kurondera uburyo bwo kuriha abo bagore bariko barakorana na we.


Aho niho Bitcoin yinjiye... Kubera ko gufata Bitcoin bitasaba ko nyirayo aba afise konti ya banki ya kera, uwufise internet wese arashobora kuyikoresha. Ivyo bisigura ko abagore bo muri Afghanistan bashobora kuba badashobora kuronka ubufasha bwa banki busanzwe bashobora kuronka ubufasha bw’amahera biciye ku Bitcoin.


Rero, kubera Trustless yayo, ibiranga ata ruhusha n’ugushirwa ahantu hamwe, yatanze ubuzima kuri abo bagore bari barafunzwe mbere mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubutunzi bwa kera.


Roya Mahboob yarabonye ubwo bushobozi kuva akiri muto, aca atangura kubushira mu bikorwa vyiwe n’ikigega c’abanyagihugu c’ubuhinga bwa none. Yabonye ko Bitcoin ishobora gutanga uburyo abagore bo muri Afghanistan bashobora kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’amahera no kugenzura ubuzima bwabo bw’ivy’amahera.


Uburyo bumwe Roya Mahboob yakoresheje Bitcoin ni biciye muri porogarama yitwa Fondation d’Annexe des Femmes. Ishirahamwe ry’abagore ryitwa Women’s Annex Foundation ni urubuga rutanga inyigisho n’akazi ku bagore bo muri Afghanistan. Biha abagore akaryo ko gukora ibintu nk’ama blogs, amasanamu, n’ivyo bashira ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi. Ivyo birimwo rero birasangizwa ku rubuga rwa Women’s Annex, bikabafasha kwifatanya n’abantu bo kw’isi yose no kuronka amahera mu buryo bwa Bitcoin muri Exchange kubera igikorwa cabo. Ivyo ni ikintu cari kuba kidashoboka mbere y’uko Bitcoin igaragara.

Kuva ryatangura, ishirahamwe Women’s Annex Foundation ryarateye imbere cane, ryafashije abagore batagira uko banganye bo muri Afghanistan kwigenga mu vy’amahera no kugenzura ubuzima bwabo bw’amahera. Iyo abo bagore baronse Bitcoin, barashobora guca mu bigo vy’ivy’imari vya kera, bagashobora kuronka ibikorwa vy’ivy’imari ivyo batashobora kuronka.


Uretse gutanga ubwigenge mu vy’amahera, Bitcoin yarasubije abagore bo muri Afghanistan icubahiro cabo. Kubera ko Bitcoin yegerejwe, yarashoboje abagore kwigenzura mu buzima bwabo bw’amahera ata n’umwe akeneye umugabo abarera. Iyi ni intambwe ikomeye cane mu gihugu aho abagore bafatwa kenshi nk’abanyagihugu bo mu rwego rwa kabiri.


Ikindi kandi, bafashijwe na Mahboob na Bitcoin, abo bagore bo muri Afghanistan ubu barashobora kwifatanya n’abantu bo kw’isi yose. Ni vyiza ko mu myaka izoza, abo bagore bazobandanya babwira isi inkuru zabo n’ukuntu babona ibintu, bagafasha gusenyura intambamyi ziri hagati y’imico kama n’imibano itandukanye.


Muri rusangi, Bitcoin yarabaye igikoresho gikomeye co guha ubushobozi abagore mu vy’amahera.


## Mercedes


<chapterId>dfa10b75-19f6-578a-9d14-a0a541806076</chapterId>


Mercedes yavukiye muri Megizike mu 1949 mu bukene, kandi yarabonye ubusumbasumbane bukomeye bwari buteye akaga abantu bo mu kibano ciwe kuva akiri muto. Mu bwana bwiwe bwose, yarahuye n’ingorane nyinshi, harimwo n’uguhahazwa kwa Leta ku migwi y’abanyeshure be n’intambara zidasanzwe abagore baba mu bukene bashikirwa. Vyongeye, itandukaniro rinini ryari hagati y’abatunzi n’abakene, hamwe n’ukuntu abantu bataronka inyigisho nziza, vyatumye umuryango wiwe n’abandi bantu batagira uko banganye bafatwa n’ubukene. Mercedes yarababajwe cane n’ivyo bikorwa vy’akarenganyo, aca akwegeranya ubumarxiste (ubukomunisita), akavuga ko habaho ihinduka ry’imibano n’ihinduka ry’ubutunzi.


Naho yari afise imyizere ikomeye y’aba Marxiste, Mercedes amaherezo yaraje kwemera ingorane zisanzwe ziri muri izo nzira z’imigenzo ku bijanye n’ubutegetsi n’ugusangira ubutunzi. Ivyo vyatumye arondera ahandi, niho yahura na Bitcoin n’ubushobozi bwayo bwo gutera intambwe uburyo bw’ivy’ubutunzi nyene yari amaze igihe kirekire anegura. Mercedes yavyuriwe umutima n’icizigiro co gutuma abantu bagira umwidegemvyo mu vy’amahera no guhabwa ubushobozi, yaciye ahindura inguvu ziwe mu guharanira ubushobozi bwo guhindura ibintu bwa Bitcoin.


Mu gihugu ciwe c’amavukiro ca Mexique, aho ubukazi bujanye n’ibiyayuramutwe n’ukudatekana kw’ubutunzi bitera abagore mu buryo budasanzwe, Mercedes arakora ataco arushe kugira ngo abo bantu bashobore kuronka Bitcoin nk’uburyo butekanye kandi bundi bwo gucunga amahera yabo. Mu kubigisha ingene boshiraho no gukoresha ama wallets digitales, arabashoboza kurushiriza kugenzura amahera yabo no kuva mu bihe vya kera vy’ubukene n’ubugizi bwa nabi.


Mercedes yizera ko guha ubushobozi abagore ari co kintu nyamukuru co gufungura ubushobozi bwose bwa Bitcoin. Mu guha abagore kw’isi yose uburyo bwo kuronka igitabu Bitcoin n’ibikoresho bikenewe kugira ngo bashobore kugitahura no kugikoresha, yizigiye ko azobashoboza kwikurako ubukene n’agahahazo, bigatuma bo ubwabo n’imiryango yabo bagira kazoza keza.


Ivyo yaciyemwo mu bihugu nka Mozambike, Mexique, Venezuela na Argentine vyerekana ko afise ubushobozi bwo guha ubushobozi abagore biciye mu buhinga bwa none. Muri Mozambike, aho abagore bo mu ntara z’ivyaro badashobora kuronka ubufasha bw’ivy’amahera, Mercedes irafasha abo bagore kumenya ivyerekeye Bitcoin n’ingene yokoreshwa mu gucuruza amahera ata nkomanzi, mu kuzigama amahera ata nkomanzi, no mu kwigenga mu vy’amahera.


Muri Venezuela na Argentine, ibihugu bifise ingorane z’ukudatekana kw’ubutunzi n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro, Mercedes yaragize uruhara runini mu guteza imbere kwemera Bitcoin. Arwana n’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro muri Venezuela kwatumye abagore batagira uko bangana bagorwa no gutunga imiryango yabo mu gushiramwo Bitcoin nk’ifaranga rikomeye cane, bikabaha ubushobozi bwo kurinda amafaranga yabo bazigamye mu Hard no kumenya ko bashobora kuronka ibintu n’ibikorwa vy’ingenzi. Hagati aho, muri Argentine, Mercedes yibanze ku kuyobora abagore bafise ubucuruzi mu nzira yo gushinga ubucuruzi bwabo kugira ngo bemere amahera ya Bitcoin, bikaba vyugururira amahirwe mashasha yo gutera imbere no kwigenga mu vy’ubutunzi mu gihe c’ubutunzi butoroshe.


Commitment ya Mercedes idahungabana ku ngorane zidasanzwe zihanganirwa n’ababa mu bukene, hamwe n’utwigoro twiwe tw’ubutsimvyi two gukuraho itandukaniro hagati y’ubuhinga n’ingaruka z’isi nyakuri, bihagaze nk’igihe c’uguhindura cane Bitcoin n’impwemu y’abantu. Yazirikanye urugendo rwiwe rwo kuva mu bumarxiste gushika mu gukunda cane Bitcoin, yarabonye ko amahera n’ububasha bitagira akamaro nk’amasano, impukwe, n’ingaruka nziza iyo bishitse ku migenderanire y’abantu n’insobanuro nyakuri y’ubuzima.


Yuzuye icizigiro n’umunezero, Mercedes ibona ko Bitcoin ishobora guhindura isi ikaba nziza, kubera ko iri mu maboko y’abantu bafise umutima ukunze kandi biyemeje. Kubera ko abagore ari bo bari imbere muri iryo hinduka, yizera ko ata n’aho bazoshika ku vyo bashobora gushikako bari kumwe.


Ubuzima bwa Mercedes bwabaye urugendo rudasanzwe, kandi ingaruka Bitcoin yagize ku buzima bwiwe ni ibitangaje vy’ukuri. Inkuru yiwe irakora nk’ikimenyetso c’icizigiro kuri Bitcoin co kuzana impinduka zifise insiguro no guha ubushobozi abantu bo mu mice yose y’ubuzima. Nk’umuvugizi w’uburinganire mu vy’amahera, akoresha ubumenyi bwiwe bwinshi n’ubumenyi afise mu bijanye n’ingendo kugira ngo yigishe yongere atere imbere abaciwe ku ruhande n’imigenzo y’ivy’amahera. Utwigoro twiwe tubandanya turatanga akarorero k’ingene urukundo n’umwiyemezo w’umuntu umwe bishobora gutuma habaho ihinduka ryiza mu mibano kw’isi yose.


## Inkuru z'ibiceri bikomeye


<chapterId>7b6d8d57-905d-5168-9be6-3df7c938de2a</chapterId>


Uko twegereza iherezo ry’iri shure, twoshima gushikiriza urutonde rw’inkuru zitera intege z’amahera y’amahera. Ivyo bimenyetso vyerekana ivyashikiye abantu ku giti cabo, abafise ubudandaji be n’amashirahamwe bakoresheje ububasha bw’amahera y’agaciro kugira ngo bashire hejuru ubuzima bwabo.


Mu ngero zikurikira, uzokwumva inkuru z’abantu ubwabo zivuga ingene amafaranga y’agaciro yatumye uwo mugwi w’abantu batandukanye ushobora guhangana n’ibintu bigoranye vyo mu vy’ubutunzi vyo muri iki gihe mu buryo bworoshe kandi bukora neza. Kuva ku bikorwa vy’ubudandaji mpuzamakungu bitagira umurongo n’amahirwe y’ubudandaji yagutse gushika ku gushiramwo amafaranga n’ububiko bw’agaciro buhamye, inkuru yose irashira ahabona ingaruka z’amahera adahinduka ku ngendo zabo.


Loc

Nyir'ikawa, muri Vietnam


“Ku cafe yanje mu karere ka Binh Thanh, turafasha abakiri bato n’abagenzi baza rimwe na rimwe, tugatanga ibinyobwa bitandukanye, harimwo ikawa, ibinyobwa vya Soft, n’ibinyobwa bimota neza. twebwe n’uburyo bwiza bwo gukuraho ikinogo c’amafaranga no kwakira abaguzi bacu bo kw’isi yose kenshi baratangazwa n’ukuntu twiyuguruye kwemera kwishura amafaranga y’amahera y’amahera, bikasiga ikimenyetso kiramvye ku bumenyi bwabo.”

Kugira ngo Address izo ngorane, namenyesheje incuti zanje ukuntu bimeze neza gukoresha USDt. Hamwe na USDt, ubu turaronka uburyo bwo kwohereza amafaranga mu mahanga, tukamenya ko abakundwa bacu bashobora gufashwa neza kandi bitazimvye."

Nta mipaka yo kohereza, amafaranga make, n'ibikorwa vyihuta n'amahera."

Ugukoreshwa kwayo ni kworoshe, kandi kenshi, urashobora gukora amafaranga ataco utanga. kuva nabona ko vyoroshe, ndaronka amahera yanje ku madolari y’Amerika, kandi nkazigama amahera y’aho hantu arambiranye agira ico akoze kuri benshi muri twebwe!”

USDt kandi yaramfashije mu vyo nazigamye kuko iyo nzoba mfise amakonte yanje y'ubucuruzi muri Bolivar ya Venezuela, sinari gushobora gutegura imbere y'igihe ivy'ugukura kw'agaciro k'ibifungurwa vyanje kubera"

Kubera ikiza c'indwara ya Coronavirus, narashikiwe n'ikibazo kidasanzwe co kwimuka, bituma ntegerezwa kurindira igihe kirekire kugira ngo nshobore kuba mu gihugu canke ngo nshobore kuronka ubwenegihugu. Naramaze imyaka hafi itatu ntashobora kuronka konti muri banki kandi ntashobora gukora mu buryo butegekanijwe n'amategeko mu gihugu. career remotely n’amashirahamwe mpuzamakungu.Kubera Tether, ndashobora guca nsubiza amahera muhira ata n’amahera menshi nkoresha canke ngo ntevye, Tether yarashoboje gukurikirana imigambi yanje y’umwuga no kuguma mfise ubwigenge mu vy’amahera naho Leta yoba yanbujije.”
