Hakoreshejwe Tether USDt, turashobora kwishura umuntu wese tutaravye ubwenegihugu bwiwe n'aho akora hose, kandi na bo nyene barashobora Exchange USDt igihe cose bashaka“.


### **Iciyumviro**


Twizigiye ko mwabonye izo nkuru zitera intege. Ivyo bivuzwe, bikwiye gusobanuka neza ko amafaranga adahinduka, nka USDt, afise uruhara runini mu gutuma abantu bashobora kuronka amafaranga yihuta kandi akora neza, gutanga amafagitire n’ugutanga amafaranga y’Amerika, umushahara uri mu madolari y’Amerika, kandi, ikiruta vyose, ububiko bw’agaciro budahinduka ugereranyije n’amafaranga menshi ahinduka. Iyo ata stablecoins, benshi muri abo bantu bohura n’intambamyi zikomeye igihe bariko barakorana n’isoko ry’isi yose, igihe bariko barahura n’abagize umuryango bo kw’isi yose, canke igihe bariko barashikira abakiriya badashobora gushikira. Stablecoins nta gukeka ko zatumye habaho uguhuza ivy’ubutunzi kandi zitanga igikoresho c’agaciro co kugendera mu bibazo bigoranye vy’ubutunzi bwacu bwo kw’isi yose.


## Ivyigwa


<chapterId>3b23b0ae-41a7-53b0-bc48-7343a64f28bc</chapterId>


None ko mwaciye mu Module "Overcomming Doubts" muzobwirizwa kugerageza ubumenyi mushasha muronka kugira ngo mumenye neza ko mwatahuye ibice vya nyuma. Tuzotangura n’Ibibazo vyinshi vyuguruye hanyuma dukore ikibazo gitoyi.


1. Ubona gute iciyumviro c’agaciro mu bijanye na Bitcoin? Woba wibaza ko ari ngombwa ko amafaranga ashigikirwa n’ikintu gifatika kugira ngo agire agaciro?

2. Uzirikanye ibikorwa vya Roya Mahboob n’ikigega Digital Citizen Fund hamwe n’ikigega Women’s Annex Foundation, wibaza ko ari inyungu izihe nyamukuru ziri mu gushiramwo ubuhinga bwa none na Bitcoin mu migambi igamije guha ubushobozi abagore bo mu bihugu biri mu nzira y’amajambere?

3. Ni gute ubwigenge bw’amahera buhambaye mu guha ubushobozi abagore, cane cane mu bihugu bahura n’ubwoko butandukanye bw’ivangura n’amahirwe make? Woba ushobora kwiyumvira ubundi buryo uretse Bitcoin bwoshobora gufasha abagore kwigenga mu vy’amahera muri ivyo bihe?

4. Kubera ubushobozi bwa Bitcoin bwo guha abahingura inguvu ubushobozi bwo gukoresha inguvu mu buryo butaziguye, woba wibaza ko ivyo bifise akamaro kanini ku bahingura inguvu no ku isoko ry’inguvu muri rusangi?

5. Duzirikanye ku bigereranywa biri hagati y’inguvu za Bitcoin n’izindi nganda, vyoba ari vyiza gutoranya Bitcoin kubera ingufu zikoreshwa? Kubera iki canke kubera iki?


## Amajambo yo gusozera


<chapterId>2b27b4dd-10e1-56a7-978e-1e5085f9aaff</chapterId>


Murakoze cane kubera mwashitse ku mpera y’amashure! Mwaje kure cane. Muri uru rugendo rwose, twaciye mu bintu vyinshi, harimwo:



- Amateka aryoshe cane yerekeye amahera.
- Ihingurwa ry'ihinduka ry'ibintu ni Bitcoin.
- Isi ya Tether n’amashikanwa yayo atandukanye y’amahera y’agaciro.
- Gutandukanya ukuri n’ibinyoma bikikuje ivyiyumviro vyinshi bitari vyo bijanye na Bitcoin na Stablecoins.
- Ingero zitandukanye z’ukuri zigaragaza ingene ubwo buhinga bukoreshwa cane mw’isi yacu iriko irahinduka kandi iguma ihinduka.


Ivyo bivuzwe, iyo haba ikintu kimwe gihambaye co gukura muri iri shure, vyoba bizunguruka gutahura itandukaniro hagati ya Bitcoin n’ibiceri bihoraho mu kwemera ivyiyumviro vy’agaciro bidasanzwe buri kimwe muri ivyo bikoresho bizana ku meza.


Tether’s stablecoins itanga umuti w’agaciro ku bantu bafise ingorane z’ubutunzi, baba mu ntwaro z’ubutegetsi bw’agahomerabunwa, canke badashobora kuronka amafaranga ahamye canke uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki. Biha umuntu wese uburyo bwo kuronka amafaranga ahagaze neza, bifasha kwishura mu buryo bwa digitale, kandi bituma ubutunzi bujabuka imipaka. Ariko rero, ni ngombwa kwemera ko amafaranga y’amahera atagira ingorane. Si amafaranga gusa yerekanye ko atakaza agaciro mu gihe kirekire, ariko amafaranga menshi agumaho yizigira abatanga amafaranga y’abandi, bikaba bisaba ko umuntu yizigira. Ivyo ntibikwiye gufatwa nk’ibisanzwe. Ni ngombwa rero cane ko umuntu akora ubushakashatsi bwimbitse imbere y’uko abika ubutunzi mu bice vy’amahera bihoraho.


Ku rundi ruhande, Bitcoin itanga umuti w’ibibazo vy’amateka bijanye n’ubwoko bwinshi bw’amahera—ashizwe hamwe kandi ashobora gusenyuka—mu gutanga ubushobozi bw’igihe kirekire bwo kwongerera ubushobozi bwo kugura biciye ku nzira y’ubuhinga bwa none Layer yubatswe hirya no hino y’ubukene bwa Supply, ivyo bikaba bishira ukuboko kw’ubutegetsi muri twebwe. Naho uguhinduka kw’igihe gito kwa Bitcoin gushobora kuba intambamyi yo kwinjira ku bantu bafise umutungo muto, ku bafise ubushobozi bwo kuraba igihe kirekire, ubushobozi bwayo bwo guhindura ubuzima biciye mu kwirundanira ubutunzi bw’igihe kirekire buratangaje kandi ntibushobora gukurwaho.


Mu rugendo rwacu rwose turi kumwe, intumbero yacu yari ibiri: kubaha ugutahura kwimbitse kw'ingene amafranga afise ubushobozi bwo guhingura kazoza, kandi, ikiruta vyose, kubaha ubumenyi bukenewe kugira ngo mufate ingingo zishingiye ku makuru no kugira uruhara mwizigiye cane mw'isi yose y'ubuhinga bwa none. Ni vyiza ko twashitse kuri izo ntumbero.


Uko dusozera iri shure, twizigiye ko uzofata ubumenyi uronse hano ukabushira mu ngiro mu bikorwa vyawe bwite canke mu vy’umwuga. Waba usanga uriko uragendera mu ngorane z’amahera, uvyurwa n’ugushaka kumenya, wipfuza gushiramwo amahera, canke urondera gukoresha ubu buhinga mu bikorwa vy’ubudandaji, twizigiye ko ubumenyi bw’agaciro uzoronka muri iri shure buzoba ubw’agaciro kanini mu rugendo rwawe.


Ese ukwo gutahura gushasha kwoguha ubushobozi bwo kugendera mw’isi y’ivy’ubutunzi iriko iratera imbere wizigiye kandi ufise intumbero. Amahirwe menshi mu nzira yawe yo gukura no kuvumbura!


Kazoza ni Keza!
